1b1: spyan 'dren rgyud gsum pa/ bla ma'i bla ma bla med dkon mchog gsum/ che ba'i tshe mchog
1b2: dbang mchog dam pa la/ gus pas phyag 'tshal dang bas skyabs su mchi// gnam sa'i mnga' bdag skye
1b3: dgu'i longs spyod gzhi/ / bstan pa dam pa chos kyi mgon mdzad pa// tshangs pa brgya byin rgyal chen yul
1b4: 'khor srung / / 'phags skyes mig mi bzang dang lus ngan po// 'jig rten skyong ba dbang po me lha dang //
1b5: gshin rje bden bral chu lho rlung gi lha// rnam thos bu dang dbang bdag sa yi lho// nyi zla gza' skar phyogs
1b6: kyi glang po rnams/ / blon po sde dpon lha mo phyogs mtshams srung // btsun mo sras bcas so so'i 'khor kun
1b7: dang / / lha yi sde dpon chen por mtshan grags pa// khyab 'jug tshogs bdag nan ti kar ti ka/ nag po chen po
1b8: stobs chen stobs po che/ / gnod 'dzin padam pad mchen po dang // dung dang dung chen gang po shin du gang //
2a1: mgrin bzang gang ba bzang po nor bu bzang // bum rna dril rna rna gsum rna bo che// yang dag shes dang yang dag rgyal ba dang // rgyal ba'i khyu mchog 'brog gnas gangs la gnas// bde ri lngas rtsen lnga len tshigs lnga ser
2a2: mgrin cu rnam 'jigs 'brug sgra nam mkha'i dbyings/ / stong gsum rgya mtsho dga' bo bsnyen dga' bo// ma dros gzi can nor rgyas gdon la 'jebs// drang srong rig 'dzin char sprin lo tog lha// lam lha nyin mtshan dus mtshams
2a3: tshe grangs yud/ / ha nu man ta la sogs mthu chen dang // tshig dbang lha mo sgra dbyangs dbyangs can dang // be'u 'dra dpal gyi lha mo 'od zer can// dkar sham brjod skyob gang gA ya mu na// sras 'phan dung can ri mkhar nag mo dang //
2a4: ma bdun srin mo bdun dang sring mo bzhi// nag mo chen mo ral pa gcig la sogs// lha mo chen mo gnod sbyin chen mo dang // sring mo chen mo sha za chen mo dang // gzhon nu'i sku 'tsho rdzu 'phrul dbang gis 'phags// smag chen brjid pa lha
2a5: dmag g.yul du bstod/ / rmang grags chen po'i dge bsnyen chen po dang // lha sras bzhon nu klu sras bzhon nu dang // rig 'dzin gzhon nu drang srong gzhon nu dang // bi k+Shus bsten pa'i gzhon nu lnga brgya spun// gnod sbyin gzhon nu tir/
2a6: ka la sogs// gzi brjid chen po'i gzhon sde thams cad dang // skye dgu'i bdag po la sogs lha dang klu// gnod sbyin dri za lto 'phye lha ma yin// gser 'dab grul bum srin po mi 'am ci// 'byung po sha za yul bdaga' dre
2a7: la sogs/ / cang shes snying rje'i lam du zhugs dgu dang // rig pa'i lcags kyus zin pa kun gson cig/ gang gi ming la'ang bkra shis dpal 'bar ba// yi ge gnyis 'brel dkon mchog gsum gyi mtshan//
2a8: skyes bu gang zhig nyan tam 'don pa yang // gzhi gsang yun gyi chu srid 'thob 'gyur na// yon tan phun sum dpag yas dkon mchog la// bsnyen bkur mnyes byed bka' la gus pa dang // chos thos nyams su len ba cu
2b1: zhig thos/ / dbas gsung rab dpag bsam rgyas pa yi// lha yi longs spyod tshal du kun gshegs te// chos rjenyi ma thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka'// bdud sde lha min g.yul las rgyal byed pa// rin chen 'od mchog/
2b2: lha dbang gtsug gi rgyan// bag yod dang pa'i spyi bos blang bar mdzod// kye rgyal ba'i sras khyod chur shog/ bdag dang sems can kun kyang yongs su mya ngan las 'das par bgyis la/ sems can ma rgal ba sa ma 'jigs par
2b3: bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs bcal bas mi ngoms pa la sems zhog shig/ mngon par 'du byed pa'i rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid kyang ma gtang shig/ sangs rgyas kyi gzugs kyi sku yang ma dor cig/ 'dod chags dang /
2b4: bral ba'ang thob par gyis shig/ chos thams cad la chags pa med pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyang btsal bar gyis shig/ chos thams cad la gzhan gyi dring 'jog pa med par sangs rgyas kyi zhing yang yongs
2b5: su spyad par gyis shig/ zhing gi mtshan nyid nam mkha' lta bur yang shes par gyis shig/ sems can yongs su smin par bya bas ma skyo shig/ bdag med pa'i mtshan nyid kyang ma spong zhig/ mngon par shes pa la
2b6: yang rnam par 'phrul par gyis shig/ chos kyi dbyings las kyang ma g.yo shig/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa yang ma gtang shig/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la yang 'byung bar gyis shig/ chos kyi 'khor lo//
2b7: bskor bas sems can thams cad tshim par gyis shig/ chos nyid brjod du med pa las kyang 'da' bar ma byed cig/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / byin gyi rlabs kyang yongs su ston cig/ byang chub//
2b8: sems dpa'i lus kyang ma dor cig/ skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du yang snang bar gyis shig/ yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po yang yongs su ston cig ces/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di dag ni lta ba'i chos zung
3a1: dang grel la b+hU pa mngon par sgrub pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa 'di dag ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las yang dag phul gyi chos bcu pa zhes bya'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas/
3a2: kyi phrin las te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams rang byung gi phrin las gzhan gyi dring 'jog pa med par bla na med pa'i byang chub 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ lha'i rgyal po dbang chen mchog sbyin gtso// dpa' bo 'jigs med 'jig
3a3: rten kun la grags/ / shes rab 'od gsal zla ba nye ba'i zhal// skyes mchog smon lam zin las gcig pa'i mched// tshangs pa brgya byin 'jig rten skyong la sogs// rdo rje ting 'dzin ri rab srub shing dang // snying rje brtson 'grus
3a4: klu yi srub thag gis/ / shes rab chen po'i rgya mtsho bsrubs pa'i bcud// dam tshes bdud rtsi'i 'gron du gshegs kun la// chos bsgrags bsod nams dbyig kyang spyir 'bul gyis// srin dmag lha min g.yul las rgyal
3a5: ba dang / lha yi rgyal srid dbu chog btsan par bsngo// gzi byin g.yog 'khor longs spyod 'phel ba dang // mthu rtsal go 'phangs khyad par thob par bsngo// rdzu 'phrul mngon shes pha rol phyin la sogs// rnam par thar pa'i sgo
3a6: kun rdzogs pa dang / / dge ba'i phrin las dgongs dgu grub par bsngo// dam chos bdud rtsi'i bde bas lus khyab ste// sdug bsngal gnod pa'i rgyud las grol bar bsngo// dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka' drin byams pa'i gnyen// bdag
3a7: cag nyon mongs mtshon gyis rmas pa rnams/ / thugs rje'i byin gyi rlabs kyis bskyang ba dang // gang gis gang la spyi bos mthu skyed cing // de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa bsrung bar gsol// ma 'os 'khrul pa'i nongs pa mchis
3a8: so 'tshal/ / dus rig rgyud mkhyen kun la bzod par gsol// lha tshogs chos kyi sbyin pa'i bkra shis kyis// phun sum tshogs 'dzin dam chos rgyas par smon// rgyud gsum pa rdzogs s+ho// / rgyud gsum pa// / tshangs pa brgya
3b1: byin tul chen lha dang bla/ / gnod byin dri ba lto byed lham yin// gseng 'dab hrul bum mi'am ci la sogs// sems can gang dag bde gshegs zas rnams dang // nor bdun phun sum dpal bzhid kun gson cag/ sam
3b2: rgyam bcom ldan yon tan bsam mi khyab/ / dam pa' chos kyi yon tan bas ma ma byug// 'phags pa'i dag 'dun yon tan bas ma mi thug// dkon mchog pasam mi khyab pa mngo/ dad ba'i// rnam mi pa
3b3: pa'ang bsam mi khyab/ / bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig bgrang bar yang // dkon mchog mtshan thos tsam yang rnyed dka' bas// brgya lam lan cig khom ldan lus rnyed rnams// rdzu 'phrul dang ba'i shugs kyis 'dir gshegs te//
3b4: rnam par grol ba'i ngan chen sna tshogs gling // zab mo rgyal ba'i bka' la kun gson cig/ bsngo ba gang dag dam chos lhur len 'dir 'dus pa// lha gru gnod sbyin la sogs mthu chen rnams// chos kyi bsod nams shes
3b5: kyang khyed bzhes te/ / gzi byin 'khor 'phel dgongs pa grub par bsngo// gsung rab bdud rtsi'i rjes su sbubs mdzod la// gang la ci rigs so sor dpal bskyed cing // de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa bsrung bar gsol//
3b6: rgyud gsum pa rdzogs s+ho// / rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya rad no la ka nAmA d+hA ra NAM ma hA ya na sU tra/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa dkon mchog ta la 'a'i gzungs shes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems
3b7: dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ / 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus cig ni/ bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab na/ khyod kyi phung po'i ril dge slong stong du tshang ba thams cad kyang dkar po'i chos yongs su rdzogs pa/ sa
3b8: ge'i sgra chen po sgrog pa/ ye shes kyi tshogs dpag tu med pa tshol ba la mkhas pa sha stag gi dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun chen po 'di lta ste/ byang chub
4a1: sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun du bzang po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na/ phyag rgya rin po che dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu brtson dang / byang
4a2: chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yon tan gyis brgyan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bsod nams mngon par bsgrags dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros chen po/
4a3: dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yon tan bkod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po dang / byang chub sems
4a4: dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i 'od dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje mtshon cha dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje sra ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/
4a5: sa 'dzin dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gzungs kyi blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po don kun mthong dang / byang chub sems sa dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras
4a6: gzigs dbang phyug dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mthu chen thob dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros brtan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje dang /
4a7: byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ngan song spong ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mya ngan dang mun pa thams cad 'joms
4a8: pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mi len mi 'dor ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po can dan snying po dang / byang
4b1: chu sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros rgya mcho dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'byung dka' dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dga' 'byung dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
4b2: spyad pa'i bla gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spobs pa brtsegs dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mthogs pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa dang /
4b3: dedag la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa la gnas pa/ dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyis nges par 'byung ba/ dbyangs sgra thogs pa med pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag
4b4: du med pa zil gyis gnon pa la mkhas pa/ mi 'jigs pa la gnas pa/ rjes su chags pa dang khong khro ba dang bral ba/ yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ khams gsum la ma chags pa/ g.yog 'khor mi phyed pa dang ldan pa/ thams
4b5: cad mkhyen pa nyid las nges par skyes pa/ ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ re ba thams cad yongs su skong ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rtogs par khong du chud pa/ lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las
4b6: kyi mtha' don yod pa la mos pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la mngon par brtson pa/ ting nge 'dzin dang spyod pa tshad med par byin gyis brlabs pa/ mi 'jigs pa thob pa/ stong pa nyid spyod yul ba/ mtshan ma med pa la gnas pa
4b7: sha stag dang yang thabs gcig go/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba 'khor de nyid du 'dus par gyur te/ 'dug pa des bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal nas
4b8: bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das chos kyi dbyings ji ltar rtogs par bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni dngos po med par rtogs par bya'o// rigs
5a1: kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa dang / spros pa med pa dang ma spros pa dang bla na med pa dang dong ba med pa dang / dngos po med pa dang / gnas pa med pa ste de ltar rtogs par bya'o// byang chub sems da/
5a2: kun tu bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ci lags/ chos kyi dbyings 'byung ba lags sam/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni 'byung ba med pa'o// rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings
5a3: ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o/ / rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni dngos po med pa rtogs pa ste/ dngos po gang du yang brjod par bya ba ma yin zhing bstan par bya ba ma yin pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos gsol pa/
5a4: bcom ldan 'das byang chub la rnam pa du mchis/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub kyi rnam pa ni tshad med de de ni tshad dang ldan par bstan par mi nus so// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos
5a5: gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ci lags/ chos kyi dbyings rnam par rtog par bgyid dam/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni rnam par mi rtog go// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos
5a6: gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gal te chos kyi dbyings rnam par mi rtog pa lags na/ byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams ci'i slad du rtog par bgyid/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byis pa so so'i skye bo
5a7: thams cad ni ma rtog pa dang / rnam par rtog pa dang / yongs su rtog pa las byung ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi byang chub ni zab lags
5a8: so/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de de bzhin te/ ji skad smras pa de de bzhin no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang chos thams cad spros pa med pa ni byang chub ces bya'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon
5b1: nur gyur ba 'khor de nyid du 'dus par gyur te 'dug pa des bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'dang kyi dgen mchog tal la zhes pa
5b2: ba'i gzungs bshad du gsol/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po chos thams cad la thogs pa med pa'i spobs pa la gnas pa 'di la dris shig dang 'di
5b3: snod la snyan par gyur pa/ denas 'jas dpal gzhon du byung bas bcom ldan 'das la mder daphyogs te duganas song mo bcuthal po snang te bcom ldan 'das la 'dis ces gsol to// thams cad mabyed
5b4: cing thams cad gzigs pa bcom ldan 'das nyid kyis ci'i slad du mi bshad/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu gang na byang chub sems dpa' yon tan 'di lta bu dang ldan pa dag 'khod pa den
5b5: de bzhin gshegs pa rnams btang snyoms su bzhugs so/ / 'jam dpal gyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni 'dir btang snyoms su bzhugs pa ma lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
5b6: stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu nga ni sems can gyi khams yal bar 'dor ba ma yin te/ rigs kyi bu 'on kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bstan pa ni bstan pa tshad med cing bstan pa bsam gyis mi khyab bo// de nas 'jam dpal
5b7: gzhon nur gyur pas yang bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis dkon mchog ta la la zhes bgyi ba'i gzungs bshad du gsol// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang
5b8: chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po 'di la dris shig dang / 'di khyod la ston par 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu skyes bu dam pa 'di ni ye shes kyi tshogs la gnas pa'o// 'jam dpal gyis gsol pa/ gal te de bzhin
6a1: gshegs pas bdag la dgongs na bdag gis skyes bu dam pa 'di la dri ba rabagyi'o/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// 'jam dpal khyod kyis ting nge 'dzin rdul tha rab kyi rdul snyed thob pa yin na de bzhin gshegs
6a2: pa la gsol pa gdab ci dgos/ rigs kyi bu khyod ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la skal pa dang ldan pa yin no// 'jam dpal gyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das bdag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos gang dag kun tu bsten pa dang bsgom
6a3: pa dang mang du bgyis pa de thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i skyes bu'i mthur rigs par bgyi'o/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu legs so legs so khyod kyis tshig 'di legs par smras te/ 'on kyang 'jam
6a4: dpal da khyed la gsol ba 'debs kyis khyod byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la dris shig/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'
6a5: kun tu bzang po 'di ni shin du zab mo ston pa ste/ theg pa chen po rtogs par khong du chud pa lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu khyod kyang chos thams cad kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po yin gyis bdag la gsung
6a6: shig/ yang rigs kyi bu khyod ni stong pa nyid la gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la sor mo bcu'i zil mo sbyar te phyag 'tshal
6a7: nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so/ / kye'i rgyal ba'i sras khyod kyis bdag la skabs phye na khyod la bdag yi ge 'bru gnyis shig 'dri'o// byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos smras pa/ rigs kyi
6a8: bu de'i dus la dbab par shes na dris shig/ de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun du bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas sangs rgyas shes bya ba'i gzhi'i/
6b1: don gang yin/ byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni gzhi med pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni dngos po med pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni bsam gyis
6b2: mi khyab pa'i don to/ / sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni spros pa med pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni ma spros pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni blang ba med pa'i/
6b3: don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni dor ba med pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don ni bsnyad du med pa'i don to// rigs kyi bu sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams kyi rang bzhin
6b4: ni de lta bu yin no/ / 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras gal te chos thams cad spros pa med pa yin na/ 'o na sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams shes ji skad bstan// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i
6b5: sras bstan pa 'di ni bstan du med pa'o/ / 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bstan du med na ci zhig bstan/ byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos smras pa/ 'jam dpal bstan du med pa ni btags te bstan to//
6b6: 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras btags pas ci zhig 'dogs par byed/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos smras pa/ 'jam dpal btags pas ni dngos po yang mi 'dogs/ dngos po med pa yang mi
6b7: 'dogs so/ / 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras gal te btags pas dngos po yang mi 'dogs/ dngos po med pa yang mi 'dogs na/ theg pa gsum po dag ji ltar bstan/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang bro/
6b8: smras pa/ 'jam dpal khyod chos kyi dbyings chags pa med pa la chags par ma byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pas chos thams cad ni dngos po med pa'o zhes bstan pa'i phyir te/ gang dngos po med
7a1: pa'i phyir zhe na/ phung po lnga dmigs pa med pa'i phyir ro// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ byang chub spros pa dang bcas pa yin nam/ 'on te spros pa med pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos smras pa/
7a2: rigs kyi bu byang chub ni spros pa dang bcas pa yang ma yin/ spros pa med pa yang ma yin te/ 'di ltar byang chub dang / spros pa dang bcas pa dang / spros pa med pa ni gnyis su med de gnyis su dbyer med do// de nas bcom ldan
7a3: 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun du bzang po la rigs kyi bu bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan pa 'di legs so legs so zhes bya ba byin no/ / gtam 'di brjod pas lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten 'di
7a4: la rmongs par 'gyur ro/ / 'jam dpal gyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das chos bstan pa 'di lta bu ni rnam par 'tshal bar mi rung ngo // bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de de bzhin te/ ji skad smras pa
7a5: bzhin no/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das la 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad btags pa lags sam/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de de
7a6: bzhin te/ ji skad smras pa bzhin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rnam par dag pa'i sgo 'di ni mos par bgyi dka' ba lags so//
7a7: bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de de bzhin te/ ji skad smras pa bzhin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' blo gros rgya mtshos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub
7a8: sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos rnam par dag pa'i sgo bstan pa 'di legs par spras lags so/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de de bzhin te/ ji skad smras pa bzhin no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang 'din
7b1: chos thams cad kyi rgyu 'thun pa yin no/ / 'di ni chos kyi char chen po yin no// de nas shing sa la chen po lta bu'i bram ze mnyam pa nyid du gnas pas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub
7b2: ni nanyam pa nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa lags te/ de la yi ge mi dmigs/ tshig 'bru mi dmigs so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de de bzhin te/ chos kyi dbyings la tshig 'bru phyi snang / don kyang mi snang
7b3: do/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das la 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das stong pa nyid kyi rgyu 'thun pa gang lags/ rnam pa gang lags/ rtags gang lags mtshan ma gang lags/ bcom
7b4: ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal stong pa nyid ni brjod du med pa/ bsnyad du med pa ste/ brjod du med pa'i chos nyid 'di la mos pa gang yin pa de stong pa nyid ces bya'o// stong pa nyid de ni yi ge med pa ste/ de'i phyir
7b5: stong pa nyid ces bya'o/ / stong pa nyid de ni bsnyad du med pa ste/ de'i phyir stong pa nyid ces bya'o// rigs kyi bu chos thams cad ni ngo bo nyid kyis stong ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'di skad ces gsol
7b6: to/ / bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i chos la gnas pa rnams kyi rnam par 'phrul ba la gzigs/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu sems dang po bskyed bI/
7b7: byang chub sems dpa'i shes pa ni mchog yin gyi dgra bcom pa'i shes pa ni de ltar ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ dgra bcom pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams las ring du gnas la/ byang chub sems dpa' de ni sangs rgyas bcom
7b8: ldan 'das su 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos thams cad kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar bcom ldan 'das
8a1: kyis gsungs pa'i don bdag gis 'tshal ba ltar na nyan thos kyis ni nyan thos kyi chos rnams ma thob pa nyid lags so/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal ba/ rigs kyi bu nyan thos kyis nyan thos kyi chos rnams
8a2: mthob pa ni ma yin te/ 'on kyang nyan thos la byang chub sems dpa' dang lhan cig tu dris pa la lan gdab pa 'am/ spyod pa byin gyis brlabs par bya ba'i nus pa dang mthug la yod/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la 'jam dpal gzhon
8a3: nur gyur pas 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pas shes rab dang ldan pa rnams kyi mchog tu bstan pa lags na bstan pa 'di gang la bstan pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis//
8a4: bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal ngas gang bstan pa 'di ni bstan pa med pa'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas gnas brtan shA ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces smras so// gnas brtan gyis nyan thos kyi chos rnams thob bam/
8a5: smras pa/ de ni ma yin no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ 'o na ci khyod so so'i skye bo 'am/ smras pa/ de ni ma yin no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ 'o na ci khyod slob pa 'am/ smras pa de ni ma yin no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/
8a6: 'on khyod ci shes rab dang ldan pa'i mchog yin nam/ smras pa/ de ni ma yin no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ gal te btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu so so'i skye bo yang ma yin/ slob pa yang ma yin/ shes rab dang ldan pa'i mchog kyang
8a7: ma yin ni de nyid khyod dmigs pa can du 'gyur ro/ / shA ra dwa ti'i bus smras pa/ rigs kyi bu kho bo ni skyes bu dam pa rgya mtsho ltar gting dpag dka' ba khyod dang 'gyed par ma byed do// jam dpal gyis smras pa/ btsun pa shA rA tI'i ts+tsha/
8a8: khyod na rgan rabs thu bo mchog yin gyis btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu de skad mazer cig/ gnas brtan gyis smras pa/ rigs kyi bu rgas pa'i dngos pos ni ci yang 'do bar mi 'gyur/ mngon par rtogs par mi 'gyur ro// rigs kyi
8b1: bu don de nyid shes par bya ba'i phyir khyod la dpe bya'o/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na rdo rje ngan don gyis kyang ri brag chen po rnam par 'jig go/ rigs kyi bu de bzhin du khyod kyi spu'i khung bu gcig na shes rab 'dug pa gang yin/
8b2: pa de ni kho bo lta bu'i sems can rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed rnams la med do// rigs kyi bu don de nyid shes par bya ba'i phyir yang khyod la dpe bya'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na ba lang glang po che shin du mi bzad pa chen po
8b3: de yang mi stobs dang ldan pas lcags kyu chung ngus dul bar byed do/ / rigs kyi bu de bzhin du khyod ni stobs dang ldan pa/ kho bo ni nyam chung ba ste/ glang po che chen po 'di lta bu dang kho bo 'gye ga la nus/ de nas bcom ldan 'das
8b4: la gnas brtan shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na mi dmus long gis shul du mchi ba 'am/ grong khyer mthong bar yang rngo mi thogs na khyim nas khyim du mchi ba'i rdo lta ga la thog
8b5: ste/ de ni gnas ma mchis so// de bzhin du glang po che chen po lta bu 'di dag gi 'dun na bdag ni dmus long dang mtshungs par mthong ste/ sangs rgyas kyi chos 'di dag ni de tsam du rgya che ba lags so// bdag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos
8b6: rnams kyi snod du ma gyur te/ da ci bgyir yang ma mchis so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu de skad ma zer cig/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di lta ste dper na de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis sems can ji
8b7: snyed cig la reg pa de dag thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams thob pa yin no/ / shA ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin du khyod ni ting nge 'dzin mtha' yas shing bsam gyis mi khyab pa thob pa yin no// bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi rnam
8b8: grangs 'di bshad pa na/ lha dang mi'i skye dgu las sems can dgu khri nyis stong gis chos mngon par rtogs par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin dkon mchog tu
9a1: la la sbyor ba mtha' yas pa zhes bya ba de la snyoms par zhugs so/ / byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu phyogs bcu'i phyogs re re'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong
9a2: phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyi pha rol nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyis/ zhal mngon par bstan te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag thams cad kyang
9a3: mtshan rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya bar 'thun pa sha stag go/ phyogs gcig ji lta bar phyogs bcu rnams nas kyang de bzhin te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// chos kyi blo gros khyod
9a4: ltar byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sbyor ba mtha' yas pa la snyoms par zhugs pa legs so legs so/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad 'di nyid kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang /
9a5: sngon gyi byin gyi rlabs dang / khyod nyid kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba nye bar bstan pas 'di lta ste chos thams cad bstan par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rnam par sbyang ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / chos kyi
9a6: dbyings su 'jug par bya ba dang / sems can gyi khams rnam par dgrol ba dang / chags pa med pa'i ye shes la 'jug cing chud par bya ba dang / kun du sbyor bar bya ba dang / skad thams cad brjod par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen
9a7: pa'i ye shes la 'jug par bya ba dang / chos thams cad la sgrib pa med par bya ba dang / dus gsum thams cad yongs su shes pa'i chos bstan pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir phyogs bcu nas de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas
9a8: kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed thams cad kyang mtshan mthun pa 'di dag thams cad khyod la byin gyis rlob kyis rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa bcu las brtsams te/ sangs rgyas
9b1: kye mthu dang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis chos bstan pa 'di la spobs pa skyed cig/ de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la thogs pa med pa'i ye shes kyi snga
9b2: ba dang / sgrib pa med pa dang / chod pa med pa dang / brjed pa med pa'i chos nyid dang / tha dad pa med pa'i ye shes dang // nga na ma tho ba med pa dang / zil gyis mi non pa dang / zhum pa med pa dang / 'phrogs pa med pa'i chos nyid
9b3: dang / brjod pa bzang po nye bar sgrub pa mdzad do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar ting nge 'dzin 'di nyid kyi chos nyid thob pa'i phyir ro// de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis phyag g.yas pa brkyang ste/ byang chub
9b4: sems dpa' chos kyi blo gos kyi mgo la nyug pa mdzad de/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la reg ma thag tu/ de nas ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas byang chub sems
9b5: dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rigs 'di ni 'di lta ste/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa dang / nam mkha'i khams kyi mthas gtugs pa bas rgya che ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras/
9b6: ngag 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigs su skye ba yin/ ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigs su skye ba yin/ da ltar/
9b7: byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigs su skye ba yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras gang dag 'das pa dang ma/
9b8: byin pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigs su skye ba'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag ni gang yin/ gang las bsams te de skad smra/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems
10a1: dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa bcu po de dag gang yin pa de shod cig/ de skad ces smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces smras so//
10a2: kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa ni bcu po 'di dag ste/ de dag ni 'das pa dang mabyon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs sogasu
10a3: ngo gsung bar 'gyur ro/ / bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa dang / las dang po pa dang / rnal 'byor spyod pa dang / skye bar skyes pa dang / sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa dang / bsam pa phun
10a4: sum tshogs pa dang / phyir mi ldog pa dang / gzhon nur gyur pa dang rgyal tsha ba dang / dbang bskur ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam
10a5: par gzhag pa ni bcu po de dag ste/ de dag ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsung so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub
10a6: sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mthong ma thag tu gzugs bzang ba'am/ mdzes pa 'am/ kha dog bzang
10a7: po rgyas pa 'am/ rgya che ba 'am/ gzi brjid che ba 'am/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa 'am/ kun rjod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa 'am/ rjes su bstan pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa mthong ngam/ sems can sdug bsngal ba dag mthong ngam/ de bzhin
10a8: gshegs pa'i bsngags pa rgya cher thos na 'di lta ste/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'dod cing thog ma nyid du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do// sems bskyed ma thag pa de nyid kyis bsnyen par
10b1: dga' ba'i gnas bcu yongs su bzung bar 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ gnas dang gnas ma yin pa shes pa dang 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba'i chos yang dag par blangs pa shes pa dang / thams cad du gro
10b2: ba'i lam shes pa dang / khams du ma sna tshogs shes pa dang / mos pa dang rnam par grol ba du ma shes pa dang / dbang po mchog dang mchog ma yin pa shes pa dang / bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par
10b3: 'jug pa'i kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba dang / ldang ba thams cad shes pa dang / sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa'i shes pa dang / lha'i mig gi shes pa dang / zag pa zad pa shes pa ste/ bsnyen par dka' ba'i gnas bcu po de dag yod
10b4: su bzung bar 'gyur ro/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de sangs rgyas
10b5: mchod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' bde ba'i yo byad la sbyar bar bya'o// de la 'jig rten gyi bdag por 'gyur ba dang / mchog tu bya ba dang zil gyis mi gnon pa dang / sangs rgyas dpag tu med pa dang phrad ba dang / rab tu zhi ba'i ting nge 'dzin la rnal 'byor
10b6: dra bya ba dang / 'khor ba'i 'khor lo rnam par bzlog pa dang / dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba dang / sems can sdug bsngal ba yongs su bsgrub pa yang brjod par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar sems skyes ma thag le nyid kyi shas cher sangs
10b7: rgyas kyi chos thams cad la sbyor zhing gong du gnas gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid sbyor gyi/ gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jog pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
10b8: rnam par gzhag pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag nga la las dang po 'di pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la las dang po pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni sems can rnams la thog ma
11a1: nyid du sems rnam pa bcu ba skyed de/ rnam pa bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ phan par bya ba'i sems dang bde bar bya ba'i sems dang / snyid brtse ba'i sems dang / mnyen pa'i sems dang / sdug pa'i sems dang / phan gdags
11a2: pa sems dang / kun du bsrung ba'i sems dang / rnams pa'i sems dang / slob pan gyi sams dang / snyan pa'i sems te/ sems rnam pa ban po 'ad dag skyed nga// rgyal ba'i sras dag 'dan las da pa'i bya chub sems pa/
11a3: kye rgyal ba'i sras dag las dang po pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de lung mnod pa dang / kha ton la sbyar bar bya'o// mang du thos nas rab tu dben pa la sbyar bar bya'o// rab tu dben par gyur nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen la mngon par dga' bal
11a4: sbyar bar bya'o/ / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la mngon par dga' nas dka' blo bde ba la sbyar bar bya'o// dka' blo bde bar gyur nas dus shes pa la sbyar bar bya'o// dus shes par gyur nas mi 'jigs pa la sbyar ba phyag mi 'jigs par gyur nas
11a5: don shes pa la sbyar bar bya'o/ / don shes par gyur nas chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba la sbyar bar bya'o// chos kyi rjes su 'brang bar gyur nas brjed pa med pa'i chos nyid la sbyar bar bya'o// rmongs pa med par gyur nas chos rnam par dgod
11a6: ba la sbyar bar bya'o/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar sems bskyed ma thag pa de nyid kyis shes cher sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mngon par brtson par byed cing gong du gnas gang dag thob pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid sbyor gyi
11a7: gzhan gyi dring la ma 'jog pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni las dang po pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la rnal 'byar spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa
11a8: gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la rnal 'byor spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni dmigs pa rnam pa bcus chos rnams rtogs par byed de/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad la mi rtag pa nyid du rtogs par byed pa dang /
11b1: chos thams cad la sdug bsngal ba nyid dang / bdag med pa nyid dang / stong pa nyid dang / g.yo ba med pa nyid dang / dbugs 'byin pa med pa nyid dang / gnas med pa nyid dang / rnam par rtog pa med pa nyid dang / rtsol ba med pa nyid dang / mngon
11b2: par 'du byed pa med pa nyid du rtogs par byed de/ chos kyi rjes su 'brang bar gyur pa'i phyir sbyor bar mi byed mi sbyor bar yang mi byed dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni rnal 'byor spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
11b3: rnal 'byor spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de ni sems can gyi khams partag pa la sbyar bar bya'o/ / chos kyi dbyings partag pa la sbyar bar bya'o// 'jig rten gyi khams brtag pa la sbyar bar bya'o// sa'i khams btag pa la sbyar bar bya'o//
11b4: chu'i khams dang me'i khams dang rlung gi khams dang nam mkha'i khams dang gzugs kyi khams dang gzugs med pa'i khams brtag pa la sbyar bar bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar 'di ni shas cher chos rnams la snang ba 'jug cing
11b5: gong du gnas gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid sbyor gyi gzhan gyi dri la mi 'jog pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni rnal 'byor spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par bzhag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
11b6: dag skye bar skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la skye bar skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni yongs su sbyong bar byed pa bcus gsung rab 'phags par skyes pa yin te/ bcu
11b7: gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos nyid las phyir mi ldog pa dang / sangs rgyas la mi phyed pa'i dad pa mthar thug par 'gyur ba yongs su grub pa dang / chos nges par sems pa dang / sems can la rnam par dpyod pa dang / zhing la rnam
11b8: par spyod pa dang / 'jig rten la rnam par dpyod pa dang / las la rnam par dpyod pa dang / rnam par smin pa la rnam par dpyod pa dang / 'khor ba la rnam par dpyod pa dang / mya ngan las 'das pa la rnam par dpyod pa ste/ yongs su sbyong
12a1: pa byed pa bcu po de dag gis gsung rab 'phags par skyes pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni skye bar skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag skye bar skyes pa'i byang chub sems
12a2: dpa' de ni 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o/ / ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o// da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa
12a3: nyid la rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o/ / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o// 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag par 'grub pa rnam par spyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o//
12a4: ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag par 'grub pa rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o// da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag par 'grub pa rnam par spyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
12a5: chos yang dag par 'grub pa rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o/ / 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su 'grub pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o// ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su
12a6: 'grub pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o/ / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su 'grub pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos yongs su
12a7: 'grub pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de ni shas cher dus gsum mnyam pa nyid rtogs par byed cing / gong du gnas gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid//
12a8: sbyor gyi gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jog pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni skye bar skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa'i byang
12b1: byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni dge ba'i las gang ci rtsom yang de dag thams cad sems can thams cad
12b2: yongs su bskyab pa dang / sems can thams cad la phan par 'dod par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad la bde bar sbyar ba dang / sems can thams cad la snying brtse bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad rab tu thar bar bya/
12b3: ba dang / sems can thams cad la gnod pa med par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad drang bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad dad par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad gdul ba dang / sems can thams cad yongs su mya
12b4: ngan las bzla ba'i phyir brtsom ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de la gnas bcu yang
12b5: dag par brjod par bya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can mtha' yas pa dang / sems can dpag tu med pa dang / sems can grangs med pa dang / sems can bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / sems can mtshungs pa med
12b6: pa dang / sems can gzhal du med pa dang / sems can stong pa nyid dang / sems can g.yo ba med pa nyid dang / sems can med pa nyid dang / sems can rang bzhin med pa nyid do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de shas cher mngon par
12b7: zhen pa med pa la sems 'jog cing gong du gnas pa gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid sbyor gyi gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jog pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa'i byang
12b8: chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa'i
13a1: byang chub sems dpa' ni chos bcu thos na sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams la bsam pa nges pa yin te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi bsngags pa'am/ bsngags pa ma yin pa 'chad kyang rung sangs rgyas kyi chos
13a2: rnams la bsam pa nges pa yin/ chos kyi bsngags pa 'am/ bsngags pa ma yin pa 'chad kyang rung / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsngags pa 'am/ bsngags pa ma yin pa 'chad kyang rung ste/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams
13a3: la bsam pa nges pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i bsngags pa 'am/ bsngags pa ma yin pa 'chad kyang rung ste/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams la bsam pa nges pa yin/ sems can gyi khams rgya chung zhes 'chad pa 'am
13a4: sems can gyi khams rgya che zhe 'am/ sems can gyi khams kun nas nyon mongs pa can zhe'am/ sems can gyi khams kun nas nyon mongs pa can ma yin zhe 'am/ sems can gyi khams gdul sla zhe 'am/ sems can gyi
13a5: khams gdul dka' zhe 'am/ chos kyi dbyings rgya chung zhe 'am/ chos kyi dbyings rgya che zhe'am/ 'jig rten gyi khams dag 'jig ce 'am/ mi 'jig ce'am/ chos kyi dbyings yod ce'am/ chos kyi dbyings med ces 'chad kyang rung ste/ sangs
13a6: rgyas kyi chos rnams la bsam pa nges pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de la
13a7: chos kyi rjes su 'jug pa bcu yang dag par brjod par bya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad mtshan ma med pa nyid du yang dag par brjod par bya ba dang / chos thams cad mtshan nyid med pa nyid dang / dngos po med pa nyid
13a8: dang / med pa nyid dang / brdzun pa nyid dang / dben pa nyid dang / ngo ba nyid med pa nyid dang / sgyu ma lta bu nyid dang / mi lam lta bu nyid dang / rnam par rtog pa med pa nyid du yang dag par brjod par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de mi 'phrog
13b1: pa'i phyir shas cher lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam par 'phel ba'i chos can du gyur cing / gong du gnas gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid sbyor gyi gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jog pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
13b2: 'di ni bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la phyir mi
13b3: ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni dmigs pa bcu thos na/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams las phyir mi ldog ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas yod do zhe 'am med do zhes thos kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams
13b4: las phyir mi ldog pa dang / chos yod do zhe'am med do zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' yod do zhes 'am med de zhes bya ba dang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yod do zhe 'am med do zhes bya ba dang byang chub sems dpa'
13b5: byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa la nges par 'byung ngo zhe 'am/ nges par mi 'byung ngo zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dag 'das so zhi 'am ma 'das so zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dag byon te zhe 'am byin pa ma yin/
13b6: ne zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa bdag da ltar byung ba'o zhe 'am/ da ltar byung ba ma yin no zhes bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes zad do zhe 'am/ mi zad do zhes bya ba dang / dus gsum po dag mtshan nyid gcig ce'am/
13b7: mtshan nyid gcig pa ma yin no zhes thos kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams las phyir mi ldog pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub
13b8: sems dpa' de la chos kyi rgyun bcu yang dag par brjod par bya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad gcig pa nyid dang / tha dad pa nyid du yang dag par brjod par bya'o// mang ba dang gcig pa nyid dang / yi ge la
14a1: don sgro btags pa dang / do sa yig gnas pa dang / pas ngo med klogags pa dang / dngos po med pas dngos po sgo btags pa dang / mtshan mas mtshan ma med pa sgro btags pa dang / mtshan ma med pas mtshan ma
14a2: sgro btags pa dang / mtshan nyid kyis mtshan nyid med pa sgro btags pa dang / mtshan nyid med pas mtshan nyid sgro btags pa yang dag par brjod par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de shas cher chos thams cad
14a3: la mkhas pa yongs su smin pa'i tshul la nges par 'byung zhing gong du gnas gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid sbyor gyi gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jig pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni phyir mi
14a4: ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la gzhon nur gyur pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la gzhon nur gyur pa'i byang chub
14a5: sems dpa' ni chos rtogs pa bcu dang ldan pa yin te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ lus kyi las 'bras bu yod pa dang ldan pa yin/ ngag gi las 'bras bu yod pa dang ldan pa yin/ yid kyi las 'bras bu yod pa dang ldan pa
14a6: yin/ sems bskyed pa tsam gyis skye ba mngon par sgrub pa yin/ sems can gzhan dag dang / gang zag gzhan rnams kyi bsam pa shes par byed cing mos pa la rtog pa yin/ sems can gyi khams tha dad pa rab tu shes pa
14a7: yin/ 'dod pa'i khams tha dad pa rab tu shes pa yin/ gzugs kyi khams cadad pa rab tu shes pa yin/ gzugs med pa'i khams tha dad pa rab tu shes pa yin/ dus dza lta ba bzhin du 'gro ba'i phyir mngon par shes pa myung
14a8: pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni gzhon nur gyur pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag gzhon nur gyur pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de la chos mngon par bsgrub pa bcu yang dag par brjod par bya ste/
14b1: bcug shen/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su shes pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi snying gtug so par byu ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi thaM byin gyis ba dang / sangs rgyas kyin rnam par snad pa dag sangs rnas kyi nga
14b2: 'grob dang / 'dzag rten gyi khams grangs med par 'gro ba dang / dri ba grangs med pa dri ba dang / yid kyi lus mngon par bsgrub pa dang / sgra skad la sbyor ba tshad med pa dang / sems bskyed pas sangs rgyas kyi nang grangs med pa yongs su 'gyul
14b3: pa yang dag par brjod par bya'o/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de shas cher mngon par bsgrub pa mkhas pa la sbyor zhing / gong du gnas pa gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid sbyor gyi gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal
14b4: ba'i sras dag 'di ni gzhon nur gyur pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dge la rgyal tshab kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la gzhon nu rgyal tshab kyi byung
14b5: rgyachub sems dpa' ni chos rtogs pa dbub bcu la mkhas pa yinate/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can gyi sgra brtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin/ nyon mongs pa rgyu ba rtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin/ pag chags kyi mtshams
14b6: sbyor ba rtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin/ spyod yul la sbyor ba rtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin chos nyid rtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin/ nye bar spyad pa rtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dbye ba
14b7: rtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin/ sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba shes pa rtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin/ kun rdzob kyi bden pa nges par rtog pa rtogs par bya ba la mkhas pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
14b8: dag 'di ni rgyal tshab kyi byang chub sems dpa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag rgyal tshab kyi byang chub sems dpa' de la gnas bcwa yang dag par brjod par bya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor la mkhas pa yang
15a1: dag par brjod par bya'o/ / rgyal po 'pho brang 'khor kun du spyad pa dang / rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor du 'jug pa dang / rgyal po'i tho brang 'khor du rnam par spyad pa dang / chos kyi rgyal po'i dbangar bskur ba dang / chos kyi rgyal po'i byin gyi
15a2: rlabs dang / chos kyi rgyal po'i pha rol gnon pa dang / chos kyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / chos kyi rgyal po'i bka' lung yang dag par brjod par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de'i sems shas cher chos thams cad la sgrib pa med par bsgrub
15a3: pa la 'jug ci dgong du gnas gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid sgrub kyi gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jog pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni rgyal tshab kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal
15a4: ba'i sras dag de la dbang bskur ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la dbang bskur ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni shes pa mngon par sgrub pa bcu dang ldan pa ste/ bcu gang
15a5: zhe na 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa rab tu g.yo bar byed pa mang ba yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa byin gyi ma rlob pa mang ba yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa sems gcig gis 'da' bar byed
15a6: pa mang ba yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa yongs su spyad pa byed pa meng ba yin/ sems can grangs med pa'i sems gcig gis rnam par rig par byed pa mang ba yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa la rnam par lta
15a7: ba mang ba yin/ sems can grangs med pa'i sems kyi spyod pa la sems gcig gis rnam par dpyod pa la mkhas pa yin/ sems can grangs med pa'i dbang po sems gcig gis rtogs par byed pa la mkhas pa yin/ sems
15a8: can grangs med pa 'dul ba la mkhas pa yin/ sems can grangs med pa'i rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems la 'dzud pa la mkhas pa yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag rgyal tshab kyi sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems
15b1: dpa' man chad gang gis kyang dbang bskur ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de'i lus kyi las shes par mi nus/ dag gi las shes par mi nus/ yid kyi las shes par mi nus/ rdzu 'phrul shes par mi nus/ rdzu 'phrul la/
15b2: rnam par lta ba shes par mi nus/ 'das pa'i dus la rnam par lta ba shes par mi nus zhing mngon par 'du byed pa shes par mi nus/ blos rnam par lta ba shes par mi nus/ sems kyi yul shes par mi nus/ ye shes kyi
15b3: spyod yul shes par mi nus te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni dbang bskur ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag dbang bskur ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de dag la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dag
15b4: gnas bcu yang dag par brjod par mdzad de/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dus gsum shes pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos shes pa dang / chos kyi dbyings dbyer med pa shes pa dang / chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa dang /
15b5: 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par dgar ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar byed pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad byin gyis brlab pa dang / sems can thams cad yongs su shes pa dang / chos thams
15b6: cad mngon par shes pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mtha' yas pa brjod pa mdzad do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de ni shas cher thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la sems 'jug pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni dbang
15b7: bskur ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros gyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa bcu bshad ma
15b8: thag tu de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs re rer yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rnam pa drug tu g.yos/ rab tu g.yos kun tu rab tu g.yos so// 'gul
16a1: rab tu 'gul/ kun tu rab tu 'gul to/ ldeg rab tu ldeg/ kun tu rab tu ldeg go/ lu 'ur rab tu 'ur bur/ kun tu rab tu 'ur 'ur ro// chem chem/ rab tu chem chem/ kun tu rab tu chem chem mo// 'khrugs rab tu 'khrugs/
16a2: kun tu rab tu 'khrugs so// sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / chos nyid thob pas lha'i me tog gi sprin gyi char yang mngon par bab po// lha'i bdug pa'i sprin gyi char yang mngon par bab bo/ lha'i spos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po//
16a3: lha'i phye ma'i sprin gyi char dang / lha'i phyed pa'i sprin gyi char dang / lha'i gos kyi sprin gyi char dang / lha'i rin po che'i sprin gyi char dang / lha'i pad ma'i sprin gyi char dang / lha'i rgyan phreng gi sprin gyi char dang / lha'i rgyan gyi sprin gyi char yang
16a4: mngon par bab bo/ / lha'i sil snyan rnams kyang ma dkrol bar sgra byung ngo // lha'i snang ba yang rab tu byung ngo // lha'i nga ro yang grag go// gling bzhi pa 'dir ri rab kyi rtse mor lha'i dbang po'i khang par ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi
16a5: khams thams cad du yang chos bstan pa 'di khyab par gyur nas byung ste lhag chad med do/ / tshig 'bru 'di dag nyid kyis don 'di nyid ston to// sangs rgyas kyi mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyi 'jig/
16a6: rten gyi khams rnams kyi pha rol nas byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab snyed lhags te/ phyogs bcu rgyas par bkang nas 'di skad ces 'dzer to// kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar khyod byang chub
16a7: sems dpa'i chos nyid 'di ston pa legs so legs so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bdag cag kyang ming chos kyi blo gros shes bya ba sha stag ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi sprin ces bya ba dag nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i
16a8: mtshan chos kyi blo gros bzang po zhes bya ba sha stag gi thad nas 'dir phyin to/ / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis de dag thams cad du chos bstan pa 'di byung ste/ 'khor 'di lta bu dag gi nang du tshig 'bru 'di dag gis don 'di
16b1: nyid ston te/ lhag chad med do// kye rgyal ba'i sras bdag cag ni khyod kyi dbang du gyur te/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir byin to// bdag cag ji ltar 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir byin pa de bzhin du
16b2: phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gleng bzhi pa thams cad du ri rab kyi rtse mor lha'i dbang po'i khang pa rnams su yang byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed byin par gyur te/ de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/
16b3: thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor dang / chos kyi dbyings la yang rnam par bltas nas de'i tshe tshogs su bcad pa
16b4: 'di dag smras so/ / rang byung shin tu rnam dag blo mnga' ba// mdzes shing gzugs kyi stobs dang ldan gyur pa/ bsnyen dka' mtshan gyis brgyan pa mthong gyur nas// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'dzeg byed// de zla med
16b5: pa'i rdzu 'phrul stobs rnams dang / / kun rjod bzang dang rjes su bstan pa dang // sdug bsngal bzang rlag 'jig rten 'gro mthong nas// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// yon tan kun gyi 'byung gnas de
16b6: bzhin gshegs/ / kun du bzang po'i yon tan thos gyur nas// nam mkha'i dbyings 'dra 'gyur ba med pa yi// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// gnas rnams ji snyed gang dag yod gyur dang / rang bzhin gnas pa'i//
16b7: gnas rnams gzhan dag kyang // gzhan min dngos por rnam par rtog bya phyir// byang chub don du bstan pa sems 'jog byed// 'das dang ma 'ongs da ltar dus dag na// dge dang mi dge'i' las rnams gang yod pa// de dag
16b8: rgyu rnams rtogs par bya ba'i phyir/ / byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// ting 'dzin bsam gtan rnam thar spyod pa dang // de bzhin snyoms 'jug rnam dag mthar thug pa// de dag gnas skabs rtogs par
17a1: bya ba'i phyir/ / byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ 'jig rten brtson 'grus stobs dang dbang po rnams// ci 'dra ci 'dra de yid dang bder// rim pa de dag rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan
17a2: pa sems 'jog byed/ / 'jig rten kun gyi mos paci 'dra dang // lhag pa'i bsam pa tha dad rnam gsum nas// bstan bcos du ma rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du bstan pa sems 'jog byed// rnam pa sna tshogs
17a3: rnam pa du ma'i khams/ / gang dag 'jig rten gsum 'dir yod kun gyi// khams kyi rang bzhin rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems de 'jog/ chos 'dir kun du 'gro bar gang gyur cig/ dge ba'i
17a4: 'jug pa gang yang rab 'jug pa/ / yang dag rang bzhin rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// zhing rnams thams cad ji ltar 'byung ba dang // sems can ji ltar sa las 'byung 'gyur/
17a5: zhes/ chags med mig ni rab tu dbye ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ 'das pa'i dus dang da ltar byung ngus na// sems can ris dngos mtshan nyid gang yod dang // sngon gyi gnas rnams rtogs
17a6: par bya ba'i phyir/ / byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ ji ltar 'gro bar sems can 'ching byed pa// kun du sbyor ba 'jig rten gang yod pi// nyon mongs zad pa rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems/
17a7: 'di 'jog/ 'jig rten gsum na tha skad gang btags dang // ngag lam sngags tshul spyod pa gang yod pa// brda yi bden pa rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ chos rnams thams cad brjod du
17a8: med pa ste/ / stong pa ma g.yo rang bzhin ngo bo nyid// don dam bden pa rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// zhing rnams dag tus g.yo bstan pa dang // rgya mtsho dag kyang rnam par 'khrugs pa dang //
17b1: de bzhin gshegs kyi rdzu 'phrul bstan pa'i phyir// byang chub don du bstan pa sems 'di 'jog/ 'od zer rtse mo re las 'od zer rnams// de bzhin phyogs bcu kun du rab tu 'gyed// de dag 'od gcig rtogs par bya ba'i phyir/
17b2: byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// zhing mang ba sam gyis mi khyab gang yod pa// de dag rang gi lag tu mngon sprul te/ sgyu ma'i tshul ni rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// zhing rnams
17b3: ji ltar de bzhin sems can kun/ / gnod pa med par lag pa'i mthil bzhag nas// chos rnams srog med rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ rgya mtsho rnams ni ji snyed chu yod pa//
17b4: skra rtse'i thigs pa'i nang du 'jug par byed// ma lus mthar thug rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ zhing rnams kun na phra rab rdul gyi bag/ gang yod de dag ma lus bgrang byed cing //
17b5: phra rab rdul grangs rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// 'jig rten 'di na 'das dang de bzhin du// ma 'ongs sreg pa'i bskal pas 'jigs pa rnams// bskal pa zad pa rtogs par bya
17b6: ba'i phyir/ / byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ dus gsum dag gi de bzhin gshegs rnams dang // ston pa rang rgyal thos las byung rnams kyi// chos kyi rang bzhin rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan
17b7: pa sems 'di 'jog/ brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten khams 'di rnams// skra yis bcings nas ma lus srang la 'debs// dngos po'i rang bzhin rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/
17b8: 'khor yug ri bo bsam gyis mi khyab pa// skra yis bcings nas ma lus srang la 'debs// rags dang phra ba rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ lus pa med pa'i 'jig rten khams
18a1: rnams su/ / skad cig gcig la dbyangs kyi go bar byed// dbyangs kyi yan lag dag pa bstan pa'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ 'jig rten kun gyi sgra rnams ci 'dra ba// skad cig gcig
18a2: la skad cig rjod byed cing / / zhi ba'i rang bzhin rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ 'jig rten gsum po ma lus rtogs par byed// sems can kun gyis rab tu rnam par shes// /
18a3: lce yangs pargya chen rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// zhing rnams kun tu brjod dang 'dra bar yang // skad cig gcig la lta gyur sel bar byed// rnam rtog chos rnams rtogs
18a4: par bya ba'i phyir/ / byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// 'dir ni zhing rnams thams cad ma lus par// de bzhin gshegs pas gang zhing rang byung gi/ chos rnams skad cig gcig la rtogs bya 'i phyir// /
18a5: byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ rdul phran tha dad lta bur 'jig rten khams// rnam pa kun du mngon par sprul byed cing // yid las byung ba de dag rtogs bya'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed//
18a6: 'das dang de bzhin ma byon sangs rgyas rnams// ji snyed gang dag 'jig rten bzhugs so cog/ sems kyi skad cig gcig la rtogs bya'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// tshig gcig brjod kyang
18a7: bsam gyis mi khyab par/ / bskal pa zad kyi de la nyams pa med/ tshig rab dbye ba rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ phyogs bcu rnams kyi 'jig rten thams cad kyi// 'gro ba ci
18a8: 'dra ldog pa ci 'dra ba/ / sems kyi skad cig gcig la rtogs bya'i phyir// byang chub don du brtan pa sems 'jog byed// phyogs rnams kun du 'gro yang lus kyis sam// ngag gam yid kyis gang du'ang chags pa med// dus
18b1: gsus stong pa nyid du rtogs bya'i phyir/ / khyad nu ba don du brtan pa sems 'di 'jog/ byang chub sems ni ji ltar bskyed pa bzhin// gzhal yas bskal par phyogs su rgyu byed cing // sangs rgyas spyan sbyar mchod par bya'o zhes/
18b2: 'di ni mi ldog rnams kyi bstan pa yin// phyogs bcu dag gi 'jig rten tha dad par// 'jig rten bdag por rgyal ba'i sras 'gyur ba// gang yang rung ba'i dam pa sgrogs par byed// 'di ni mi ldog rnams kyi bstan pa
18b3: yin/ / byang chub don du srid par spyad spyod tshe// byang chub sems dpa'i bde sbyor gang yin pa// de yi bstsags pa rtag tu brjod par byed// 'di ni mi ldog rnams kyi brtan pa yin// chos mchog tshes rab phul du phyin pa dang //
18b4: byed par 'phags chos bla med gang yod pa// de dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams la ston// 'di ni mi ldog rnams kyi bstan po yin// yon tan kun ldan de bzhin gshegs pa yi// tshe nyid 'di na yod kyi gzhan med
18b5: pa/ / de la byang chub sems dpa' sbyor bar byed// 'di ni mi ldog rnams kyi bstan pa yin// tshad med gzhal yas bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i// sangs rgyas rnam dang phrad gyur ci 'dra ba// byang chub sems dpa' de
18b6: la ston par byed/ / 'di ni mi ldog rnams kyi bstan pa yin// ting 'dzin gang dag ji snyed yod pa dang // de bzhin ting 'dzin rgyud kyi rnam pa dag/ de dag bde gshegs sas la rjod par byed// 'di ni mi ldog rnam
18b7: kyi bstan pa yin/ / 'khor ba'i 'khor lo rnam par zlog pa dang // dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor ba// 'jig rten kun gyis rtag du ma bskor ba// byang chub sems dpang rnams la de gan/ bya// shin tu sdug bsngal 'jig rten thams cad dang / na songs rnams dag tu
18b8: gnod gyur pa'i/ / gnas dang skyabs dang dpung gnyen gyur pa de// byang chub sems dpa' rnams la bstan par bya// gang zhig byang chub don du sems 'jog pa// de ni dang po'i byang chub sems par bstan// bslab pa'i/
19a1: gdams ngag ji bzhin nges byas pa// ji bzhin rnam par gzhag pa 'di de'i yin// nad bral rnams kyi bstan pa ji bzhin du// 'jig rten kun la phan pa bya ba'i phyir// de ltar thog ma su zhig sems skyed pa/ 'di ni gnyis
19a2: te dang po'i las can no/ / phan pa thob byed sems dang rab dang bde// gnyen dang sdug dang de bzhin sdud sems dang // kun tu bsrung ba'i sems dang snyoms pa'i sems// blo dpon sems dang snyoms par ston pa'i sems// de
19a3: 'dra dag la sems gnas gyur pa de/ / lung nod kha ton byed par sbyar bar bya// / mang du thos nas dgon par gnas su gzhug/ dben par gyur nas dge bshes sten du gzhug/ dge bshes rnams la dka' blo bde bar bya// dus
19a4: tshed shes la shes bzhin ldan par bya/ / dus shes gyur nas shin du 'jigs med bya// 'jigs pa med nas don la brtson par bya// don shes gyur nas de bzhin chos brjod bya// chos rnams kun la rmongs gyur med par bya// rmongs
19a5: pa med par gyur nas rgyal ba'i sras/ / legs par gsungs pa'i chos la bsam par bya// 'di ni dang po'i las can brjod pa ste// byang chub zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yin// 'di ni gdams pa 'di ni bstan pa ste// 'di
19a6: la su slob de ni sangs rgyas sras/ / byang chub sems dpa' gsum pa gang yin pa// chos kyi rgyal po'i bstan la rab tu sbyor// mi rtag nyid dang sdug bsngal stong nyid dang // bdag med pa dang g.yo ba med pa dang // de bzhin chos 'di
19a7: thams cad bdag min dang / / mngon par 'du byed med dang dben pa dang // 'di dag thams cad rtog pa med yin pa / byang chub sems dpa' de ltar rtog par byed// sems can khams dang chos kyi dbyings la yang // brtag par bya phyir
19a8: de ni gzeng yang bstod/ / 'jig rten khams ni mtha' yas mu med ces// de ltar de ni dpyod du gzhug par bya// 'di nas dang chu dang de bzhin me// rlung dang nam mkha' ji snyed yod pa dang // phyogs na 'dod dang gzugs dang gzugs
19b1: med pa/ / de dag rnams la de ni dpyod du gzhug/ rgya chen chos rnams kun dang khams rnams kyi// rang bzhin ma lus mthar thug brtag bya ba// de ni sangs rgyas sras po sbyor byed la// phan par bya phyir rjes su bstan pa yin// byang
19b2: chub sems dpa' skye bar gang skyes pa/ / bstan la skyes shing rab tu 'byung bar byed// blo ldan de ni dngos med dngos po rtogs// dam chos gnas su skyes te legs par bskyes// de ni rang gis las yongs mi ldog/ sangs rgyas
19b3: mthar thug yin par 'dzin pa skye/ / rtag du chos la nges par sems dang ldan// sems can rang bzhin ci 'drar rnam par dpyod// las dang 'jig rten dag dang zhing rnams dang // rnam par smin dang 'khor dang mya ngan 'das// rnam par
19b4: dbye ba rgyal ba'i sras kyis shes/ / de thugs skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpar brjod// thams cad mkhyen pa 'das dang byung rnams dang // ma byon dag kyang chos rnams rnam dpyad nas// grub dang gang yang legs skyes mthar thug
19b5: dang / rang byung rnams kyi grub pa ci 'dra ba// sangs rgyas dam pa de dag thams cad ni// dus gsum mnyam nyid rjes su zhugs pa shes// nam yang mnyam nyid bye brag 'byed mi byed// de ni dus gsum tha dad med par 'jug/ gang gi
19b6: phan yon rnam par 'di 'dra ba/ / de ni byang chub sems dpa' bzhi pa ste// 'di dag rab bsgrubs byang chub sems dpa' de// byang chub don du nges par 'byung bar 'gyur// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' lnga pa ste// sbyor ba phun sum tshogs
19b7: par brjod pa yin/ / thabs la mkhas pa'i rjes su zhugs pa skye// bsod nams las dag brtsams pas mthar phyin byed// de ltar bsod nams rab tu ci byed kyang // 'jig rten kun gyi rten du 'gyur ba dang // phan par 'dod dang bde ba
19b8: thob byed dang / / snying brtse ba dang skye dgu dkrol 'gyur byed// 'jig rten gnod gyur gdul bar bya ba'i phyir// 'dren par byed cing rab tu dang bar byed// sems can mang po thams cad gdul 'dod pa// myangan 'das pa'i sems kyis bcu
20a1: yang che/ / 'jig rten thams cad mtha' ma med pa dang // de bzhin dpag tu med cing grangs med dang // mtshungs med bsam yas mnyam med gzhal yas dang // stong pa mi g.yo med pa'i rang bzhin shes// de ni byang chub
20a2: sems dpa' lnga pa ste/ / sbyor ba phun tshegs phan dang snying brtse ldan// de la rjes su bstun pa 'di 'dra ste// yon tan kun dang ldan pa rnams kyis bstan// de ni sems can mtha' yas thams cad dang // chos kyi ngo bo nyid la
20a3: rmongs pa med/ / shin tu blo ldan rtog bral rnam rtog med// 'jig rten lha dang bcas pas dbyer mi phyed// sangs rgyas chos dang byang chub sems dpa' dang // spyod pa'i sngags dang sngags pa ma yin dang // sems can chung dam/
20a4: yang na che'o zhes// thos par gyur kyang bsam las nur ba med// sems can nyon mongs can nam rnam dag gam// gdul sla zhes 'am gdul bar dka' zhe 'am// chos dbyings chung zhe 'am yang na rgya che 'am// 'jig par 'gyur
20a5: zhe 'am chags par 'gyur zhe 'am/ / chos dbyings yod ce'am med ces thos gyur kyang // dus gsum rtogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de// nges par sems shing thams cad rnam dpyod de// sangs rgyas chos 'dir bsam pa
20a6: shin tu nges/ / mtshan ma med dang mtshan nyid med pa dang // dngos med rang bzhin brdzun zhing dben pa dang // sgyu ma'i rang bzhin mig yor 'dra ba yi// chos mchog zhi ba 'di 'dra nyan par byed// de ltar mi ldog byang chub sems dpa' ni//
20a7: sangs rgyas chos dang byang chub sems dpa' dang // spyod pa yod dam med ces nges par dpyod// 'byung ngam mi 'byung zhe na'ang phyir mi ldog/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'das she 'am ma 'das sha 'am// ma byon ce'am ma byon ma
20a8: yin zhe'am/ / byung ngam ma byung zad dam mi zad dam// de bzhin mtshan nyid gcig gam mtshan nyid med// gcig dang tha dad rnam pa mang po dang // don tam tshig 'bru dngos dang dngos med pa// thams cad sgro btags rnam pa gzhan nyid
20b1: ru/ mi ldog byang chub sems dpa' yid ches byed// mtshan ma med dang mtshan ma yod pa dang // mtshan nyid med dang mtshan gyis mtshon pa dang // rnam par phye ba phan tshun sbyar ba rnams// thos nas 'di la mthar thug
20b2: 'jug par byed/ / gzhon nur gyur pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni// lus dang ngag dang de bzhin yid kyis kyang // 'bras bu yod pa'i las rnams byed 'gyur zhing // ji ltar 'dod bzhin 'dir ni skye ba ston// pha rol
20b3: rnams kyi bsam pa rtog byed cing / / de dag rnams kyi mos pa spyod par byed// sems can spyod dang rjes su 'thun chos dang // zhing rnams 'jig dang chags pa rnams kyang shes// ji ltar 'dod sbyin myur du mngon shes
20b4: thob/ / phyogs rnams kun du yid ni 'jug par byed// bde gshegs bsngags pa'i chos rnams thos nas kyang // de la de ni nur bar 'gyur ba med// yongs su shes dang zhing g.yo byed pa dang // de bzhin byin gyis
20b5: brlab dang rnam dpyod dang / / ji ltar skad cig grangs med 'gro 'gyur ba// zhing du 'gro bar bya ba brjod par bya// de ni dri ba grangs med 'dri bar byed// lus rnams ci 'drar yid kyi lus kyang ston// de la skra skad sbyor ba
20b6: 'khyam zas dang / / da cag la yang sangs rgyas grangs med brjod/ byang chub sems dpa' rgyal cha ba gang yin pa// sems can rnams kyi 'jug pa de bzhin shes// de dag nyini yongs rgyud dang gzigs dang /
20b7: nga nga / ma dang/ 'a pa da sa 'a // ba pa nu pa / u la
20b8: 'khor la mkhas pa car 'byin te/ / der yang de ltar kun du spyang pa dang // gnas dang de bzhin 'jug par bya ba dang // ba brang 'khor na ci 'dra dpyad pa dang // dam chos rgyal ba'i dbang bzung ci 'dra dang // byi gyi rna
21a1: dang gzhan gnon ci 'dra dang / / chos la 'jug dang dka' lung brjod bya ste// 'di ni rgyal tshab sa la 'jug pa yin// de tsam gyis na de yi mthar thug ste// ji skad bstan bzhin gzhan du 'gyur ba med//
21a2: tsheyi 'du byed nam zhig 'dor ba na// tshul ldan rgyal tsha ba rgyal bar mngon du phyogs// dbang bskur gang yin bde gshegs sras gcig ste// thu bo khyad 'phags mthar phyin bdag nyid can// skra thigs gcig tha
21a3: chu tshad gzung du rung / / 'dir ni bsam pa bgrang bas rtogs ma yin// rgyal sras rnams kyi spyod pa 'di 'dra ste// 'di ni sems can la las zhing rnams kun// pra rab rdul du blags nas ma lus 'grang // grangs
21a4: med 'di snyed cig ces gcod byed pa/ / de kun 'di ni byang chub sems dpas shes// 'das dang de bzhin ma byon sangs rgyas dang // gang dag phyogs bcu dag na bzhugs pa dang // rang sangs rgyas dang de bzhin nyan
21a5: thos kyi/ / sa bon gyur pa byang chub sems de skye// thog mar byang chub sems shes gang brjod pa// de ni ji lta'i tshul du'ang grangs med de// 'jig rten khams 'di kun kyang khyab gyur na// de las gong du brjod pa ci
21a6: zhig yod/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu khyod kyis dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs bshad pa legs par smras
21a7: so/ / rigs kyi bu sangs rgyas kyi yon tan rnams ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste// gang dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'dri'i ming thos pa'i sems can de dag kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du nye bar gyur pa yin na// gang dag
21a8: chos kyi rnam grangs 'di 'dzin pa dang / / klog pa dang / kun chub par byed pa dang / de bzhin nyid du sgrub par byed pa lta smos kyang ci dgos te// de dag ni nges par sangs rgyas su 'gyur ro// chos kyi blo gros kyis
21b1: smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de de bzhin no// ji skad smras pa bzhin te/ shes rab zab mo dang ldan pa de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pas dbang bskur ba yin par rig par bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang
21b2: pos smras pa/ / rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig gi rna lam du'i// bu'i chos 'di dag grag par gyur pa'i skyes bu dam pa de dag kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams la lung bstan par rig par bya ba
21b3: yin na/ chos kyi rnam grangs 'di gang dag gis lag tu thob pa lta smos kyang ci dgos// de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom
21b4: ldan 'das gzigs su gsol/ / bdag gis 'di lta bu'i chos 'di dag ma 'tshal bas bdag ni dmus long dang 'dra ba lags so// bcom ldan 'das bdag gcig bud mus long lta bur gyur par ma pas kyi/
21b5: bcom ldan 'das sems can gang dag gis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di ma thos pa de dag thams cad kyang dmus long lta bur gyur pa lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ gnas brtan de de bzhin
21b6: teji skad spras pa bzhin no/ / shA ra dwa ti'i bus gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa nyid bkang gso// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu song la brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang
21b7: 'jig rten skyong ba thams cad skul cig/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' yang sgrogs shig/ chos kyi phyag rgya dam pa dkon mchog ta la la zhes bya ba'i gzungs 'di yang 'khor der sgrogs shig/ de nas che
21b8: d ang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' thos nas dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs 'di'i don gyi phyir yongs su skom pas brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten skyong ba de dag la don 'di'i
22a1: skabs brjod de chos nyan pa thams cad 'du bar bgyis shig/ de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog tA la la'i gzungs 'chad cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa nyid kyang ston par 'gyur gyis 'du bar gyis shig/
22a2: khyed phyis 'gyod par gyur ta re/ kye grogs po dag mdo sde rin po che 'di lta bu dag 'jig rten du 'byung ba ni shin tu rnyed par dka'o// de nas skad cig de nyid la brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten skyong ba thams cad 'dus
22a3: nas bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis spyan sngar 'khod nas thal mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba btab pa bcom ldan 'das kyis dkon mchog ta la la'i
22a4: gzungs bshad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das cang mi gsung bar gyur pas gnang ba mdzad do// brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten skyong ba tham cad kyis lan gnyis lan gsum du gsol ba btab na yang
22a5: bcom ldan 'das cad mi gsung bar gyur to/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyis dkon mchog ta la la zhes bgyi ba'i gzungs bshad du
22a6: gsol/ bde bar gshegs pas bshad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe zhal nas ljags kyi dbang po phyung ste/ rigs kyi bu gang la la dag dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs 'di'i don gyi phyir/
22a7: de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba 'debs pa de dag thams cad ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ro zhes stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su dbyangs
22a8: kyis go bar mdzad do/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis yang tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ra dwa ti'i bu khyod song la 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la tshes bshad par gsol
22b1: pathob shig de'i tshe 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa shing blag sha dang sa la'i dring gzhan zhig dadakyil mo dkrung bcas shing lus mi g.yo bar 'dug ste/ nyi ma bye ba zhag khrig bcu stong pas lhag pa'i kha dog
22b2: dkod pa chen po dang ldan pa'i khang pa brtsegs par brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten skyong ba rnams kyis yongs su bskor cing mdun gyis bltas na 'dug par gyur te/ gser gyi kha dog lta bu'i lus dang / dpal
22b3: gyis lam me ldan ne lteng nger 'dug go/ / de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA rA dwa ti'i bus 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa ga la ba der song ste 'jam dpal gzhon nur b+har pa la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu de bzhin
22b4: gshegs pa ni khyod la chos bshad par gsol ba 'debs so/ / de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces smras so// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa zhes
22b5: bya ba'i gzhi'i don 'di gang yin/ shA ra dwa ti'i bus smras pa/ rigs kyi bu khyod ni shes rab zab pa ste/ kho bos ni khyod dang 'gyed mi nus so// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ khyod snying las chung ngur 'dug shig dang khyod
22b6: kyis ji ltar bzod pa de bzhin du bstan par bya'o/ / shA ra dwa ti'i bus smras pa/ rigs kyi bu kho bo nyan gyis khyod kyis shod cig/ de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas ting nge 'dzin de las langs te/ stong gsum
22b7: gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams dbyangs kyis go bar byas so/ / de nas de'i tshe stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams na gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu nas 'og min gyi bar gyi lha'i bu ji snyed
22b8: 'khod pa de dag thams cad 'dus par gyur to/ / rgyal po chen po bzhi dpung dang g.yog tu bcas pa yang gnod sbyin bye ba du ma dang lhan cig 'dus par gyur to// brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten skyong ba rnams
23a1: kyang 'dus par gyur to/ / lha'i bu mo mang po yang 'dus par gyur to// dge slong gi 'khor dang dge slong ma'i 'khor dang / dge bsnyen gyi 'khor dang / dge bsnyen ma'i 'khor dang / de bzhin du sum bcu rtsa gsum pa'i
23a2: bar gyi 'khor dang / 'thab bral gyi 'khor dang / dga' ldan gyi 'khor dang / 'phrul dga'i 'khor dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha'i 'khor dang / tshangs pa'i 'khor dang / de bzhin du 'og min gyi bar gyi lha'i 'khor rnams
23a3: 'dus par gyur to/ / de bzhin du nyan thos kyi tshogs kyang 'dus par gyur te/ 'di lta ste/ tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor dang / tshe dang ldan pa 'od srung chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa maud gal gyi bu chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i/
23a4: bu dang / tshe dang ldan pa kA t+yA'i bu chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa ma 'gag pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa gA ya 'od srung dang / tshe dang ldan pa gsus po che dang / tshe dang ldan pa lam phran bstan dang / tshe dang ldan pa nam gru dang / tshe dang ldan pa chu
23a5: klung 'od srung dang / tshe dang ldan pa steng rgyas 'od srung dang / tshe dang ldan pa byams ma'i bu gang po dang / tshe dang ldan pa sgra can zin dang / tshe dang ldan pa bzang skyong dang / tshe dang ldan pa rlangs pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo
23a6: dang / de dag dang nyan thos chen po gzhan dag dang / grags 'dzin la sogs pa dge slong ma lnga brgya yang 'dus par gyur to// khams kyi rgyal po dang / stobs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba dag kyang 'dus par gyur to// rgyal rigs/
23a7: dang bram ze dang khyim bdag gi 'khor dag kyang 'dus par gyur to// de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas te 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das deng 'di ltar
23a8: 'khor chen po 'dus pa 'di su'i mthu lags/ de ji ltar 'tshal bar bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dra ti'i bu 'di ni dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs kyi mthu yin no// shA ra dwa ti'i bus
23b1: gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das dkon mchog ta la la'i gzus mnyan par 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu song la 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun du
23b2: bzang po la gsol ba thob shig/ de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu khyod kyis ting nge 'dzin rin po che bstan pa dkon mchog tal la 'di shod cig/
23b3: 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs nyan par 'gyur ba su yin/ shA ra dwa ti'i bus smras pa/ 'khor bzhi 'dus pa 'di dag dang / brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten skyong ba rnams
23b4: 'dus pa 'di dag ste kho bo yang nyan pa'i phyir 'ongs so/ / de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas gnas brtan shA ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces smras so// gnas brtan shA ra dwa ti'i bu chos nyan pa 'di dag ni sgyu mas byung ba sha stag
23b5: na kho bos su la chos bshad/ nyan pa ni su yin/ 'chang ba ni su yin/ gnas brtan gyis smras pa/ skyes bu dam pa khyod kyis shod cig/ kho bos nyan to// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu bshad ces bya ba de
23b6: gang gi tshig bla dgas yin/ / smras pa/ 'jam dpal bshad pa zhes bya ba de ni stong pa nyid kyi tshig bla dgas so// smras pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu stong pa nyid gang gi tshig bla dgas yin/ smras pa/ 'jam dpal stong pa nyid ni tshig med
23b7: pa yin no/ / 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu chos thams cad ni bstan du med pa yin te/ de dag ni bstan du med cing mnyan du med do// gnas brtan gyis smras pa/ rigs kyi bu khyod kyis ji lta bu bstan
23b8: pa de dag thams cad ni stong pa nyid bstan pa/ mtshan ma med pa bstan pa/ smon pa med pa bstan pa/ blang ba med pa bstan pa/ dor ba med pa bstan pa/ spros pa med pa bstan pa ste/ ma spros pa bstan pa yin no// de nas
24a1: thams cad dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor de dang / brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba de dag kyang rab tu dga' nas 'grin gcig tu 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa shA ra
