24a2: dwa ti'i bus dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs 'di legs par bshad do zhes legs so zhes bya ba byin no/ / de nas tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces smras so// 'jam dpal byang chub
24a3: sems dpas dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs 'di ji ltar gzung bar bya/ klag par bya/ kun chub par bya/ gzhan dag la yang rgya cher yang dag par bshad par bya/ 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ rab 'byor gzungs 'di ni skye ba med
24a4: par yid la bya'o/ / dngos po med pa dang / mtshan nyid med pa dang / spros pa med pa dang / dor ba med par yid la bya'o// 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bshad pa na 'khor de'i nang nas byang chub sems dpa' dgu
24a5: bcu rtsa gnyis kyis dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob par gyur to/ / lha dang mi drug bcu rtsa gnyis ni mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po bstan las langs te bla gos
24a6: phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas thal mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi snying rje chen po ci 'dra ba zhig lags/ bcom ldan 'das
24a7: kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi snying rje chen po ni gang khams gsum pa yongs su mi gtong ba ste/ 'di ni snying rje chen po yin no// gang sems can thams
24a8: cad la sangs rgyas kyi zhing kun du ston pa 'di ni snying rje chen po yin no/ / gang sems can tshul khrims 'chal ba yongs su 'dzin pa 'di ni snying rje chen po yin no// gang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mi 'dor ba 'di ni snying
24b1: rje chen po yin no/ / gang sems can thams cad kyi don gyi phyir lus dang srog yongs su gtong ba de ni snying rje chen po yin no// gang 'dod chags spyod pa'i sems can rnams la byams pa yang dag par brjed pa 'di ni
24b2: snying rje chen po yin no/ / gang sems can stobs dang ldan rnams la byams pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi snying rje chen po yin no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa'
24b3: sems dpa' chen pos sems can thams cad la zhe 'grus pa med pa'i sems su bya'o/ / 'dre ba med pa mang du bya'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos 'di skad ces gsol
24b4: to/ / skye bo mang po la sman pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba dang / skye bo phal po che dang lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang sman pa dang / bde bar 'gyur ba'i slad du/ bcom ldan 'das kyi dkon mchog
24b5: tal la zhes bgyi ba'i gzungs bshad du gsol/ sems can thams cad la sman pa dang / thugs brtse ba mnga' ba bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshangs pa'i dbyangs kyis
24b6: byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / khyed kyi nang na phyi ma'i tshe phyi ma'i dus lnga brgya tha ma la dam pa'i chos nub pa'i dus kyi tshe chos kyi rnam grangs 'di yang dag par rab tu ston par spro ba su
24b7: yod/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po dang / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug dang / byang chub sems dpa' mthu chen thob dang / byang chub sems
24b8: dpa' ngan song spong dang / byang chub sems dpa' sman gyi rgyal po dang / byang chub sems dpa' spobs pa brtsegs dang / byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad kyis mngon 'phags rgyal po dang / byang chub sems
25a1: dpa' blo gros mi zad pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' blo gros rgya mtsho dang / byang chub sems dpa' rin chen zeb ldan dang / byang chub sems dpa' nor bu 'od dang / byang chub sems dpa' gtsug na nor bu can dang /
25a2: byang chub sems dpa' rnam par lta dang / byang chub sems dpa' bltar mi thod dang / byang chub sems dpa' rtag du lta dang / byang chub sems dpa' lag na rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' rin chen phung po dang / byang chub
25a3: sems dpa' dkon mchog 'byung gnas dang / byang chub sems dpa' chos dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' tog dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' nor dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams dpal dang / byang
25a4: chub sems dpa' tsan dan dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' bdud rtsi blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' bsam yas blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams
25a5: kyis brgyan dang / byang chub sems dpa' yon tan gyis brgyan dang / byang chub sems dpa' mtshan gyis brgyan dang / byang chub sems dpa' rtag tu dgod cing dbang po thams cad rab tu dga' ba dang / byang chub sems
25a6: dpa' ri'i rtse mo rdob pa'i rgyal po dang / byang chub sems dpa' spobs pa mkhas dang / byang chub sems dpa' rtag tu lag brgyad dang / byang chub sems dpa' sa 'dzin dang / byang chub sems dpa' spobs pa myur dang / byang
25a7: chub sems dpa' nam mkha'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' zla ba'i snying po dang // byang chub sems dpa' nyi ma'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' zla ba dri ma med pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa'
25a8: gdugs snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' mngon 'phags rgyal po dang / byang chub sems dpa' lhun po chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa' blo gros brtan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' spobs pa dpa' ba dang
25b1: byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa dang / de dag la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag drug bcu rtsa gnyis kyis mgrin gcig tu tshig tu smras pa/ bcom ldan 'das slar
25b2: ma'i tshe slad ma'i dus lnga brgya tha ma la dam pa'i chos nub pa'i dus kyi tshe bdag cag thams cad 'dus shing tshegs te/ dkon mchog ta la la zhes bgyi ba'i gzungs yang dag par bshad par spro lags so// bcom ldan
25b3: 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu dag legs so legs so// rigs kyi bre dag 'di dka' ba ste/ cho ga 'di 'dra ba 'di ni shin tu bya dka' ba'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa'
25b4: kun du bzang po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / rigs kyi bu skye bo mang po la phan pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde bar 'gyur ba dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs nyon cig/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dkod pa chen
25b5: po'i seng ge'i khri la bzhugs te bsngags bka' stsal pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// tad+ya thA/ oM ma/ b+ha ra te/ b+ha ra te/ b+ha ra
25b6: na b+ha ra na te swA hA/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mal lachog mal la chos A la la chos shes lan gnyis lan gsum du ched du brjod pa ched du ba pa do// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang
25b7: pos 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das chos chos shes bgyi ba 'di'i gzhi'i don gang lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu chos thams cad kyi gzhi'i don ni gzhi
25b8: med pa'i don to/ / chos thams cad kyi gzhi'i don ni dngos po med pa'i gzhi'i don to// chos thams cad kyi gzhi'i don ni nam mkha'i gzhi'i don to// chos thams cad kyi gzhi'i don ni blang ba med pa'i
26a1: gzhi'i don to/ / chos thams cad kyi gzhi'i don ni dor ba med pa'i gzhi'i don to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'on ci'i slad du ches thams cad
26a2: ces bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu chos thams cad ces bya ba ni mig dang / rna ba dang / sna dang / lce dang lus dang yid dang de bzhin du khams rnams dang skye mched rnams dang rten cing
26a3: 'brel bar 'byung ba ste/ rigs kyi bu 'di ni chos thams cad ces bya'o// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang chos thams cad ni gzod ma nas ma skyes pa'i phyir stong pa'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas byang
26a4: chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs 'di ji ltar gzung bar bya/ de skad ces smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos
26a5: 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces smras so/ / de bzhin nyid bstan pa dang / skye ba med pa'i de bzhin nyid dang / 'byung ba med pa'i de bzhin nyid dang / mtshan nyid med pa'i de bzhin nyid dang / nam mkha'
26a6: de bzhin nyid dang / dngos po med pa'i de bzhin nyid dang / ngo bo nyid kyi de bzhin nyid dang / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi de bzhin nyid du gzungs 'di gzung bar bya ste/ rigs kyi bu dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs
26a7: 'di gzung ba dang / kun du gzung ba dang bsgom pa dang rnam par dpyad pa dang / gdags pa dang rab tu gzhag pa dang / rnam par dgrol ba dang / rnam par dbye ba dang gsal bar bya ba ni 'di 'dra ste/ rigs kyi bu 'di ni dkon
26a8: mchog ta la la'i gzungs bsgom pa dang / rnam par brtag pa'i don to// de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces smras so// 'jam dpal khyod chos kyi rnam grangs 'di
26b1: la yang dag par zhugs nas yun ji srid cig lon/ / 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ shA ra dri ti'i bu 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang gti mug rnams yAn ji srid nas zhugs pa srid do// shA ra dwa ti'i bus smras pa/ rigs kyi
26b2: bu 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug rnams yun ji srid nas zhugs/ 'jam dpel gyis smras pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu sa'i khams yun ji srid cig nas zhugs pa srid do// shA dwa ti'i bus spras pa/ rigs kyi
26b3: bla sa'i khams yun ji srid nas zhugs/ 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ shA ra dri ti'i bri dag pa dang / mau rag pa yun ji srad nas zhugs pa srid do// shA ra dI ti'i dus smras pa/ rigs kyi bu rig pa dang / mi rig pa yun tri
26b4: srid nas zhugs/ 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu nam mkha'i khams yun ji srid nas zhugs pa srid do// shA ra dwa ti'i bus smras pa/ 'jam dpal nam mkha'i khams yun ji srid nas zhugs 'jam dpal gyis
26b5: smras pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis chos thams cad yun ji srid nas zhugs pa srid do// de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces smras so// kho bo skyes
26b6: bu dam pa 'di lta bu dag dang gtam bya ba'i nus pa kho bo lagal to/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ khyi dang byi la thams cad dam/ wa thams cad kyis kyang ri'i rgyal po ri rab gzhig par mi nus so// rigs kyi bu de bzhin
26b7: du shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di 'dra ba'i nyan thos thams cad kyis kyang byang chub sems dpa'i bstan pa gcig gi mtha' yang rtogs par mi nus na/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i bstan pa lta ci smos// de nas byang chub sems
26b8: dpa' kun du bzang pos 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces smras so/ / 'jam dpal bzhud la phyi ma'i tshe phye ma'i dus na mdo sde'i rgyal po 'dzin pa chos smra ba de dag la kun du bsrung ba dang / yongs su bskyang
27a1: ba mdzad par de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol pa thob shig/ de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas rang gi chos kyi stan las langs nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// gang dag chos kyi rnam
27a2: grangs 'di 'dzin pa dang / klog pa dang kun chub par bgyid pa dang / gzhan dag la yang rgya cher yang dag par ston par bgyid pa/ chos smra ba de dag gi yon tan gyi khyad par rnams bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad du gsol/
27a3: bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal dge slong mdo sde'i rgyal po 'dzin pa chos smra ba/ de dag ni de'i chos kyi sku la nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byang chub thob par 'gyur ro de dag
27a4: ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams la nye bar 'gyur ro/ / de dag la bdud dang bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu glags lta ba rnams kyis glags mi rnyed par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu gang su dag chos smra ba'i dge slong de la se gol gtog
27a5: pa gcig tsam srid cig mi byams pa'i sems bskyed pa de dag ni mir 'gyur ba las kyang ring du gyur pa yin na sangs rgyas kyi byang chub la lta smos kyang ci dgos/ 'jam dpal gzhan yang gang dag mdo sde'i rgyal po
27a6: 'di 'dzin pa'i dge slong rnams lam dang pa'i sems bskyed pa de dag ni so thags ngan par 'gyur/ lce dang sna med par 'gyur/ rkang lag phyi phyogs su 'gyur// / lus nad bu can du 'gyur/ mig med par 'gyur/ shes
27a7: rab 'chal ba'i rang bzhin du 'gyur/ brtson 'grus chung bar 'gyur te/ 'jam dpal 'di dag ni mi gti mug pa de dag gi skyon du gyur pa'o// 'jam dpal mdor bshad na de dag 'chi ba'i dus kyi tshe de dag gi spu'i khung bu
27a8: re rer yang sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal dpag tu med par 'jug go/ gal te mir skyes na yang rtag du dmus long du 'gyur/ lce med par 'gyur ro// 'jam dpal gzhan yang gang dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'di
27b1: spong ba de dag ni tshe 'di nyid la lus mdze can du 'gyur/ mchu 'jigs 'jigs ltar 'dug par 'gyur/ lus zhom par 'gyur/ lus gcer bur 'gyur/ lus skam por 'gyur/ yi dgas 'dra bar 'gyur ro// dam
27b2: dpal gzhan yang mi gti mug pa de dag gang du skye bar 'gyur ba de dag gi gnas na ngas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pas mkhyen to/ / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas gsol pa/ bcom ldan
27b3: 'das kyis lung bstan du gsol/ bde bar gshegs pas lung bstan du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal kha rog de skad ma dri shig/ 'di la lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten
27b4: myos par 'gyur te skrag par 'gyur dngang par 'gyur/ rab tu dngang bar 'gyur ro// 'jam dpal gyis gsol pa/ sems can 'di dag gis 'di lta bu thos nas slan chad nam yang dam pa'i chos spong bar mi 'gyur bar bgyi ba'i
27b5: slad du thugs brtse bar dgongs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad du gsol// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal sa'i 'og na sems can dmyal ba yod pa'i ming la 'di lta ste/ tsha ba dang rab tu tsha ba dang
27b6: thig nag dang kun du 'bar ba dang rab tu 'bar ba dang reg dka' ba dang / drag po dang mchu rnon dang lcags kyi thu lum dang lcags kyi be con can dang mun khung dang mgo bstod dang spyi'u tshugs dang spyi'u gtong dang rtag tu 'bar dang dul
27b7: pa dang rtag du dring dang rab 'joms dang des 'joms dang shin du gnod 'joms rnams te 'jam dpal mi gti mug pa de dag gang du skye bar 'gyur ba'i sems can dmyal ba ni 'di dag go/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub
27b8: sems dpa' kun du bzang pos 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das chos smra ba de dag 'di nas shi'i phos nas gang du skye bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun du bzang po khyod kyis zhus pa de legs
28a1: par zhus so/ / kun du bzang po rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo chos smra ba de 'di nas shi 'phos nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa spobs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi
28a2: khams rab tu brgyan par skye bar 'gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi khams de na byang chub sems dpa' kun nas mdzes pa sha stag go/ 'chi ba'i dus kyi tshe rigs kyi bu de la sangs rgyas bye ba phrag bcu gnyis mngon du 'gyur ro// rigs
28a3: kyi bu mdor na rigs kyi bu de'i phan yon ni grangs med dpag tu med de/ de dag ni bskal pa stong dag gis kyang brjod par mi nus so// byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das slad ma'i chi slad ma'i
28a4: dus na gang dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'di spong bar 'gyur ba'i sems can ji lta bu dag 'byung bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun du bzang po 'di lta bu'i chos 'di dag spong bar 'gyur ba'i sems can de dag ni phal
28a5: cher rab tu byung ba dag 'byung ste/ 'di skad du 'di dag ni snyan dngags sbyar ba yin gyi/ 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa ma yin no// 'di dag ni nga bzor byas pa yin te/ mdo sde 'di dag ni sngon nam yang ma thos so zhes 'dzer
28a6: cing de dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'di spong bar 'gyur ro/ / spangs nas kyang mthol zhing 'chags par mi 'gyur te/ de dag chos spangs pas 'chi bI tshe sems can dmyal ba kun du 'bar ba mi bzad par skye bar 'gyur ro// skyes ma thag tu
28a7: lcags kyi 'khor los mi gti mug pa de dag gi mgo gcad nas sa la lung bar 'gyur ro/ / de ltar gyur nas kyang bskal pa mang po bskal pa brgya phrag mang po dang / bskal pa stong phrag mang por dmus long du 'gyur ro// gal te bskal
28a8: pa brgya dag 'das nas mir skye bar 'gyur na yang tshe rabs thams ca du mum du bye bar 'gyur zhing lce med pa dang / gdong phyin phyogs su 'dug pa dang ltag skur dang / 'jid pa nub pa dang rkang kyol dang re khyi skad lta bu dang rtag tu bkres
28b1: shing sgom pas nyen pa dang / lus skams pa dang kha mnam pa dang / sems can thams cad kyis mthong nga ma thos na yid du mi 'ong bar skye bar 'gyur ro// de nas thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor des mgrin kacig tu tshig smras pa/
28b2: bcom ldan 'das ma 'tshal ba bdag cag gis mdo sde 'di lta bu dag spangs pa dang / chos smra ba de dag la khros pa'i sems kyis bltos par gyur pa rnams nom pa la nongs par chags so// bcom ldan bdag cag ji ltar byis par gyur
28b3: pa dang / ji ltar rmongs par gyur pa dang / ji ltar shes rab 'tshal par gyur pa dang / ji ltar blo chung bar gyur pa rnams 'chags shing mchis na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dgongs su gsol// de nas nyan thos chen po
28b4: de dag dang brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten skyong ba de dag dang dge slong dang dge slong ma dang dge bsnyen dang dge bsnyen ma de dag spangs nas bcom ldan 'das bdag cag ni bstan pa 'di lta bu 'di dag thos nas rab tu sngangs lags so/ /
28b5: bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ grogs po dag de de bzhin no// ji skad smras pa bzhin te/ khyed kyis skrag par bya ba'i rigs so// grogs po dgar thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes brnyes pa yin na nga nyid kyang skrag na
28b6: gang dag nga'i slob ma rnams lta ci smos/ rigs kyi bu dag chos 'di ni zab pa ste/ de ni mi 'am mi ma yin pa'am lha 'am klu 'am/ gnod sbyin nam/ dri za 'am sus kyang rnam par dkrug par mi nus na dge sbyong ngam bram ze
28b7: gzhan dag gis lta ga la nus te ci smos/ rigs kyi bu dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'di ni lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi mchod rten du gyur pa ste/ rigs kyi bu dag dper na dkon mchog za ma tog ji lta bar mdo sde'i rgyal
28b8: po 'di yang de ltar bzhin du blta bar bya'o/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das la 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das 'di ni legs par gsungs pa legs so// bcom ldan 'das dge slong
29a1: de lta bu de dag gis dad pas stsal ba ji ltar yongs su 'ju bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal gang dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'di spong ba dang / chos smra ba de dag la mi byams pa'i
29a2: sems skyed pa de dag ni nyi ma gcig gam/ se gol gtogs pa gcig srid tsam zhig dang pas phyin pa yongs su spyad pa 'am/ tha na dge 'dun la phul ba'i sa la mchil mthal gcig 'dor du yang ngas ma gnang ngo //
29a3: nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das mtshams ma mchis pa lnga po dag 'di dang nye ba lags sam/ 'on te ring ba lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis ba kA
29a4: stsal pa/ gnas brtan shA ra dwa ti'i bu kha rog de skad ma smra shig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu mtshams med pa lnga po dag ni bla'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di spangs pa ni nam yang de lta ma yin no// shA ra dwa ti'i bu
29a5: mtshams med pa lnga byed pa ni mtshams med pa lnga po dag myur du zad par byas nas mir skye bar 'gyur ro/ / dam pa'i chos spong ba'i gang zag de na nam yang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams thob par mi 'gyur te/ de ni bdag
29a6: kyang phung la gzhan yang phung bar byed par 'gyur ro/ / de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan snga na du zhing 'di skad ces gsol to// e ma'o dam pa'i chos spong ba'i sems can rnams ni sdug
29a7: bsngal lo/ / las kyi sgrib pa 'di lta bu dag ni bdag gis rmi lam na yang mthong bar ma gyur cig/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ra dwa ti'i bud snyam
29a8: ma sems shig ngas chos bstan pa ni 'byung ba dang bcas pa yin na 'jig rten ni las bdag gir bya ba rang gi las kyi bgo skal la spyod pa/ rang gi las brtan par bya ba ste/ sems can dag reng rang gi las
29b1: rnams kyis sdug bsngal gyi tshor rab myong gi de la de bzhin gshegs pas ni ma lan no/ / shA ra dwa ti'i bu ngasi na dge legs su 'gro ba'i lam bshad de/ bde bar 'gro ba dang / 'jigs pa med par 'gro ba dang / mya ngan
29b2: las 'da' bar 'gro ba dang / 'chi ba med par 'gro ba'i lam bshad na/ 'on kyang sems can 'di dag ni lus kyis nyes par spyod pa dang ldan/ ngag gis nyes par spyod pa dang ldan/ yid kyis nyes par spyod pa dang ldan
29b3: zhing 'phags pa rnams la skur pa 'debs pa dang / log par lta ba dag ste/ log par lta ba'i las dang / chos yang dag par spangs pa'i rgyus lus zhig nas shi ba'i 'og tu ngan song ngan 'gro log par ltung ba'i
29b4: sems can dmyal ba rnams su skye ste/ de la de bzhin gshegs pas ni ma lan no// shA ra dwa ti'i bu sems can thams cad la nga'i snying rje 'di lta bu skye ste/ ngas sems can gcig gi don du yang bskal pa 'am/
29b5: bskal pa las lhag par sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal rnams myong bar bya ba'i sems can gcig po ni yongs su btang bar mi bya'o snyam ste/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po ni de 'dra'o/
29b6: shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di lta ste dper na/ mi nige la bu gcig pa gzugs bzang ba mdzes pa/ blta na sdug pa kha dog bzang po rgyas pa mchog dang ldan pa zhig yod la/ de rkyen 'ga' zhig dang phrad nas 'chi ba'i dus byas par
29b7: gyur na/ me de bu la sems pas sdug bsngal zhing yid mi bde bar 'gyur te/ ngu zhing smre sngags 'don to// shA ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang sems
29b8: can sdug bsngal bdag la bu gcig pa bzhin du dgongs pa mdzad de/ de bzhin gshegs pa dag nyon mongs pa rnams dang lhan cig gnas pa ni ma yin no// shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di lta ste dper na rgya mtsho chen po ni shi ba'i ro dang
30a1: lhan cig mi gnas so/ / shA ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa dag kyang nyon mongs pa rnams dang lhan cig mi gnas so// shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di lta ste dper na sgyu ma mkhan nam/ sgyu ma mkhan gyi slob ma mkhas
30a2: pas lam po che'i bzhi mdor skye bo'i tsho gas chen po mngon par sprul te/ bya ba dag ston kyang bya ba de dag ni yul na mi gnas phyogs nam gnas te/ ma skyes ma 'gags shing 'gags par mi 'gyur ro// shA ra dwa ti'i
30a3: bu de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyang sems can rnams yongs su smin par mdzad cing 'dod chags kyi spyod po yang ston te/ mdzad pa ston kyang spyod pa de dag ni yod pa ma yin no// dper na nam mkha'i
30a4: khams ni rnam par rtog pa med cing spros pa med pa'o/ / de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la yang rnam par rtog pa med cing spros pa med do// 'on kyang sems can rnams dang 'thun par de bzhin gshegs pa
30a5: rnams 'thun par mdzad do/ / sems can rnams ji ltar 'dul bar 'gyur ba de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'thun par 'jug go/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa la 'khrul pa mi mnga'o// de bzhin
30a6: gshegs pa la mi mkhyen pa mi mnga'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa la bskal ba mi mda'o// shA ra dwa ti'i bu nga ni lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi mthu bo dang / gtso bo dang rab dang mchog dang phul dang bla ma dang bla na med pa dang
30a7: gong na med pa dang / mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa yin te/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu tshig smras pa 'dri ni bden pa'i rjes su 'thun pa'o// rab tu byung ba 'am/ khyam pa yang rung ste/ sems can gang dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'di spong ba
30a8: dag thams cad ni sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal 'di lta bu dag rnyed par 'gyur ro/ / de nas tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis bcom ldan 'das kyis bstan pa 'di thos nas thal mo sbyar te bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad
30b1: ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das sems can de dag gis ni rnyed pa nongs par rnyed do// gang dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'di spong bar 'gyur ba de dag lce ci 'dra ba zhig du 'gyur ba lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal
30b2: pa/ rab 'byor de dag gi lu ni dpag tshad 'bum par 'gyur te/ de la lcags kyi theng gshol 'bar ba rab tu 'bar ba/ kun tu rab tu mched cing 'bar ba/ me lce gcig tu gyur pa bye ba phrag lnga brgyas rmo bar 'gyur ro// de ci'i
30b3: phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar des dag ma bsrungs pa'i phyir te/ rab 'byor mi gti mug pa de dag gi las kyi sgrib pa ni de lta bur 'gyur ro// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor des de bzhin gshegs/
30b4: pas bstan pa ni rmad du byung ba chen po lags so zhes ched du brjod pa ched du brjod do// de nas bcom ldan 'das la lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag gis chos smra/
30b5: ba'i dge slong de dag phrag pa la bkur bar bgyi'o// me tog dang bdug pa dang spos dang phreng ba dang byug pa rnams kyis mchod par bgyi'o// gdugs lan gsum mtshan lan gsum du phyag bgyi'o// bsnyen bkur
30b6: brtsi'o/ / sti stang bgyi'o// bla mar bgyi'o// ri mor bgyi'o// mchod par bgyi'o// rjed par bgyi'o// gsol bar bgyi'o// sti stang bgyi ba dang / bla mar bgyi ba dang / gus par bsrung bar bgyi'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ de dag
30b7: ni bcom ldan 'das kyi sras te chos kyi sku las nges par byang ba'i slad du'o/ / bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste dper na rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i bur gyur pa/ gzugs bzang pa mdzes pa/
30b8: blta na sdug pa de ni 'og ma thams cad kyi mchod pa'i 'o sa dade/ phyag bgyi ba'i 'os lags so// de bzhin du chos smra ba de dag kyang lha dang bcos pa'i 'jig rten gyi mchod pa'i 'os dang phyag bgyi ba'i 'os
31a1: lags so/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu lnga'i dbang po brgya byin gyis chos smra ba'i dge slong de dag snying las
31a2: chung ngur bya ba dang / yongs su bskyang ba dang / kun du bsrung ba dang / bskyab pa'i phyir tshig 'di legs par smras so// byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das bdag gis kyang rigs kyi bu
31a3: 'am rigs kyi bu mo de dag kun du bsrung bar bgyi'o/ / yongs su bskyab pa dang / yongs su gzung ba dang / zhi ba dang bde legs su 'gyur bar bgyi'o// dpag tshad brgya khor khor yug tu yongs su bskyang bar bgyi'o//
31a4: de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po la rigs kyi bu tshig 'di legs par smras pa legs so legs so zhes bya ba byin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshangs pa'i dbyangs kyis
31a5: tshigs su bcad pa 'di bka' stsal to/ / gzhan la phan dang bde ba byed pa bsags pa po// rnam pa sna tshogs rab mdzes mchog rab tshig ldan pa/ shin tu dri med bzhin ldan khyod kyi bsam pa mchog/ yon tan
31a6: rin chen mi mnyam mnyam pa tshig legs smras/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
31a7: dag chos du dang ldan na dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs 'thob par 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dag chos gcig dang ldan na dkon
31a8: mchog ta la la'i gzungs 'thob bo/ / chos gcig po gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste sems can thams cad la khong khro ba med pa'o// kun du bzang po byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dag gi chos gnyis te/
31b1: gnyis gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ phrag dog med pa dang rlom sems med pa ste/ kun du bzang po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dag gi chos gnyis so// kun du bzang po gzhan yang byang
31b2: chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni sems can thams cad la dbang po gnod par mi 'gyur ro/ / rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad la thams cad kyi thams cad du
31b3: rnam par 'tshe ba bskyed par mi bya'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan brjod pa 'di bshad pa dang / dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs kyi khyad par gyi yon tan yongs su brjod pa bshad pa na lha dang / mi'i skye dgu las sems
31b4: can dpag tu med pas gzungs thob par gyur to/ / dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs kyi khyad par gyi yon tan yongs su brjod pa'i le'u'o// // de nas tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa
31b5: gcig tu gzar nas pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su la mo sbyar btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das chos kyi rnam grangs 'di ni
31b6: zab lags so/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo de de bzhin te/ gzugs zab pa'i phyir zab po// tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa zab pa'i phyir zab bo// stong pa nyid zab pa'o
31b7: phyir zab po/ / nam mkha' zab pa'i phyir zab bo// kun dga' bos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das bdag gis chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong de bzhin gshegs pa las mngon du thos na chos kyi rnam grangs 'di lta bu ni/
31b8: nam yang ma thos so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ chos kyi rnam grangs 'di ni shin du thos par bya dka' ba yin no// kun dga' bos gsol pa/ slad ma'i tshe slad ma'i dus lnga brgya tha ma la dam pa'i tshes nub pa'i
32a1: dus kyi tshesems can mang po dag la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bgyid par 'gyur bar bcom ldan 'das kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di byin gyis brlab du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo ngas chos
32a2: kyi rnam grangs 'di byin gyis brlabs zin te/ de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa ngas chos smra ba de dag kyang byin gyis brlabs so// kun dga' bo gang la la zhig chos kyi rnam grangs 'di yi ger 'dri ba de ni mig na bar mi 'gyur
32a3: ljon par mi 'gyur/ snu na bar mi 'gyur/ so na bar mi 'gyur/ lag pa dang rkang pa na bar mi 'gyur/ klad pa na bar mi 'gyur/ rna ba na bar mi 'gyur/ lus dman par mi 'gyur/ lus dri mi zhim par mi 'gyur/ pha rol gyi gnod pas
32a4: 'chi ba'i dus byed par mi 'gyur ro/ / de la mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad srung bar 'gyur ro// 'di nas shi 'phos nas kyang de spros pa thams cad yongs su spangs nas bde 'gro mtho ris kyi 'jig rten du lha rnams kyi nang du skye bar/
32a5: 'gyur ro// kun dga' bos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das chos 'di bshad pa'i tshe bdud par chad mi bgyid pa'i rgyu gang lags/ rkyen gang lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo bdud thams cad chos kyi
32a6: rnam grangs 'di la bar chad byed mi nus te/ kun dga' bo gang gi tshe bdud sdig can 'di snyam du bdag dkon mchog ta la la'i gzungs 'chad pa la bar chad byed du 'gro'o// snyam pa'i sems bskyed pa de'i tshe/ bdud sdig can gyi
32a7: rang gi khyim kun du 'bar ba mthong ste/ kun dga' bo chos kyi rnam grangs 'di de ltar zab po// kun dga' bos phyogs gang na chos kyi rnam grangs 'di spyod pa'i sa phyogs de mchod rten du 'gyur// phyag bya ba'i 'os su yang 'gyur
32a8: ro/ / kun dga' bos gsol pa/ gal te de bzhin gshegs pa sa phyogs gang na bzhugs pa'i sa phyogs de nyid na chos kyi rnam grangs 'di yang gnas par 'gyur la/ bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la blta ba'i slad du ma
32b1: shing / mchis nas kyang sngar de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag bgyis nas slad kyis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la phyag bgyis na nongs pa ci mchis/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo gang gi tshe khyod kyis chos
32b2: kyi rnam grangs 'di lta bu bkol te/ de la phyag 'tshal ba de'i tshe khyod nyes pa dang bcas par 'gyur ro// kun dga' bo gzhan yang da lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi mthu bo// gtso bo dang mchog dang dam pa yin gyi/ kun dga' bo
32b3: ngas sngar chos kyi rnam grangs 'di thos nas phyis byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so/ / kun dga' bos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pas gang las ting nge 'dzin rin po che dkon mchog
32b4: tra la la bstan pa 'di gsan pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i gong na su mchis/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo mi'i 'jig rten dang lha'i 'jig rten dang dri za'i 'jig rten na nga'i gong na su yang med
32b5: de/ 'on kyang byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa na ngas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes thogs pa med pa brtsegs pa'i snying po 'od zer bzang po bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i 'od zer du ma'i lte ba rgyas
32b6: pa las mngon du thos te kun dga' bo bya dka' ba chen po bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma myong nas ngas chos kyi rnam grangs 'di thos te/ de'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa des nga lung bstan to// kun dga' bo de bas na khyod
32b7: kyis sngar chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la phyag bgyis la phyis ngal phyag 'tshal cig/ de nas brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten skyong ba thams cad kyis mgrin gcig tu tshig 'di skad ces smras so// a la la chos
32b8: a la la chos/ chos rnams kyi rnam par 'phrul pa a la la'o// sems can gang dag chos kyi rnam grangs 'di'i ming thos pa de dag kyang phyag bya ba'i 'os yin na/ gang dag 'dzin pa dang klog pa dang kun chub par byed
33a1: kha dang / gzhan dag la yang rgya cher yang dag par rab tu ston pa lta smos kyang ci dgos te/ de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa zhes brjod par bya'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis brgya byin dang tshangs pa
33a2: dang 'jig rten skyong ba de dag la kye grogs po dag khyed kyis tshig 'di legs par smras pa legs so legs so zhes bya ba byin no/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhalanas lcags kyi dbang po byung ste/ snong
33a3: gsum gyi snod chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams ljags kyi dbang pos snang bar byas nas byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / sems can gang dag chos kyi rnam grang sa 'dzi
33a4: mi thos pa de dag ni ji ltar mi nga sras lang gis nyi ma'i snang ba mi mthong ba dang / ji ltar tshong ba thabs mi shes pa dang ji ltar mi dbul po gzhan gyi ngor lta ba dang 'dra ste/ de dag gi don dungs ye 'di byas na ni nas
33a5: sems can rnams chas rin po che'i phung po 'di 'dra ba las ring du mi 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir chos kyi rnam grangs 'di'i ched dang sems can thams cad kyi don du khyod la gsal ba 'deb san rigs kyi bu khyod spro/ denas bamamasu pa shAn bang po sa las langs krigs ga/
33a6: sa pa nas pas mArnams pa'i ljang stsal bcugs te/ com ldan 'das gapa pa de legs sul ma
33a7: l dan sa ga sag
33a8: kun bur btsu g.yas so/ / phrul rab tu 'phrul/ ban tu ba cu 'phral to// sdig rab ldan/ phan rtsa tu ldeg go// 'am / ra kyar chung/ phan d+ha bcur bang po// che mtsham/ rab tu mchag kun
33b1: shAnas gas ng+gA k+sha / g+sa s+yA// gad+hA nga sa sh+tha yAk+Sha yA/ Sh+TA na thamams pa ba ya sa ma rgya a t+ta/
33b2: bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag spro lags so// bde bar gshegs pa bdage slo lags so// bcom ldan 'das khyod ni thams cad mkhyen pa/ sems can thams cad la phan ba
33b3: bzhed pa/ thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa lags kyi steng du bdag ni de bzhin gshegs pa las skyes pa lags na/ ci'i slad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' ltar mi bgyid/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i
33b4: bka' ni bdud rtsi'i bka' lags na/ bdag de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' dang 'gal bar bgyid pa'i mthu bdag la ga la mchis/ bcom ldan 'das bdag gis ni byas pa gzo bar bgyi ba lcags kyi/ byas pa mi
33b5: gzo bar bgyi ba ma lags so/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la le gse zhes bya ba byin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras legs so logs so// khyod ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams
33b6: kyi sras kyi thu bo dang / gtso bo dang / mchog dang dam pa dang phul yin te/ chos kyi rnam grangs 'di khyod la yongs su gtad do// 'di ni nga'i ston pa yin te/ de'i phyir khyod kyis bsrung bar bya'o// dus dus su sti
33b7: sta gyis shig/ rin po che'i snod du chug la brag pa la thogs shig/ phyi ma'i tshe bye ma'i dus na dge slong sdig can de dag la yid ma nyon cig/ rigs kyi bu 'di ni khyed la rjes su bstan pa'o// byang chub sems
33b8: dpa' kun tu bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das rab tu byung ba ci 'dra ba de dag 'byung bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu kha rog de skad ma 'dri shig/ byang chub sems dpa'
34a1: kun du bzang pos gsol pa/ sems can mang po la sman pa bgyid par 'gyur lags na/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad nga gsal/ bde bar gshegs pa bshad du gsol/ bka' stsal pa/ kun du bza
34a2: po bshad kyis nyon cig/ 'khor rgya mtsho lta bu 'di dang 'jam dpal dang spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po grangs med dpag du med pa thams cad yid la byed pa
34a3: gzhan thong la/ phyi ma'i tshe phye ma'i dus na rab tu byung ba ci 'dra ba dag 'byung bar 'gyur ba de dag nyon cig/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// kun du
34a4: bzang po rab tu byung ba dam pa'i chos sun 'byin pa/ khyim la chags pa/ rnyed pa la chags pa/ gtsug lag khang la chags pa/ gnas la chags pa/ lhung bzed dang chos gos la chags pa/ khyim sun par byed pa/ sdig
34a5: pa'i chos kun du spyod pa de dag 'byung ste/ kun du bzang po mi gti mug pa de dag gidon du ngas mdo sde 'di yongs su gtad kyis mdo 'di nub par g+hur ta ri/ de nas phyogs bcu nas lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za
34a6: thams cad lhags te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag kyang thams cad 'dus shing tshogs te/ ji srid 'tsho'i bar dang dam pa'i chos ji srid gnas kyi bar du chos
34a7: kyi rnam grangs 'di yongs su bsnang bar bgyi'o/ / chos smra ba'i dge slong de dag la yang yongs su bstang bar bgyi'o// sta stang du bgyi'o// btsun par bgyi'o// rim gror bgyi'o// mchod par bgyi'o// brjed par
34a8: bgyi'o/ / gsol bar bgyi'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa gnyis po de dag la yang dag par skul ba'i tshigs
34b1: su bcad pa 'dir dgagasangs so/ / yon tan pha rol phyin pa de dag gi/ yon tan kun bshad thams cad nga las nyon// / nga rgyal rgyags dang bag med spang byos la// dga' zhing mgu ba'i yid kyis mnyan par
34b2: gyis/ / ma ga d+hA 'dir shing dbang byang chub drung // rang byung me yi seng ge bzhugs shes grag/ ting 'dzin rnam par thar pa mchog la gnas// shing rgyal chen po de yi drung na bzhugs// phyogs bcu'i zhing rdul snya/
34b3: dang de thabs gcig/ skyes bu dam pa rnams kyis dpa' bo bskor// sangs rgyas phal chen zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin// ting nge 'dzin de la mo yi dbang po gnas// mi dbang de ni snyoms par zhugs rtogs nas//
34b4: 'jam dpal gzhon nu shar gyi phyogs logs nas// sangs rgyas zhing bcu rdul snyed lhan cig tu// skyes bu dam pa rnams dang rgyal drung 'ongs// de bzhin sbyar te phyogs bcu'i zhing kun nas// sangs rgyas sras po
34b5: dpal zhes bya ba kun/ / phyogs bcu'i zhing rdul snyed dang lhan cig tu// skyes bu dam pa rnams dang lhags par gyur// der 'dus gyur nas 'jig rten pan 'dod pa// 'jam dpal grags pa mtha' yas ldan
34b6: rnams la/ / sems can dam pa bzang po'i dpal gyis dris// sangs rgyas sras kyi spyod gang yon tan ci// de nas sems dpa' 'jam dpal zhes bya ba// rnyog pa med pas byang chub yon tan dang // bde yangs
34b7: yon tan ldan gyi spyod yul gtsang / / sems can dam pa bzang po'i dpal la dris// sangs rgyas sras po rnams kyi spyod yul gtsang // rgyal bas brten pa bdag gis 'dir smras kyis// khyod kyang sangs rgyas sras
34b8: na yon tan dang / / spyod pa gang dag yin pa brjod par gyis// bzang po'i dpal gyis smras pa rgyal sras nyon// yon tan mtha' yas ldan de'i yon tan las// dpe tshul cung zad tsam zhig brjod pa // rgya mtsho'i
35a1: thigs pa bzhin du shin du chung / / byang chub gzhir gyur pa yi rang byung sems// thog ma nyid du bskyed pa gang yin pa// de yi yon tan bsngags pa mtha' yas te// mtshungs med kyis kyang yongs su brda na
35a2: spyod/ / pha rol phyin dang sa yi yon tan rnams// bskal pa mang por spyad pa ci smos te// phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba kun gyis de dag ge// yon tan chu bo zad par mdzad mi spyod// yon tan mtha' yas rnams kyi yon tan
35a3: las/ dpe tshul cung zad tsam zhig brjod bya ste// mkha' la bya rjes 'dra bar chung ba dang // sa chen rnams las rdul phran gcig dang mtshungs// byang chub yon tan gnas kyi sems skye ba// rgyu med ma yin gyi nam yin gyi/
35a4: rgyal dang rgyal ba'i chos dang dge 'dun la// dad dang dad pa bskyed nas sems skye ste// de ni 'dod dang longs spyod rgyal srid dang // bdag la bde dang snyan dang grags phyir min// 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal ma lus zhi bya'i phyir//
35a5: 'jig rten phan pa byed pa'i sems skye'o// rtag tu sems can phan par bya phyir dang // zhing rnams spyad dang sangs rgyas mchod pa dang // chos yongs gzung dang sangs rgyas byang chub dang // ye shes rnam par sbyang phyir
35a6: sems de skye/ / rgyal ba kun dang chos dang de bzhin du// 'phags pa'i tshogs la rtag du dad pa dang // dang zhing mos dang gus par rab bskyed nas// bla ma gus par mchod phyir sems de skye// rgyal dang rgyal ba'i chos la
35a7: dadadu gyur cing / / sangs rgyas sras kyi spyod la dad byed la// byang chub bla na med la dad gyur nas// skyes bu chen po rnams kyi sems skye'o// dad pa'i stobs kyis mi bdag gyur pa rnams// pas bsam las rgya chen mchod ngam mchod byas
35a8: mtsho bye zhi/ / chos da debazhin mi phyed dge 'dun la// bsam yas mchod pas mchod nas sems skye'o// dang pa sngon 'dren ma ltar spyod pa ste// yon tan thams cad srung zhing 'phel bar byed// dogs pasel cing chu bo rnams
35b1: las snol/ / dad pa bde ba'i grong khyer mtshon pa yin// dad pa rnyog pa med cing sems dang byed// dargyal spong zhing gus pa'i rtsa ba yin// dad pa gter dang nor dang rkang pa'i mchog/ lag pa bzhin du dge srung rtsa ba yin/
35b2: dad pa yongs su gtod la dga' bar byed// dad pa rgyal ba'i chos la rab dga' skyed// dad pa yon tan ye shes khyad par byed// sangs rgyas go 'phang ston cing thob par byed// dbang po rno zhing rab tu gsal bar
35b3: byed/ dngad pa'i stobs la gzhan gyis mi rdzi zhing // nyon mongs rnam par sel ba'i gzhi rten yin// dad pa rang byung yon tan rnams kyang tshol// dad pa chags pa'i sgo la chags pa med// mi la spangs shing
35b4: dal ba'i mchog gcig yin/ / dad pa bdud kyi lam las 'da' byed cing // thar pa'i lam mchog ston par byed pa yin// yon tan zhing gi sa bon ma rul ba/ dad pa byang chub zhing ni rnam par skyed// ye shes
35b5: khyad par yon tan 'phel bar byed/ / ngang pa rgyal ba thams cad ston pa yin// dad pas mos pa'i khyad par dga' rnams kyi// de la spyod pa rim gyis brjod par bya// 'di 'dra'i chos ni 'jig rten rab dkon te// rgya mtsho'i nang
35b6: na rin chen rgyal po bzhin/ / gang dag rtag tu sangs rgyas dang gus pa// de dag tshul khrims bslab pa yongs mi 'dor// gang dag tshul khrims bslab pa mi 'dor ba// yon tan ldan de yon tan ldan pas bstod// tshul khrims
35b7: byang chub sems ston byed pa ste/ / slob pa'i sa yi yon tan rnams la sbyor// tshul khrims bslab pa 'dor bar mi byed pa// de dag rgyal bas bsngags pa'i 'os su 'gyur// gang dag rtag tu sangs rgyas dang gus pa// de dag rgyal
35b8: la mchod pa rgya chen byed/ / gang dag rgyal la mchod pa che byed pa// de dag sangs rgyas dad pa bsam mi khyab// gang dag rtag tu chos la dang gus pa// de dag rgyal ba'i chos nyan ngoms pa med// gang dag rgyal ba'i chos nyan mi ngoms
36a1: pa/ / de dag chos la mos pa bsam mi khyab// gang dag rtag tu dge 'dun dang gus pa// de dag mi ldog dge 'dun dad pa yin// gang dag mi ldog dge 'dun rab dad pa// de dag dad pa'i stobs kyis mi ldog 'gyur// gang dag dad ba'i
36a2: stobs kyis mi ldog pa/ / de dag dbang po rno zhing rab tu gsal// gang dag dbang po rno zhing rab gsal ba// de dag sdig pa'i grogs po rnam par spangs// gang dag sdig pa'i grogs po rnam spangs pa// de dag chos lngar grogs kyis yongs
36a3: su gzung / / gang dag chos ldan grogs kyis yongs gzung ba// de dag dge ba rgya chen sogs par byed// gang dag dge ba rgya chen sogs byed pa// bdag nyid chen po de dag chu stobs ldan// bdag nyid chen po chu stobs gang ldan pa// de dag
36a4: mos pa'i khyad par rgya chen 'gyur/ / gang dag mos pa'i khyad par rgya che ba// de dag rgyal ba kun gyis rtag byin brlabs// gang dag rgyal ba kun gyis byin brlabs pa// de dag byang chub don du sems kyang skye// gang dag byang chub don du sems
36a5: skye ba/ de dag drang srong chen po'i yon tan brtson// drang srong chen po'i yon tan gar brtson pa// de ga rigs mtho sangs rgyas rigs su ste// nga dag rig sa ma thos ngas rgyas rigs skyes pa// dag mnyam zhing skyo dang mi skyor grangs// mnyam zhe de sbyor dang mi sbyor gang spangs pa// de dag
36a6: dad dang bsam pa rnam par dag/ gang dag dad dang bsam pa rnam dag pa// de dag lhag pa'i bsam pa dam pa mchag/ gang dag lhag bsam dam pa mchog ldan pa// de dag rtag tu pha rol phyin pa spyod// gang dag rtag tu pha rol phyin spyod pa//
36a7: de dag theg pa chen po 'di la zhugs// gang dag theg pa chen po 'dir zhugs pa// de dag sangs rgyas rnams la sgrub pas mchod// gang dag sgrub pas sangs rgyas mchod byed pa// de dag sangs rgyas rjes su dran mi byed// gang dag sangs rgyas//
36a8: rjes dran mi phyed pa// de dag rtag tu sangs rgyas bsam yas mthong // gang dag sangs rgyas bsam yas rtag mthong ba// de la nam yang sangs rgyas mi bzhugs min// gang dag nam yang sangs rgyas mi bzhugs min// de dag par
36b1: skabs chos las nyams mi 'gyur/ / gang dag par skabs chos las mi nyams pa// de dag spobs pa sgrib pa med par 'gyur// gang dag spobs pa sgrib pa med gyur pa// de dag chos rab ston pa mtha' yas 'gyur// gang dag chos rab ston//
36b2: pa mtha' yas pa// de dag 'gro la byams shing phan par 'dod// gang dag 'gro la nyams shing phan 'dod pa// de dag snying rje chen po'i rtsa ba brtan// gang dag snying rje chen po'i rtse brtan pa// de dag tshes dga' dga' ba'i dbang por 'gyur// gang dag
36b3: chos dga' dga' ba'i dbang po can/ / de dag 'dus byas skyon gyis yal bar bar// gang dag 'dus byas skyon gyis yal bor ba// de dag nga rgyal rgyags med pag med min// gang dag nga rgyal rgyags med pag med min// de dag rtag tu
36b4: bdag dang gzhan don brtson/ / gang dag rtag du bdag gzhan don brtson pa// de dag 'khor bar yongs su skyo ba med// gang dag 'khro bar yongs su ma skyo ba// de dag rtun pa dam pa mchog dang ldan// gang dag rtun pa dam pa mchog ldan pa// de dag
36b5: mngon shes rnam par dag pa skyes/ / gang dag mngon shes rnam par dag skyes pa// de dag 'gro ba'i spyod pa mang po rtogs// gang dag 'gro ba'i spyod pa mar rtogs pa// de dag 'gro ba yongs su smin byed mkhas// 'gro ba yongs su smin byed gang/
36b6: mkhas pa// de dag 'gro ba sdud shes cho ga mkhas// 'gro ba sdud shes tshegasu mkhas pa// de dag bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi la brtson// gang dag bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhir brtson pa// de dag 'gro ba'i don ni mtha' yas byed// gang dag 'gro don
36b7: mtha' yas bye gyur pa/ / de dag shes rab thabs la rten pa yin// gang dag shes rab thabs la rten gyur pa// dpa' bo de dag bla med la mal gnas// dpa' bo gang dag bla me la ma gnas pa// de dag bdud dpung rnams kyis yongs mi tshug//
36b8: gang dag bdud dpung rnams kyis mi tshugs pa// de dag bdud kyi lam las rab tu 'das// gang dag bdu dkyilam las rab 'das pa// de dag mi ldogs ni rjes su 'thob// gang dag mi ldogs ni thob gyur pa// de dag mi skye bzod pa thob
37a1: pa yin/ / gang dag mi skye bzod pa thob gyur pa// 'jig rten sgron de rgyal bas lung bstan to// 'jig rten sgron gang rgyal bas lung bstan pa// de dag rgyal ba kun dang mngon sum gnas// rgyal ba kun dang mngon sum su
37a2: gnas pa/ / de dag rgyal gsang rnam 'phrul cho ga mkhas// rgyal gsang rnam 'phrul cho ga su mkhas pa// de dag rgyal ba kun gyis dgongs pa yin// gang dag rgyal ba kun gyis dgongs gyur pa// de dag yon tan kun gyis legs par
37a3: brgyan/ / gang dag yon tan kun gyis legs brgyan pa// de dag bsod nams dam pas lus kyang sbyangs// bsod nams mchog gis gang lus rnam sbyangs pa// de dag gser gyi ri bo 'dra bar 'bar// gser gyi ri bo 'dra bar su
37a4: 'bar ba/ / de dag sum bcu rtsa gnyis mtshan rnams rdzogs// gang dag sum bcu rtsa gnyis mtshan rdzogs pa// de dag lus rnams dpe byad bzang pos spras// gang dag lus rnams dpe byad bzang spras pa// de dag lus kyi 'od
37a5: ni mtha' yas so/ / gang dag lus kyi 'od ni mtha' yas pa// de dag 'od zer bkod pa bsam mi khyab// gang dag 'od bkod bsam gyis mi khyab pa// de dag 'od las pad ma rnams kyang 'byung // gang dag 'od las pad ma rnams
37a6: byung ba/ / de dag rgyal gzugs pad ma'i gdan 'khod pa// phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten dag tu ston byed cing // don yod gnas pa sems can 'dul bar byed// gang dag rgyal gzugs pad ma'i gdan 'khod par// phyogs bcu'i
37a7: 'jig rten dag tu ston byed cing / / don yod gnas pa sems can 'dul byed pa// de dag mngon shes rnam 'phrul mtha' yas so// gang dag mngon shes rnam 'phrul mtha' yas pa// de dag bsam gyis mi khyab zhid rgyu zhing //
37a8: bsam gyis mi khyab chos rnams ston par byed// sems can bsam gyis mi khyab tshim par byed// gang dag bsam gyis mi khyab chos ston cing // sems can bsam gyis mi khyab tshim byed pa// de dag so so rigs shes
37b1: stobs rnams kyis/ / bsam pa ji bzhin 'jig rten sems can 'dul// de dag rtag tu lus dang ngag dang yid// ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing rjes su 'brang // gang dag rtag tu lus dang ngag dang yid// ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing
37b2: rjes 'brang ba/ / de dag smon lam stobs kyis ci 'dod par// sems can rgyud na gzugs ni ston par byed// gang dag smon lam stobs kyis ci 'dod par// sems can rgyud na gzugs ni ston byed pa// de dag tshig rnams brjod
37b3: par byed pa'i tshe/ / dbyangs kyi yan lag bsam yas sgra 'byung ngo // gang dag tshig rnams brjod par byed pa'i tshe// dbyangs kyi yan lag bsam yas sgra 'byung ba// de dag 'gro ba ma lus kun gyi sems// skad cig gcig la sems/
37b4: kyis rnam par shes// gang dag 'gro ba ma lus kun gyi sems// skad cig gcig la sems kyis rnam shes pa// de dag nam yang mi 'chi skye mi 'gyur// nyon mongs rgyu ba 'ang 'byung bar 'gyur ba min// gang dag nam yang mi
37b5: 'chi mi skye zhing / / nyon mongs rgyu ba'ang 'byung bar mi 'gyur ba// de dag yon tan chos nyid ye shes lus// chos kyis rab tu phye bas 'jig rten rgyu// gang dag yon tan chos nyid ye shes lus// chos kyis rab bye 'jig rten
37b6: klu byed pa/ / de dag sa bcu rnams dang dbang bcu dang // pha rol phyin dang rnam thar mchog la gnas// gang dag sa bcu rnams dang dbang bcu dang // pha rol byin dang rnam thar mchog gnas pa// de dag dbang bskur bkod dang rnam 'phrul
37b7: dang / / ting 'dzin mchog la gnas pa rjes su 'thob// gang dag dbang bskur bkod dang rnam 'phrul dang // ting 'dzin mchog la gnas pa rjes thob pa// de dag phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba thams cad las// dbang bskur thams
37b8: cad ma lus nod par byed/ / gang dag phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba thams cad las// dbang bskur thams cad ma lus nod byed pa// de dag spyi bor phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyis// phyag mthil bdud rtsi can gyis dbang bskur te//
38a1: gang dag spyi bor phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyis// phyag mthil bdud rtsi can gyis dbang bskur ba// mthu brtan de dag nam mkha' lta bur ni// ma lus khyab byas phyogs rnams kun du gnas// mthu brtan gang dag
38a2: nam mkha' lta bur ni/ / ma lus khyab byas phyogs rnams kun gnas pa// mtshungs med de dag spyod yul lhar bcas kyi// 'jig rten rnams kyis shes par yongs mi nus// mtshungs med gang dag spyod yul lhar bcas
38a3: kyi/ / 'jig rten rnams kyis shes par mi nus pa// de dag rkun pa kun dang mthong ba dang // ming thos pa dang spobs pa don yod do// gang dag rtun pa kun dang mthong ba dang // ming thos pa dang spobs pa don yod pa// skyes chen
38a4: de dag sbyin pa sbyin byed kyi/ / sbyin pa thams cad don yod 'gyur ba yin// skyes bu dam pa de dag rnams kyi mthus// chos kyang gnas shing byams pa nyams mi 'gyur// dge ba'i las rnams rab tu spyod 'gyur te// dkon
38a5: mchog mthu yang dam pa mchog tu 'gyur/ / rdo rje mkhregs pa'i rin chen tshogs yod pa// de yi mthu yis rgya mtshor rin chen rnams// mi zad mi 'grib 'phel bar mi 'gyur te// de bzhin yon tan mtha' yas yon tan
38a6: chu/ gang na sangs rgyas med pa'i zhing gyur pa// de ni byang chub rnam par sangs rgyas ston// phyogs rnams gang na chos kyang med gyur pa// phyogs der chos kyi gter ni ston par byed// de dag rtog med rnam par mi rtog cing
38a7: de dag lhun gyis grub par phyogs kun du/ / zla ba lta bur snang bar rab ston cing // thabs stong dag gis sems can 'dul bar byed// de dag skad cig re la phyogs bcu yi// 'jig rten kun du byang chub sangs rgyas
38a8: ston/ / 'khor lo bskor dang mya ngan las 'das zhing // ring bsrel rab tu rgyas pa'ang dpa' bo ston// mkhas pa de dag nyan thos rang rgyal sa// sangs rgyas bkod pa rnam 'phrul mtha' yas pa// bskal pa bsam
38b1: mi khyam par ston nung pa/ / theg gsum sgonas sems can 'dral bar byed// mos pa kun gyi bsgrub pa shes pa rnams// khye'u dang bu mo bud med lus rnams dang // lha mi lA min k+Sha dang gnod sbyin dang // sbrul
38b2: bum lho 'phye chen po'i gzugs rnams ston/ / rgya mtsho'i phyag rgya'i ting nge 'dzin gyi sgos// dpa' bo de dag 'gro ba'i gzugs spyod dang // rtags dang spyod dang sgra skad 'jug pa dang // ji snyed thams cad ma lus ston
38b3: par byed/ de dag zhing bkod bsam gyis mi khyab pas// phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba kun la mchod par byed// gang dag zhing bkod bsam gyis mi khyab pas// phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba kun la mchod byed pa// de dag 'od
38b4: zer bkod pa bsam yas shing / / sems can 'grel pa'o ye shes mtha' yas so// gang dag 'od zer bkod pa bsam yas shing // sems can 'grel ba'i ye shes bsam yas pa// de dag lus dang ngag gi
38b5: rnam 'phrul dang / / yid kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam mi khyab// gang dag lus dang ngag gi rnam 'phrul dang // yid kyi rnam 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ de dag sbyin dang tshul khrims rnam 'phrul dang // bzod dang brtson/
38b6: 'grus rnam 'phrul pasam mi khyab// gang dag sbyin dang tshul khrims rnam 'phrul dang / bzod brtson rnam 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa// de dag sangs rgyas phal chen ting 'dzin sgos// bsam gtan rnam par 'phrul
38b7: dang shes rab dang / / thabs dang mngon shes rnam 'phrul bsam mi khyab// yon tan kun gyi rnam 'phrul mtha' yang yas// de dag phra rab rdul 'jug ting nge 'dzin// rdul rnams kun la mngon par sgrub byed cing //
38b8: rdul gcig steng na zhing rnams bsam mi khyab// ston par byed kyang rdul la 'phel ba med// rdul de'i steng na sangs rgyas bcas zhing dang // sangs rgyas med pa'i zhing yang kha cig ston// nyon mongs rnam dag
39a1: dog pa kha cig dang / / yangs shing phra dang che ba'i zhing yang ston// zhing rnams la la 'dzag dang 'chags pa dang // la la spyi'u tshugs gyur dang 'thun pa dang // la la snrel zhi smig rgyu lta bu dang // la la mig 'phrul /
39a2: bu gyur pa rnams// ji ltar rdul gcig steng du stor byed pa// de bzhin rdul rnams ma lus kun la ston// drang srong ting 'dzin rnam 'phrul 'di 'dra ste// grags pa mtha' yas rnam thar 'di 'dra'o// de dag rgyal mchod nam 'phrul
39a3: ting nge 'dzin/ / rgyal ba kun la mngon par sgrub byed cing // lag pa'i mthil du stong gsum rgyas bkang ste// skyes bu chen po rnams la mchod pa byed// phyogs bcu dag na me tog phreng ba dang // spos byug rin chen rin chen ji snyed
39a4: pa/ / de dag byang chub shing drung bzhugs pa yi// rgyal rnams mchod phyir lag pa'i mthil nas 'byin// gos dang phye ma rin chen ji snyed dang // rgyal mtshan ba dan gdugs mchog sna tshogs dang // gser gyis brgyan pa'i rin
39a5: chen bla re rnams/ / de dag lag pa'i mthil nas char du 'bebs// phyogs bcu dag na yo byad mtha' yas gang // drang srong chen po rnams la mchod 'os pa// de dag lag pa'i mthil nas char 'bebs shing // byang chub shing
39a6: drung bzhugs pa'i rgyal ba mchod/ / phyogs rnams dag na rol mo ji snyed pa// rnga dang rdza rnga sgra snyan pi bang dang // sil snyan sgra dang sgra chen gling bu rnams// de dag lag pa'i mthil nas rab tu sgrogs// phyogs bcu kun gyi dpe
39a7: rna med rnams kyi/ / yang dag yon tan bsngags pa sna tshogs dang // bstod pa'i tshig bcad sgrub pa sna tshogs pa// de dag lag 'i e nas rab tu sngogs// 'od zer gang dag las dges yongs bsags pa// lag pa
39a8: g.yas nas yongs su 'byed byed cing / / spos chus rgyal ba'i zhing rnams thams cad du// 'bebs shing 'jig rten sgron ma rnams la mchod// 'od zer bkod dang ldan pa mdzes pa'i 'od// pad ma'i rgyan phreng bsam
39b1: yas rab 'phyang / / pad ma mtshan rab gzugs can du ma dag/ lag nas rgyal ba rnams la mchod par byed// me tog phal chen me tog bla re dang // me tog bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// me tog sna tshogs
39b2: kun du bkram byas shing / / bdag nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod// bdug pa phal chen bdug pa'i bla re dang // bdug pa bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// bdug pa sna tshogs kun du bkram byas shing // bdag nyid chen po de
39b3: dag rgyal ba mchod/ / phal chen spos dang spos kyi bla re dang // spos kyis bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// sna tshogs spros rnams kun du bkram byas shing // bdag nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod// phreng ba phal chen phreng
39b4: pa'i bla re dang / / phreng ba bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// phreng ba sna tshogs kun du bkram byas shing // bdag nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod// phye ma phal chen phye ma'i bla re dang // phye ma bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// phye
39b5: ma sna tshogs kun du bkram byas shing / / bdag nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod// na bza' phal chen na bza'i bla re dang // na bza' bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// na bza' sna tshogs kun du bkram byas shing // bdag
39b6: nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod/ / phal chen gdugs dang gdugs kyi bla re dang // gdugs kyi bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// sna tshogs gdugs rnams kun du bkram byas shing // bdag nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod
39b7: rin chen phal chen rin chen bla re dang / / rin chen bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// rin chen sna tshogs kun du bkram byas shing // bdag nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod// pad ma phal chen pad ma'i bla re dang // pad ma bkod pa'i
39b8: 'od zer rab bkye ste/ / pad ma sna tshogs kun du bkram byas shing // bdag nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod// rgyan phreng phal chen rgyan phreng bla re dang // rgyan phreng bkod pa'i 'od zer rab bkye ste// rgyan phreng sna tshogs kun du bkram
40a1: byas shang / / bdag nyid chen po de dag rgyal ba mchod// rgyal mtshan mchog bkod 'od zer rab bkye zhing // dag rgyal mtshan dkar dmar ser po dang // sngo dang rgyal mtshan bkod pa sna tshogs pa// du mas rgyal ba'i zhing
40a2: rnams rgyan par byed/ / nor bu'i dra ba sna tshogs bkod pa'i gdugs// dar gyi lnga ldi ba dan rab sbyangs shing // dril g.yar dra ba rgyal ba'i gsung sgrogs pa// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de dag 'dzin// lag pa'i mthil
40a3: nas mchod pa mtha' yas rnams/ / rgyal ba gcig la de dag byed pa ltar// rgyal ba ma lus kun la'ang de bzhin te// drang srong ting 'dzin rnam 'phrul de 'dra'o// de dag 'gro bsrung ba'i ye shes kyis// rnam par 'phrul dang
40a4: ting 'dzin mchog bsgrubs shing / / bya ba dag dang bsnyen bkur kun gyi sgo// thabs stong dag gis sems can 'dul bar byed// kha cig de bzhin gshegs pa mchod sgo dang // sbyin pa bsam gyis mi khyab gtong sgo dang // sbyangs
40a5: pa'i yon tan tshul khrims kun sgo dang / / bzod pa mi zad mi 'khrugs sgo dag dang // kha cig brdul zhugs dka' thub brtson sgo dang // bsam gtan rab tu zhi bar gnas sgo dang // don la rnam des shes rab sgo rnams dang // smad
40a6: pa kun tha thabs kyi sgo dag dang / / tshangs pa'i gnas pa dag dang mngon shes s+ho// bsdu ba'i dngos po phan par 'dod sgo dang // bsod nams bsags dang ye shes sgo dag dang // bden dang rten dang rnam thar sgo dag dang //
40a7: kha cig stobs dang dbang po lam sgo dang // nyan thos theg pas rnam par grol sgo dang // rkyen gyi theg pas rnam par dag sgo dang // theg pa mchog gi rnam par 'phrul sgo dang // kha cig mi rtag nyid dang sdug bsngal sgo// kha cig/
40a8: bdag med srog med sgo dag dang // mi sdug 'du shes 'dod chags bral sgo dang // zhi 'gog ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo yis 'dul// 'gro ba'i spyod pa'i sgo rnams ji snyed pa// de snyed chos kyi sgo la rab zhugs te// de dag kun
40b1: du rnamatharasgo dag nas/ / bsam pa ji bzhin 'jig rten sems can 'dul// gang dag kun du rnamathar sgo dag nas// bsams bzhin 'jig rten sems can 'dul byed pa// de dag sus kyang mtshanam
40b2: gzung mi nus/ / ting 'dzin rnam par 'phrul ba de 'dra'o// de dag dga' ba bkod pa'i ting 'dzin mchog/ 'gro ba thams cad yongs smin 'thun byed pa// dga' ba de spro ba rab dga' kun ldan pas// bsams pa bstan nas sems
40b3: can 'dul bar byed/ / gang du lo nyes 'jig rten yo byad gang // bde byed thams cad rab tu dkon gyur pa// der ni kun gyis bsams bzhin bya ba yin// sbyin pa sbyin zhing 'gro ba'i don rnams byed// de dag zas skam mchog dang
40b4: ro mchog dang / / gos dang bgo ba rin chen sna tshogs dang // rgyal srid nor dang bdag phangs yongs gtong bas// sbyin la mos pa'i 'gro ba 'dul bar byed// brtan pa de dag mtshan mchog lus spras shing // gos dang rgyan mchog
40b5: bgos shing brgyan byas te/ / phreng bas spud cing spos kyis bskus pa yi// gzugs rnams bstan pas sems can 'dul bar byed// mthong nas dga' tshim rab tu dga' rnams la// blo mchog de dag gzugs mchog gzugs
40b6: bzang ba/ / gzugs kyi dam pa yongs su ston byed cing // gzugs la mos pa'i sems can 'dul bar byed// de dag ka la bing ka'i sgra snyan dang // khu byug kun la dang pa'i sgra skad dang // rnga dang tshangs dang mi 'am ci yi smras//
40b7: mos pa kun la de bzhin chos kyang ston// stong phrag brgyad bcu rtsa bzhi gang yin pas// rgyal ba gang dag 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa'i// chos kyi bye brag sgo mo de dag gis// bsam pa ji bzhin 'jig rten sems can 'dul//
40b8: de dag bde dang sdug bsngal grags kyang byed// don dang gnod pa'i grogs kyang de bzhin byed// bya ba kun la grogs su 'gyur byas shing // grogs kyi sgo nas sems can 'dul bar byed// sdug bsngal gnod pa 'dus byas skyon/
41a1: zin pas// grogs kyi don du de dag bzod byed cing // 'gro ba kun la phan don pa de dod du// de dag grogs don gnod pa dang du len// gang na mngon byung med cing chos med de// dgon par 'gro nga thang pa mid dgas pa/ de nicis
41a2: zi 'byor bar bsungs te/ / zhi ba'i yid kyis gnas med mngon par 'byung // de dag zhim dang 'bying dang sbed pa'i gnas// 'gro ba thams cid yongs su grol ba'i rlung // 'ad pa dga' ba kun la mi gnas pa pa mas
41a3: bar byung zhing thar parab tu brjod/ / de dag spyod pa brnyarnams rjod byed cing // skyes chen rnams kyi chos spyod gang yin dang // drang srong rnams kyi spyod kun ma lus par// yongs su brjod cing 'gro ba din rnams byed// gang na
41a4: sems can dpag med che ldan zhing / / bde dang ldan la nyon mongs chung yod pa/ der ni rga bas nyen cing nad bu can// bdag la dbang med 'tsho ba'i dbang gyur ston// 'dod chags 'bar zhing zhe sdang rab 'bar la// 'jig
41a5: rten gti mug me chen rab 'bar zhing / / rga dang na dang 'chi ba rab 'bar ba'i// 'jig rten bstan nas sems can 'dul bar byed// de dag sangs rgyas stobs bcu brtson bzhi dang // chos kyi khyad par brtsa brgyad rnams kyis
41a6: kyang / / sangs rgyas che ba'i bdag nyid rjod byed cing // sangs rgyas yon tan rnams kyis 'gro don byed// de dag kun brjod rdzu 'phrul rjes bstan pas// gzugs kyi byin rlabs stobs kyis thams cad du// de bzhin gshegs pa'i
41a7: rdzu 'phrul ston byed cing / / rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul pas sems can 'dul// de dag thabs tshul rnam pa sna tshogs kyis// 'jig rten rgyu zhing 'gro ba'i don rnams byed// 'jig rten mi chags chu la pad ma bzhin// dga' zhing
41a8: dade par byed la rnam par hU~M/ / dadag stan dang sa mkhan rgyal snyan dgas sbyor// gang sa na rnam khan gyi dang rom po mkhan// bzhig sadzes rgyan phreng thogs shing gar byed da/ sgra ma mkhan po gzugs pazang ldan
41b1: du ston/ / grong pa grong dpon kha lo skur bar 'gyur// de bzhin ded dpon tshong dpon khyim bdag 'gyur// rgyal po blon po bdun don pho nya dang // sman pa 'jig rten bstan bcos cho ga mkhan// de dag dgon par ljongs shing chen por
41b2: 'jur/ / sman dang rin chen mi zad gtor rnams dang // yid bzhin nor bu 'dod 'byin sdong po dang // lam gol dong ba rnams la lam ston 'gyur// 'jig rten byung nas mi ring shes gyur cing // sems can las kyi tshul
41b3: rnams mi shes pa/ / de dag kun la rlos chos chod thabs dang // sna tshogs bzo rnams 'jig rten rjod par byed// 'tshe byed gnod pa med pa'i sbyor bgang // sems can bde byed mkhas pas rab bsngags pa// rigs stobs
41b4: sman dang bstan bcos sna tshogs kun/ / drang srong de dag rnams kyis rab tu brjod// gang la lhar bcas 'jig rten mos 'gyur ba// drang srong spyod mchog dam pa gang yin dang // brtul zhugs dka' spyad dka' thub/
41b5: mchog kun kyang // mkhas pa de dag rnams kyis rab tu brjod// de dag spyod can kun rgyu mu stegs can// gdung ba go ta ma dang mi spar spyod// gcer bu gos med/ lhur len dge sbyong la// mu stegs can gyi slob dpon
41b6: mkhas par ston/ / de dag kun du 'tsho ba'i chos 'dzin dang // bla na yod dang bla na med rnams dang // ral pa ring dang gzhon nu'i brtul zhugs can// de dag tu yang slob dpon 'gyur ba yin// nyi ma'i rjes lta dka' thub
41b7: lnga ldan dang / / khyi dang ba lang brtul zhugs ri dgas spyod// gle'u can dag dang mu stegs sum bcu pa// de dag tu yang de dag slob dpon 'gyur// lha yi shes la 'jug pa dga' rnams dang // mu stegs nya reg yul
41b8: du rgyu rnams su/ / rtsa ba 'bras bu chu spyod gyur nas kyang // bsam yas chos la de dag dam pa mchog/ cog pur 'dug dang gcig pu rgyu ba dang // tshe ram rtsa dang thal bar nyal ba dang // gang dgagatun shing mal can
42a1: gnas pa dang / / de dag tu yang de dag slob dpon 'gyur// phyi rol mu stegs can rnams ji snyed pa// de dag bsam pa mos pa rtogs byas shing // bsnyen dka' mi zad drag shul dka' thub kyis// mu stegs//
42a2: can gyi sdug bsngal spangs par 'dul// 'jig rten lta bas 'khrugs pa shes byas nas// lta ba ngan la gnas pa'i mu stegs can// kun la phra ba'i gzhi dang thabs tshul gyis// de dag rnams la bden pa ston par
42a3: byed/ la lar 'gro lding pa yi sngags kyi gzhi// shin du gsang ba'i gzhi yis den pa ston// la la dag la gsal zhing drang tshig gis// la la dag la lha yi gsang tshig gis// la la dag la yi ge dbye tshig dang // don
42a4: la rnam des rdo rje'i tshig rnams dang / / rgol ba 'dul ba shes pa'i tshig rnams dang // bstan bcos thub med thar pa'i tshig rnams kyis// la la dag la mi skad tshig rnams dang // kun la 'jug pa'i tshi ga nges tshig
42a5: nams kyis/ / la la dag la lha tshig nges tshig dang // klu yi nges tshig gnod sbyin nges tshig gis// la lar srin po 'byung po sha za dang // dri za grul bum lto 'phye che tshig dang // mi ci lha min mkha' lding tshig rnams
42a6: gyis/ / bden pa bstan cing thar bar 'dren par byed// de dag bden dang des tshig tshul shes te// de ltar rgyal ba'i chos rnams ma lus pa'i// chos nyid bsam yas tshig la ma shes pas ston// de dag ting 'dzin rnam//
42a7: 'phrul de 'dra'o// de dag 'gro bde mchog gi tid nge 'dzin// 'gro ba kun la mngon par sgrub byed cing // 'od zer bsam gyis mi khyab rab bkye ste// 'od zer bkye nas sems can 'dul bar byed// mthong nas legs
42a8: pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing / / sems can ji snyed 'od zer de shes pa// de dag mthong legs don med ma yin te// bla na med pa'i ye shes mchog gi rgyu// mi rnams kun la sangs rgyas yongs bstan cing // chos
42b1: kyang yongs stan de la ma bstan cing / / rgyal ba'i sku gzugs mchod rten bstan byas pas// des na mthong legs 'od zer grub par 'gyur// lha yis 'od zer zil gyis gnon pa yi// 'od zer 'od byed ces bya rab
42b2: gtong zhing / / rdul dang mun pa thams cad bsal byas te// 'jig rten phan pa'i 'od des rab tu snang // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// de dag rgyal ba mchod phyir sgron ma 'dzin// de dag rgyal ba mchod
42b3: phyir skyon bzung bas/ / 'jig rten skyon ma mdzad pa'i rgyal bar 'gyur// 'bru mar mar me mar gyi mA medang // rtsa shing 'dam bu 'od ma'i sgron ma dang // spos dang bcud len rin chen sgron me dag/ rgyal ba rnams la phul nas
42b4: 'ad byed thob/ / sgrol zhes bya ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// de dag sred yangs srid pa'i rgya mtsho las// sems can bsgral ba'i don du go cha gyon// gang dag sred yangs
42b5: srid pa'i rgya mtsho las/ / sems can bsgral ba'i don du go gyon pa// de dag chu bo bzhi la rab tu sgrol// mya ngan med pa bde ba'i grong khyer ston// stegs dang zam pa du ma byas pa dang // chu klung lam la sgrol ba'i gru 'byin
42b6: te/ 'dus byas mun phyung zhib bsngags byas pas// de nas sgrol ba'i 'od zer grub par 'gyur// skom pa sel ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// 'dod pa'i yon tan sgom pa
42b7: rab spangs shing / / chos la mos pa'i ro na don du gnyer// 'dod pa'i yon tan skom pa rab spangs te// chos mos rol don du gnyer gyur pas// bdud rtsi cha rab 'bebs pa'i sangs rgyas 'gyur// 'jig rten sgom
42b8: pa'i srid pa rnam par sal/ / rje dang chu klung khron pa chu dong dang // mtsho rnams byang chub don du byed btsud de// 'dod pa spad cing bsam gtan bsngags byas pas// des na sred pa sel ba bsgrub par gyur// dga' bar byed
43a1: pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing / / sems can gang dag 'od des bskal byas pa// dga' ba rgyas shing byang chub mchog don du// rang byung 'gyur bar bya zhes sems bskyed do// thugs rje ldan pa'i sku gzugs mtshan
43a2: brgyan pa/ / pad ma'i gdan la bzhugs pa rnams byas shing // rtag tu sangs rgyas yon tan rnams brjod pas// des na dga' byed 'od zer grub par gyur// mgu bar byed pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang
43a3: dag 'od des bskul byas pa/ / rtag tu sangs rgyas la ni dga' mgu zhing // chos la dga' mgu dge 'dun dga' mgu'o// de dag rtag tu sangs rgyas dga' mgu zhing // chos la dga' mgu dge 'dun dga' mgu nas// sangs
43a4: rgyas chos dang 'phags pa'i tshogs rnams dang / / rtag tu 'grogs thob bzod pa bla med thob// sangs rgyas rjes dran chos dang tshegs mchog la// sems can mang po bskul cing dran byas te// byang chub sems kyi yon tan
43a5: rab brjod pas/ / des na mgu byed 'od zer grub par 'gyur// bsod nams bsags pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// bla na med pa'i byang chub don gnyer zhing // sbyin pa sna
43a6: tshogs du ma sbyin par byed/ / gtan pa med pa'i mchod sbyin de byed tshe// slong ba rnams kyi bsam pa rdzogs byas te// bsam pa thams cad sbyin pa byin byas pas// bsod nams bsags pa'i 'od zer grub par 'gyur/
43a7: ye shes ldan pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// chos gcig sgo mo nas ni du ma yin// chos kyi sgo rnams yid kyis khong du chud// chos kyi dbye ba sems can 'dzin
43a8: bcud de/ / den la nges pa'i ye shes nas phye zhing // chos kyi tshig den brjod pa byas pas na// des ni ye shes ldan pa'i 'od zer grug// shes rab smon pa'i 'od zer ba gtong zhing // sems can gang dga'o/
43b1: des bsgral byas pas// stong pa bdag med ma skyes ma byung zhing // rang bzhin med pa'i ches la rab tu 'jug/ bdag po med chos stong pa byed med pa// sna ma sdig rgyu rmuzla mtshungs 'dra zhing / tshal sa mtshungs lag na
43b2: brnyan 'dri ba pag/ / bstan pas shes rab smon pa dgrub po// chos kyi nas 'phrul 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// mi zad pazod kyi gzungs na thob gyur nas// de bzhin ga shin
43b3: pa kun gyi mdzod kyang 'dzin/ / chos 'dzin rnams la yongs su phan gdags te// drang srong rnams la chos kyis bsrung byas shing // 'gro ba chos kyis rjes su bsrung byas pas// chos kyi rnam 'phrul 'od zer 'grub
43b4: par 'gyur/ / gtong dang ldan pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can 'dungs pa gang dag des bskul ba// longs spyod mi rtag mi rten shes gyur nas// de dag rtag tu gtong la dga' mos 'gyur// mdul gdul dka'i
43b5: sems can ser sna can/ / nor rnams rmi lam sprin dang 'drar shes nas// dga' ba'i yid kyis sbyin pa spel byas pa// des na stong dang ldan pa'i 'od grub bo// yongs su gdung med 'od zer rab gtong zhing // khrims
43b6: 'chal sems can gang dag des bskul ba/ / tshul khrims rnam par dag la gnas gyur nas// rang byung 'gyur bar bya zhes sems bskyed do// dge ba'i las lam yongs su dag pa dang // tshul khrims la yang sems
43b7: can mar 'dzud cing / / byang chub sems kyang yang dag 'dzin 'jug pas// yongs gdung med pa'i 'od zer de grub po// bzod pa bkod pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // mi bzod sems can gang dag des bskul ba// khro dang
43b8: thab dang nga rgyal yongs spangs shing / / de dag rtag tu bzod mos dga' bar 'gyur// sdig ldan rnams kyi zhes byas bzod byas te// byang chub don du 'khrugs pa ma byas shing // bzod pa'i yon tan rtag du bsngags brjod
44a1: pas/ / des na bzod pa bkod pa de grub bo// sbyangs dang ldan pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // le lo'i sems can gang dag des bskul ba// rigs par brtson pa dkon mchog gsum rnams la// sbyor ba sgo med
44a2: mchod pa byed par 'gyur/ / rigs par brtson pa dkon mchog gsum rnams la// sbyor ba skyo ba med pas mchod byas nas// de dag bdud bzhi'i lam las rab 'das te// byang chub bla med myur du reg par 'gyur// sems can mang/
44a3: po brtson 'grus 'dzin bcug ste// dkon mchog gsum la mchod pa rab byas nas// zad pa'i dus na dam chos yongs gzung bas// des na sbyangs dang ldan pa'i 'od thob po// zhi bar byed pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // rnam
44a4: 'khrugs sems can gang dag des bskul ba/ / de dag chags med sdad med rmongs med cing // rtogs par gyur nas mnyam bzhag sems su 'gyur// sdig pa'i grogs po skyon ldan spyod can dang // 'dre ba yongs su rnam par spangs/
44a5: byas te// dgon par rabazhi bsam gtan bsngags brjod pas// des na zhi bar byed pa'i 'od grub bo// shes rab bkod pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // shes 'chal sems can ji snyed des bskul ba// bden dang rten dang rna ma thar
44a6: tshul rnams dang / / dbang po shes pa rtogs par khongs chud 'gyur// bden dang rten dang rnam thar tshul rnams dang // dbang po shes pa rtogs par khong chud cing // nyi ma sgron ma'i ting 'dzin thob gyur nas// shes rab snang bar mdzad//
44a7: ba'i rgyal bar 'gyur// rgyal srid nor dang bdag pangs yongs btang ste// byang chub don du chos gang gtsal byas pa// shes rab bkod pa'i 'od zer de grub po// sangs rgyas ldan pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag
44a8: 'od des bskul byas pa/ / sangs rgyas stong phrag du ma bsam yas rnams// pad ma dam pa rnams la bzhugs par mthong // sangs rgyas tshe dang sangs rgyas rnam thar dang // sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul mtha' yas brjod byas shing/
44b1: sangs rgyas stobs dang rdzu 'phrul rab brjod pas// de nas sangs rgyas ldan pa'i 'od grub po// mi 'jigs sbyin pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // 'jigs nyen sems can gang dag der reg pa// 'byung po gza' dang gsang brdeg
44b2: bcing ba dang / / nad 'go 'jigs pa kun las thar bar gyur// mi 'jigs sbyin pas sems can gang bskyabs dang // srog chags gsod las bzlog pa byas pa dang // 'jigs pa bskyabs tshal rnams la skyabs
44b3: byas pas/ / mi 'jigs sbyin pa'i 'od zer des grub po// bde ba kun byed 'od zer rab gtong zhing // nad pa na ba gang dag des reg pa// nad pa kun du nad kyi sdug bsngal thar// bsam gtan ting 'dzin bde ba rnams kyang thob//
44b4: nangad gsos 'bras bu sman dang rtsa ba dang // rin chen bcud len spos dang byug pa dang // bu ram sbrang rtsi 'o ma mar dag dang // 'bru mar zas skom byin pas de thob bo// sangs rgyas ston pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing //
44b5: tshe zad tha mar gang dag des bskul ba// sangs rgyas rjes dran sangs rgyas mthong bar 'gyur// de dag shi 'phos sangs rgyas bzhugs zhing 'gro// 'chi ba'i dus su sangs rgyas dran byas te// dga' byed rgyal ba
44b6: sku gzugs bstan byas shing / / 'chi ka ra sang sa rgyas skyabs su gtang brjod pas// sangs rgyas ston pa'i 'od zer de thob bo// chos rab brjod pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas
44b7: pa/ chos nyan klog cing yi ger 'dri bar byed// de dag rtag tu chos la dga' mos 'gyur// chos kyi mu ge byung che chos brjod de// chos tshol rnams kyi bsam pa rdzogs byas shing // 'dun pa bskyed de chos la brtson
44b8: gyis shes/ / brjod pas chos rab brjod pa de thob bo// sangs rgyas sras rnams yongs su bskul ba'i phyir// dbyangs dang ldan pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // 'jig rten gsum na sgra rgud ji snyed pa// kun kyang de
45a1: bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung du thos/ / gas bstod sgra yis drang srong che bstod de// rgyal ba'i gsung sgra don du sil snyan dang // sgra chen dril bu sprin rnams 'gro kun la// rab tu bsgrags pas dbyangs ldan rjo/
45a2: thab bo// 'chi med sbyin pa'i 'od zer rab gtor zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// bag med spyod pa thams cad rab spangs te// yon tan kun la brtson pa nyams su len// 'dus byas rtag tu bde
45a3: ba med pa ste/ / sdug bsngal 'tshe ba du mas yongs su gang // 'gog pa rtag tu bde zhing zhi skyid ces// brjod pas 'chi med sbyin pa de thob po// khyad par ldan pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od
45a4: des bskul byas pa/ / rgyal ba rnams kyi tshul khrims khyad par dang // tid 'dzin khyad par shes rab khyad par thos// thub mtshan rgyal po khrims kyis mchog gyur cing // ting 'dzin mchog dang shes rab mchog rlu ces
45a5: byang chub don du bstod cing bsngags brjod pas/ / des na khyad par ldan pa'i 'od grub po// rin chen bkod pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// rin chen mi zad gter rnams thob/
45a6: zur nas// drang srong chel rin chen dam pas mchod// rgyal dang rgyal ba'i mchod rten rin chen phul// skye bo nyon mongs rin chen rnams kyis bsdus// rgyal ba rnams la rin chen rab phul
45a7: bas/ / rin chen bkod pa'i 'od zer grub par 'gyur// spos rab snang ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sems can gang dag 'od des bskul byas pa// mi la med spros yid 'od tshor gyur nas// sangs rgyas yon tan rnams la
45a8: nges par 'gyur/ / mi dang lha yi spos dang byug pa yis// me yi gtse la mchod par ba byas te// spos las rgyal ba'i gzugs dang mchod rten dag/ byas pas spos rab snang ba de grub bo// sna tshogs bkod pa'i 'od zer ba
45b1: gtong zhing / / rgyal mtshan ba dan gdugs mchog sna tshogs dang // sil snyan bsgrags shing spos kyis gdugs pa yis// pho brang dam pa mdzes byas me tog bkram// sil snyan dag gis rgyal ba rnams bsdu zhing // me
45b2: tog byug pa bdug spos phye ma dang / / rgyal mtshan ba dan gdugs mchog rnams kyis mchod// des na sna tshogs bkod pa grub par gyur// shin du dang byed 'od zer rab gtor zhing // sa rnams lag 'thil bzhin du gnas
45b3: par byed/ / mchod rten drang srong gnas rnams sbyangs byas pas// des na shin du dad pa'i 'od grub po// sprin dang ldan pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // spos kyi char 'bebs sprin rnams kun du gnas// mchod rten 'khor
45b4: sar spos kyi chus btab pas/ / sprin dang ldan pa'i 'od de rab tu thob// ltab lhub bkod pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // gcer bu gos yod brgyan dang ldan par 'gyur// gos dang bgo brgyan phreng ba sna tshogs dag/ sbyin pa byas
45b5: pas lhab lhub bkod pa grub/ / ro mchog ldan pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // bkres pa kha zas ro mchog thob par 'gyur// zas dang sgom dang ro mchog sna tshogs rnams// byin pas ro mchog ldan pa'i 'od grub po// nor
45b6: rnams ston pa'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing / / dbul po dag gis rin chen gter rnams thob// dkon mchog gsum la gtor gzhi mi zad pa// dbul ba byas pas nor ston 'od thob po// mig rnam sbyor ba'i 'od zer rab stong
45b7: zhing / / de tshe long bas sna tshogs gzugs rnams mthong // rgyal ba dag dang rgyal ba'i mchod rten la// mar me phul bas mig spyod 'od zer grub// rna ba rnam spyod 'od zer rab gtong zhing // rna ba nyams pas sgra mang thos par
45b8: 'gyur/ / rgyal ba rnams dang rgyal ba'i mchod rten la// sil snyan phul bas rna skyod 'od zer grub// sna rnam sbyor ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sngon chad mtsher dri zhim tshor bar 'gyur// rgyal ba rnams dang rgyal ba'i mchod rten la/
46a1: spos rab phul bas sna skyong 'od zer grub// lce rnam sbyong ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // sgra snyan yid 'ong rnams kyis sangs rgyas bstod// mi snyan brlang bar smra ba rnam spangs te// 'jam par smras pas lce
46a2: skyong 'od zer grub/ / lus rnam sbyong ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // dbang po nyams pa dbang po ldan par 'gyur// rgyal ba rnams dang rgyal ba'i mchod rten la// lus btud byas pas lus rnam sbyong ba thob// sems rnam
46a3: sbyong ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing / / spros pa thams cad sems dang ldan par gyur// ting 'dzin dbang rjes sems 'gro byas pas na// sems rnam sbyong ba'i 'od zer de grub po// gzugs rnam sbyong ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing //
46a4: mi dbang rnams kyis bsam yas sku mthong ste// sku gzugs ri mo sna tshogs mang po dang // mchod rten brgyan byas gzugs spyod 'od grub po// sgra rnam sbyong ba'i 'od zer rab stong zhing // sgra ni sgra mi stod par rab tu shes//
46a5: rkyen las byung bas brag cha 'dra'o zhes// sgra rnams bstan pas 'od zer de grub po// dri rnam sbyong ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // dring thams cad dri zhim mchog tu 'gyur// spos rab mchog chus rgyal ba'i mchod rten dag/ khrus
46a6: byas byang chub zhing gi 'od de yin/ / ro bro skyong ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // dug can dug med ro yi mchog tu 'gyur// sangs rgyas nyan thos bcas dang pha ma la// ro mchog thams cad phul ba'i 'od de yin// reg rnam skyong
46a7: ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing / / reg na rtsub pa 'jam zhing bde bar 'gyur// mdung thung rtse gsum ral gri mda' chen char// phreng ba 'jam pa pad ma u pa la 'gyur// bcos bu'i ras mda' 'jam zhing reg bde rnams//
46a8: rgyal ba rnams kyi gshegs shul bting bkram ste// me tog byung ba na bza' 'jam rnams dang // phreng ba bla re phul ba'i 'od de yin// chos rnam sbyong ba'i 'od zer rab gtong zhing // 'jig rten phan mdzad rgyal ba thams cad
46b1: kyi/ spu rnams kun nas chos rnams bsam mi khyab// byung ba thos nas mos pa thams cad tshim// rkyen las byung ba ma skyes ngo bo nyid// rgyal ba rnams kyi sku ni chos sku ste// chos nyid mkha' bzhin rtag tu gnas so zhes//
46b2: brjod pas chos rnams sbyong ba thob par gyur// 'od zer sgo mo de dag la sogs pa// drang srong rnams kyi spu yi sgo gcig nos// 'od zer gang gA'i bye ma snyed byung ste// kun kyang las sbyor tha dad tshul can no// ji ltar de dag
46b3: spu yi sgo gcig nas/ / 'od zer gang ga'i bye ma snyed 'byung ba// ma lus spu rnams kun nas de bzhin te// drang srong ting 'dzin rnam 'phrul 'di 'dri'o// yon tan gang gis 'od zer gang grub pa'i// yon tan re grogs sngon
46b4: chad gang gyur pa/ / de dag nyid las 'od zer rang byung ste// drang srong ye shes rnam 'phrul 'di la'o// de dag bsod nams sngon grogs gang yin la// rjes su yid rang gsol ba sus btab dang // gang gis mthong ste dge ba bsag/
46b5: gyur pa// de dag kun gyis 'od zer de dag shes// gang dag bsod nams byas shing dge bsags dang // gang dag yang yang sangs rgyas rnams mchod cing // sangs rgyas yon tan 'dun te don gnyer ba// de dag kun la
46b6: 'od zer de dag bskul/ / dper na dmus long nyi ma mi mthong yang // de med ma yin 'jig rten dag tu 'char// mig dang ldan pas shar bar shes gyur nas// kun kyang rang rang so so'i las la 'jug/ de bzhin skyes chen
46b7: 'o bar de dag kun/ / rab tu 'byung yang log pas nyen gyur cing // mos nyams phal pa rnams kyis mi mthong ste// the gos g.yas pa rnams la de dag mod// dper brgya dor bu gzhon pa gzhal med khang // bcud
