67b7: pa thams cad dri med 'od ces bya ba'i mtshan yang gzung ngo / / tshig 'don to// phyag bya'o// lho phyogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas spobs pa'i brgyan la dgos pa zhes bya
67b8: mtshan yang gzung ngo / / yod la bya'o// nub phyogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa dri med zla ba'i tog gi rgyal po grags ldan zhes bya ba'i mtshan yang gzung ngo // phyag bya'o// byang phyogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa me tog
68a1: gi bkod pa snang bar mdzad pa zhes bya ba'i mtshan yang gzung ngo / / phyag bya'o// shar lho'i phyogs mtshams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa 'od mdzad ces bya ba'i mtshan yang gzung ngo // phyag kyang bya'o// lho nub kyi phyogs/
68a2: mtshams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen mchog gi tog grags ldan zhes bya ba'i mtshan yang gzung ngo // phyag kyang bya'o// nub byang gi phyogs mtshams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa 'jigs med rnam par gzigs shes
68a3: bya ba'i mtshan yang gzung ngo / / phyag bya'o// byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa 'jigs bral bag tshe mi mnga' spu zad mi byed pa'i mtshan yang gzung ngo // phyag bya'o// 'og gi phyogs kyi de bzhin gshegs
68a4: pa seng ge bsgyings pa'i med pa zhes bya ba'i mtshan yang gzung ngo / / phyag bya'o// steng gi phyogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa gser 'od gzi brjid 'jigs bral rgyal po zhes bya ba'i mtshan yang gzung ngo // phyag bya'o// byams pa
68a5: d ad pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcu gnyis po 'di dag gi mtshan brjod la nyi ma bcur sdig pa thams cad kyi nyes
68a6: pa bshags par bya/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad la rjes su yi rang bar bya/ sangs rgyas thams cad la bskul ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad la gsol ba gdab pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad chos kyi dbyings su yongs su//
68a7: bsngobs lo rtsa bsngo bar bya'o// 'on kyang sdig pa thams cad zad par 'gyur ro// las kyi sgrib pa thams cad rnam par byang bar 'gyur ro// de'i 'og du sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / mi 'jig
68a8: pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / mtshan phun sum tshogs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun phun sum tshogs pa dang / gzungs phun sum tshogs pa yang 'thob po// ting nge 'dzin phun sum tshogs pa yang 'thob po// bsam pa ji lta ba/
68b1: bzhin sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen phun sum tshogs pa yang myur du yongs su 'dzin te// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las nyams par mi 'gyur
68b2: zhing yongs su nyams par mi 'gyur ro/ / 'khor ba na 'khor ba'i tshe yang kun du mdzes pa dang / de'i longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa dang / rigs phun sum tshogs pa dang / skye ba phun sum tshogs pa dang rus phun sum tshogs pa dang /
68b3: gzugs phun sum tshogs pa dang / res 'dra ba'i skye bo'i 'khor phun sun chog pa yang yongs su 'dzin to// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ gang dang gang du skyes pa yi/ tshe rabs tshe rabs thams cad du/ mthong na dga' zhing dga' byed dang // 'od/
68b4: byed pa dang mthu chen dang // 'byor pa chen por 'gyur ba yin// gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di rnams kyang brjed par bya'o// tad+ya thA/ a khe ma khe/ sa man ta mu khe/ sau ti yug te/ nirA ga te/ pra b+he sa ma yo ge/ tsing ta tsi da tarte/ a
68b5: khe ma khe ma ne/ bibe te/ sa man ta gu ni/ sat+kA ra me/ yug te/ pra yug te/ tsi li mi laM/ ma sa le/ A na le/ tsa me/ a tsi te/ tsa tse/ a ra he/ btud tshe/ ma yu gra he he ma ba ti/ dz+ye ti ba ti/ d+harma tsid te/ tsU ta bang ge/ a bik+She ge ra d+hik+Sha me/
68b6: skan d+ha bi be ga te/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis gsang sngags kyi gzhi rnams grub par gyur cig/ de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ gzungs 'di dag gzung
68b7: byas nas/ phyogs bcu dag na gang bzhugs pa// bye ba drug bcu'i drang srong rnams// de dag de la dgongs par 'gyur// skye ba dag ni kun du yang // dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnyed par 'gyur// cung zad dge ba gang yin pa// don rnams thams cad 'byor
68b8: bar 'gyur/ / pad ma'i snying por bzhugs pa yi// sangs rgyas nams ni mngon sum mthong // gzungs 'di dag ni badzin byed pa// mkhas pa dpal ldan rdzus te skye// dran dang blo gros rtogs pa dang / mos da shes rab btu 'phel// thos pa thams
69a1: cad 'dzin par 'gyur/ / thos pa thams cad 'dzin ma nyams// 'jig rten pagon po 'di dag gi/ mtshan rnams su zhig rjod byed pa// ngan 'grothams cad spangs nas ni// bzang 'gror myur du 'gro bar 'gyur// nge 'dzin pa
69a2: gnas ky-i co/ / de dgades mngon pa gyur/ byang chub ba ng+ge 'tshang u0f7f// shin gyi ba thug stong // gsang kyis bkang ste spyo bye pas// gang shig banadu gshegs rnams kyi// mcher rnams 'dzid par byed pa /
69a3: bsod nams phung ba de ches mang // rtag tu tshe rabs dran par 'gyur// byang chub spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe// mi khom thams cad rnam spangs te// sangs rgyas 'byung ba rab mdzes rnyed// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mnyes par byed// da pa bla na mad
69a4: pa 'thog/ / sangs rgyas rnams la rab dad cing // mchod pa dam pa byed par 'gyur// sangs rgyas 'gyur ba mnyes byed de// mthong nas ston la rab tu dang // 'jig rten sgron ma mthong nas ni// mchod pa bzang po byed par 'gyur// mtshan rnams
69a5: 'di dag 'dzid byed pa/ / bskal pa bye ba grangs med du// 'khor ba rnam par spangs nas su// byang chub mur du 'chang yang rtsa// nyin zhag bdun du chang bar ni// mtshan rnams 'di dag 'dzin byed na// gang gis 'dren rnams mthong 'gyur ba'i//
69a6: rgya chen mig ni sbyangs par 'gyur// 'jig rten mgon po de dag gi/ mtshan rnams mi gang 'dzin byed pa// skye ba gang dang gar skyes pas// de ni phyag bya'i 'os su 'gyur// mtshan rnams 'di dag 'dzin byed pa// bskal pa bye ba bsam yas su/
69a7: bkur sti ma yin thob mi 'gyur// 'jig rten dag na grags pa thob// mtshan rnams 'di dag 'dzin byed pa// de la bskal pa du mar ni// lha rnams sti stang byed par 'gyur// byang chub myur du 'tshang yang rgya// mtshan rnams 'di dag 'dzin
69a8: byed pa/ / mos med shes rab 'chal mi 'gyur// g.yo dang sgyu ni rnam par spangs// rtag tu sangs rgyas rnams kyang mthong // mtshan rnams 'di dag 'dzin byed pa// lha dang dra zi klung dbang dang // mkha' lding lha mon gsang ba pa// rtag tu de la
69b1: bsrung bar byed/ / gzugs dang batshad ni phud sub tsogs// nor chad khyim du skye bar 'gyur// sems can kun la sbyin par byed// dpa' zhing gtong por ser sna med// sal babye ba brgya mang por// lha yi can dan dbang po dang //
69b2: shin du dri zhim spos kun gyi// spos dang de yi kha nas byung // mtshan rnams 'di dag 'dzin byed pa// bskal pa bye bar sgra skad ni// tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan par 'gyur// rtag tu chos rgyal tshul dang ldan// mtshan rnams 'di
69b3: dag 'dzin byed pa/ / rin chen sna bdun pad ma 'dab// bye ba stong phrag mang yos las// 'byor chen de skye lha gzugs ldan// mtshan rnams 'di dag su 'dzin pa// de ni pha ma spud sdug dang // skye bo dag gi tshogs rnams dang // 'bral
69b4: bar 'gyur ba mi mthong ngo / / drang srong chen po rnams kyi mtshan// bu med kyis ni gzung byas na// bud pad lus la ma chags nas// skyes pa blo gros ldan par 'gyur// mi yi lus ni thob gyur nas// bla med byang chub thob gyur te//
69b5: chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor nas// 'dod pa zhi bzhin mya ngan 'da'// mtshan rnams 'di dag su 'dzin pa// de yi lus la mtshon dang ni// dug dang me dang rgyal po dang // g.yon can rnams kyis mi tshugs so// mtshan rnams 'ad
69b6: dag su 'dzin pa/ / de yi sems la nams kyang ni// dpung dang gzhon par bcas pa yi// bdud kyis glags rnyed mi 'gyur ro// 'di dag gi ni mtshan gyi rnams// mi gang 'dzin par byed pa de// 'di ni bye ba bsam yas par// dam mkha'
69b7: las ni 'gro bar 'gyur/ / sangs rgyas bstan pa rnams mchod nas// 'jigs pa med par zhu ba'u// de dag nga yi bas pa mkhyen nas// rgyal ba de dag lung sror 'gyur// sangs rgyas mgon po de dag las// lung bstan pa ni grib
69b8: gung dang/ den gan du ma ngangs te// rgyal ba'i bstan la tha tsham med// macan rnams 'di dag 'dzin byed pa// 'dag rten sa gan po rnams las ni/ zab pa'i chos na thos 'gyur te// thos nas thams cad 'dza par 'gyub
70a1: pha rol phyin sa dang / / mi 'jigs pa dang stobs rnams dang // mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnams// ma lus par ni rdzogs par 'gyur// sangs rgyas de dag rnams kyi ni// gang gi zhing du 'dod gyur pa// der ni bla
70a2: med yang dag rdzogs/ / byang chub rtogs nas 'chang rgyar 'gyur// skyes pa 'am ni bud med gang // mtshan rnams 'di dag 'dzin pa yi// yon tan 'di dang gzhan dag dang // sangs rgyas bsngal bar rgyun du gsung // khag yod ldan
70a3: par gyur nas ni/ / yon tan phun sum 'di thos nas// rdzogs pa'o sangs rgyas grags ldan pa// de dag mtshan rnams 'dzin par 'gyur// sangs rgyas 'di dag dpal snying po// sprin gyi rgyal po mi yi mchog/ 'jig rten mgon
70a4: 'di dag gi/ mtshan ni bskal par gang mnyam dang // gang dag 'di rnams mtshan nyan cing // thos nas gus par byed 'gyur ba// de dang de dag shes rab che// rkang gnyis rnams kyi mchog du 'gyur// drang srong chen po de dag gi/ 'di
70a5: 'dra'i mtshan dag thos gyur na/ / bag yod ldan zhing mkhas gyur la// shes rab ldan pa su mi 'dzin// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa dang /
70a6: byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / dge slong de dag dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dang / lha dang mi dang lha ma yin dang // dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te// bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par
70a7: par bstod do/ / 'phags pa sangs rgyas bcu gnyis pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar gyi mkhan po 'dzin mi tra dang / dA na shi la dang / zhu chen gyi lo rgyab ban/ d+he ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te//
70a8: skad gsar chad kyis kyang bcos nas gtan la phab pa// // rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya bud+d+ha tri d+ha ya nA ma d+hA raNA d+harma pa r+yA ya/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa sangs rgyas kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs
70b1: sa ma rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ / 'di skad bdagags thos pa'i dus gcig na// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stso yul ches kyi dbye dpon pa rin po che bad
70b2: pa'i 'khor gyi byams/ yi shes kyi ma par dbyung ba/ stonas sa rnam kyi ny-id kyis dgas pa/ sebs ca/ thabs cad kyis mngan par bstod pa/ byang chubasams dpa' chen pa'i gnas rnam pa thams
70b3: kyi mchog dang ldan pa/ chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su spyod pa/ kun nas 'od kyi khang bzangs kyi dbus na byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du ma thams cad kyang lung bstan pa/ thams cad kyang
70b4: 'jig rten gyi khams tha dad pa nas 'dus pa/ thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi rgyal po'i sras// thams cad kyang gzungs dang ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs thob pa sha stag gis yongs su bskor cing mdun gyis
70b5: bltas nas thabs gcig tu zhugs te chos ston to/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor rgya chen po la bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu dag skye bo mang po la phan pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang /
70b6: 'jig rten la thugs rje ba dang / lha dang ma'i skye bo phal po che'i don dang / phan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyis gsungs pa
70b7: sangs rgyas kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs yod do/ / rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la la sangs rgyas kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di 'chang ngam/ 'dzin tam/ klog
70b8: gam/ kun chub par byed dam/ gzhan dag la yang rgya cher yang dag par rab tu ston tam/ dad dam lhag pa'i bsam pas mos par byed na/ de bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur// /
71a1: chos thams cad 'dzin pa dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa lta ba dang / bsnyen bkur byed pa dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur/ chos nyan
71a2: pa dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur/ dge 'dun la rim gro byed pa dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur// bskal pa stong du 'khor ba'i srid pa'i rgya mtsho phyir bsnyil bar 'gyur/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par
71a3: sangs rgyas kyi bar du tshe rabs dran par 'gyur/ myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur/ de la 'byung po'i tshogs thams cad srung bar 'gyur// lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin
71a4: dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye che na dang mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad dga' bar 'gyur/ de'i lus la nad kyis mi tshugs par 'gyur// pha rol gyi gnod pas 'chi ba'i dus byed par mi
71a5: 'gyur/ chad pa spang ba dang / mtshon cha spang ba dang / dug bcil nas 'chi ba'i dus byed par mi 'gyur/ de la bdud sdig can gyis glags rnyed par mi 'gyur/ bdud kyi ris kyi lha rnams kyis skabs rnyed par mi 'gyur te// gang du yid
71a6: la byas pa der bdud kyi las kyi lha de dag thams cad skrag cing dngang par 'gyur zhing phyogs bcur 'bros par 'gyur ro/ / de la 'di dag sangs rgyas kyi tshig go// sangs rgyas kyi tshig chen po'o// sangs rgyas kyis gan /
71a7: chen po'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi tshig go// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi tshig yin no// t+ya thA/ buH/ sa bud+d+he/ mahA bud+d+he/ i tA prad+d+he/ tad tra prad+d+he bud+d+he prad+he/ bud+ha maH/ bud+d+he/ sarba bud+ha/ a num te/ sarba pra/
71a8: ana? d+hAn ta pra d+ya bud+ha/ bad+ha bad+ha/ bad+ha/ bad+d+ha/ bad+ha bud+ha/ badrA sangs rgyas kyi yul mtha' yas te/ chos bstan pa yang mtha' yas mod kyi/ gcig tu yid la bya ba ni mdor na bsgom pa'o// gzungs 'di nas ng+ge/
71b1: can rnams 'thugs rtse ba'i phying sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gsungs pas/ chos thams cad kyi phyag rgya yinan// d+ya/ d+has kAr+m+ma/ sarbA d+d+he/ shar+d+ha ni/ sa shau d+han/ pral/ ma la ma bag / gnyis sa
71b2: tekra ma sams pa sa nAs rapa ri a she kaM/ bi sha kA/ sh+lo ka sha mran/ shan+ta// u ba shan tA/ b+hA shan/ A ba b+hU sa/ sarba prar+t+ta pa man to// sarbad+harmA pra ti man tat+tA/ tar ta/ ma la ta / tsAr tsA pa/ tsa
71b3: tsa la tsa la sa tsa la/ ta la ta la/ ma ha ya sa ma ta la/ ra na na/ su ra ne/ sa ma ra na/ r-i na ma ta/ lo ka d+ha ra/ lo ka d+ha ro Na/ d+ha ra d+ha ra/ Da ra Da ra/ rod+ha ro d+ha/ ma hA bi dza ya/ bA he me ha na ta na/ sarba bud+d+he/ tra pre shi tra si saH
71b4: dz+nyA pa ra mi ti/ ma hA prA ti b+ha na sa/ pan ne/ sa man te/ a lo ke bud+d+ha/ bi sha ye/ bud+d+ha pra ta ma Na Di ti/ b+ha ga ba te/ sa ra sa ra/ pra sar pra sa ra/ bi sa ra bi sa / pra sa ra sarba sho sha a bag te swA hA// bcom ldan 'das
71b5: kyis sangs rgyas kyi snying po'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bshad ma thag tu ra dang gnas su bcas pa dang / tshal rnam pa drug tu g.yos/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyis yang
71b6: g.yos so/ / rab tu g.yos so// kun tu rab tu g.yos so// rgya mtsho chen po yang 'khrugs/ rab tu 'khrugs/ kun du rab tu 'khrugs so// ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyang ldeg cing 'gul to// bdud kyi gnas thams cad
71b7: skrag nas/ bdud kyi ris kyi lha rnams dang / bdud sdig can rnams shin du sdug bsngal yid mi bde bar gyur nas nyams thag go// sems can gang dag sa chen po g.yos par mthong ba de dag gi de bzhin gshegs
71b8: pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la phyag 'tshal lo/ / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la phyag 'tshal lo zhes ched du brjod pa lan gsum ched du
72a1: brjod do/ / lha gang dag sangs rgyas la mngon par dad pa de dag gis lha'i me tog man dA ra ba dang / man dAr chen pos bcom ldan 'das la gtor/ mngon par gtor nas/ gang dag sangs rgyas la skyabs
72a2: su dong ba de dag thams cad rab tu dga' ba skyes so/ / de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ shAkya seng ge yang dag rdzogs pa yi// sangs rgyas skyob pas skad cig yu gang la// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ni snying po yi/ gzungs
72a3: 'di dag ni rab tu bshad pa yi/ / skad cig yud de sa yang rnam pa drug d+hi g.yos// rgya mtsho 'khrugs shing bdud kyi gnas kun kyang // rab tu g.yos nas bdud kyi ris rnams kyi// lha dag rab tu dngangs shing 'khrugs pa
72a4: 'gyur/ / bdud yid mi bde sdug bsngal mya ngan non// de tshe lha rnams ngo mtshar rab thos nas// 'jig rten mgon la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir// nam mkhar gnas nas me tog man du 'thor// gang dag sangs rgyas mngon
72a5: dang gzhan rnams kyi/ / se mo do dang do shol spos rnams dang // phye ma dag dang byug pa gos rnams dang // rgyan dang dpung rgyan dag kyang rab tu 'bul// brgyad po 'di dag ni de'i yon tan gyi phan yon gyi rkyen du 'gyur ba'o// rgya
72a6: gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ byang chub kyi sems mi brjed pa'i rgyan dang / thos pa thams cad yongs su tshol bas mi ngoms pa'i rgyan dang / chos zab mo rnam par nges pa rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i rgyan dang / sems can
72a7: thams cad kyi ma tshom ga sa ga ma yin pa shes pa'i rgyan dang / ji ltar thos pa dang ji ltar khong du chud pa'i chos rnams la tshul bzhin so sor rtog cing dpyod pa'i rgyan dang / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir chos
72a8: thams cad mi dmigs pa'i rgyan dang / rgyan de yang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis/ thabs la mkhas pa'i rgyan dang / gzungs thob pa'i rgyan te/ brgyad po de dag ni de'i yon tan gyi phan yon gyi rkyen du 'gyur ro// gzungs
72b1: 'di rtag par rgyun du yid la bya'o/ / sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa sgom par bya'o// gzungs kyi gzhi 'di rnams yid la byas na las kyi sgrib pa thams cad yongs su byang bar 'gyur ro// pad ma rnam par bkod pa zhes
72b2: b+hA ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob bo/ / nad thams cad dang / na ba thams cad la lag pas byab par bya'o// bzlas brjod kyang dpag tu med par bya'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ byang chub sems dpa'
72b3: sems dpa' chen po de dag dang / nyan thos chen po de dag dang / lha dang mi dang lha ma yon dang dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod de// / 'phags pa sangs
72b4: rgyas kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi kye chos kyi rnam gangs rdzogs s+ho/ / rgya gar gyi mkhan po 'dzin mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo ts+tsha ba ban d+he ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te/ skad gsar chad kyis kyang bcos nas
72b5: gtan la phab pa/ / / rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya bud+d+ha hri da ya nA ma d+hA ra NI/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa sangs rgyas kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo//
72b6: 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rgya mtsho'i 'gram gyi skyed mos tshal na sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul gyi shing ljon pa kun nas seng ge'i khri la bzhugs te/ lha'i 'khor gyi kun nas bskor cing
72b7: mdun gyis bltas te chos ston to/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dbang phyug chen po dka' thub bzang po la sogs pa gonas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu rnams la bka' stsal pa/ lha'i bu dag de'i phyi legs par rab tu nyon
72b8: la yid la zung shig dang bshad do/ / de bzhin gshegs pa phyi ma'i dus na 'khor bzhi bsdu ba dang rjes su gzung ba dang kun du rjes su gzung ba dang khyad par du 'gro bar bya ba dang / don thams cad chos thams cad dang ldan pa yo
73a1: sa rdzogs par bya ba dang / theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa rnams rnam pa thams cad du khyad par thob par bya ba'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs ston to// 'chang po de
73a2: khyed kyis zung la da ltar dang / nga yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas phyi ma'i dus na theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa'i 'khor rnam bzhi rnams la ston cig/ shod cig/ yal bar mi dor bar nges par bstan par
73a3: bya/ bsgrag par bya'o// ji tsam du phongs par gyur pa rnams dang / sgrib pa dang ldan pa rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung bskyang zhing nges par bstan par bya/ bsgrag par bya'o// gsol pa bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
73a4: dra bgyi ste/ de bzhin gshegs pas ji skad bka' stsal ba de bzhin du 'tshal lo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' 'di nan tan gyis yongs su rdzogs par bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ lha'i bu dag/
73a5: sangs rgyas kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs gang zhe na/ tad+ya thA/ a mA le/ nirma le/ sarba A kA rA aR+ShA pa ri pra ba te/ a sa ma ta sarba kun A kA re/ tA d+ha/ a saM ga a nA bri te/ sa mi ta/ da sha di sha/ ba ri pA r+Na dz+nyA ne/ sarba
73a6: a saM gad ra sha na prA ba te/ sarba d+harma ma bi sha tA pa ri pUNe/ sarba a kA rA/ a saM ga sa man+ta te/ sa men ta a pr-i ti hi ta ta dze t+yA d+hA da sha s+ya/ dik+Shu pa ri prA ba ta/ an+te/ shAn tA/ prA shA na tA/ um krAH// sam k+ShanatA bi rak+ShaM a nu pra ba
73a7: te/ su pra ti bu d+ha d+harma d+hA tu/ a t+yan ta su ni sr-i ti/ sarba A kA rA ni sa sa ra Na/ an ba she Sha bA ra da ga te/ pa pri mug ta/ a saM yo ga/ ba pri yo ga/ s+thi te d+ha ma te/ ga ga nas ma pra kri ta be ri shu d+ha/ nArme le/ a sa man ta/
73a8: tA d+hA a nu ga ta/ su pra ba te pU rban ta/ a pa ran ta/ ma d+ha t+yA d+hA sa maM ta a nu prA ba tI/ a na ba she Sha/ pa ra dzI pa han/ b+ha ba na/ sak+Shad kri ya pa ra ma ba rang ga te/ ya thA ba ti ta thA kA ki/ sarba a kA rA sa ma pa na ne/ sarba A kA
73b1: ra ma hA mai twe ma hA ka ru NA/ sarba A kA rA sa ma sa gra ha a nu pra ba te/ lha'i bu dag 'di na sangs rgyas kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs te/ theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa'i 'khor
73b2: bzhi po las rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig gis lus la thogs sam/ legs par kha ton du byas te 'dzin pa des dman pa'i sems su mi bya ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa ji lta ba bzhin du de dag
73b3: gi spyi gtsug gi steng gi mtshams su gnas par 'gyur ro/ / kha gcig ni nges par sangs rgyas mthong bar 'gyur ro// kha gcig ni thos par 'gyur/ kha cig ni chos ston par 'gyur/ kha cig ni gzungs mi rjed par 'gyur
73b4: slob pa lam la gnas pa rnams ni lam gyi rgyun mi 'chad cing chos ston pa rgyun mi 'chad par 'gyur/ kun du 'dzin pa mi brjed par yang 'gyur/ skye ba gcig gis thogs pa grub par 'gyur/ de dag dang ldan na

79a1: gsungs te/ gang gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag las 'da' bar byed pa de ni de dag thams cad la 'khus pa yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ma pham pa stan las
79a2: langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de legs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/
79a3: bcom ldan 'das padag gis kyang sems can rnams kyi don dang / sman pa dang bde ba dang mdangs dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / gzi brjid dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / grags pa dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / yon tan dang
79a4: ldan par bgyi ba dang / stobs dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / mdog dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / bsrung ba dang sba ba dang bskyab pa'i slad du gzungs kyi gsang sngags kyi gzhi 'di rnams brjod par bgyi'o// 'di lta ste/ ad
79a5: te/ ba da te/ nad te/ ku nad te/ pu ka se/ ku pu ka se/ ka se/ a nA ka se/ nA ma ka se/ a nu ta/ prA nu ta/ kha dze/ ma hA kha dze/ sa da pa pe/ ta Da be/ tu Da be/ hi la mi li/ ti le swA hA// de de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang /
79a6: ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo khyod kyis gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag zung shig/ long shig/ chongs shig lhogs shig/ kun chub par byas shig/ gzhan dag la yang rgya cher yang
79a7: dag par rab tu ston cig/ kun dga' bo sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnyed par dka'o// gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag rnyed par dka'o// kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa yang shin tu
79a8: rnyed par dka'o/ / kun dga' bo rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la la gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa dang / len pa dang / 'chang ba dang klog pa dang kun chub par byed pa dang / gzhan dag la yang
79b1: rgya cher rab tu ston pa de ni tshe rabs bcu gnyis su tshe rabs dran par 'gyur ro/ / tshe 'di nyid la yang sngon gyi las ma gtogs par gzhan gyi gnod pa thams cad la yang dag par 'da' ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang rjes
79b2: su 'thun par 'gyur ro/ / kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bye ba phrag brgyad bcu rtsa gnyis kyis gsungs te/ gang gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag las 'da' bar
79b3: byed pa ni de dag thams cad la 'khus pa yin no/ / de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas pus mo g.yas pa'i lhungs la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das
79b4: ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das bdag gis kyang sems can rnams kyi don dang / sman pa dang bde ba dang mdangs dang ldan par bgyi ba dang /
79b5: gzi brjid dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / grags pa dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / yon tan dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / stobs dang ldan par brgya ba dang / mdog dang ldan par bgyi ba dang / bsrung ba dang sra ba dang / bstab pa'i slad du
79b6: gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di rnams brjod par bgyi'o/ / 'di lta swA/ ag khe bag khe/ nI dza ta/ nI gA sa ra/ ni hi le/ na hi le/ dza hi le/ dze hi le/ dza hri la pa te/ tsaN DI la ba tA swA hA// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis
79b7: dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' ba byed gzungs kyi gas du sngags gzhi 'di dag gzung shig/ yang shig tshangs shig/ lcags shig/ kun chub par gyis srog/ gzhan dag la yang rgya char ra
79b8: na cig/ kun dga' bo sangs rgyas 'byung ba da par dga'o// gzungs kyi gas sngags gzhi 'di dag rnyed par dag / klan dga' bo gzungs kyigs sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa yang gan tu rnyed bang
80a1: dka'o/ / kun dga' bo rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la las gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa dang / len pa dang 'chad pa dang klog pa dang / kun chub par byed pa dang / gzhan dag
80a2: la yang rgya cher rab tu ston pa de ni tshe rabs bcu gsum du tshe rabs dran par 'gyur ro/ / tshe 'di nyid la yang sngon gyi las ma gtogs pa gzhan gyi gnod pa thams cad las yang dag par 'da' ba dang / 'gro
80a3: pa thams cad dang rjes su 'thun par 'gyur ro/ / kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags kyi gzhi 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bye ba phrag brgyad bcu rtsa gnyis kyis gsungs te/ gang gzungs kyi gsang sngags
80a4: gzhi 'di dag las 'da' bar byed pa de ni de dag thams cad la 'khus pa yin no/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong rnams la bka' stsal pa/ dge slong dag ngas kyang sems can rnams kyi don dang
80a5: phan pa dang bde ba dang mdangs dang ldan par bya ba dang / gzi brjid dang ldan par bya ba dang / grags pa dang ldan par bya ba dang / yon tan dang ldan par bya ba dang / stobs dang ldan par bya ba dang / mdog dang ldan par
80a6: bya ba dang / bsrung ba dang sba ba dang bskyab pa'i phyir gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi rnams bshad do// 'di lte ste/ oMd te/ pad Te/ na da Te/ ku nang Te/ Ta ke/ a Da ke/ tra ta pe/ tu Da pi/ ra Ta ke/ lo le/ hu le hi le mi
80a7: le/ ti le/ shA le/ shI la/ a D+he/ baD+he/ nAD+haM/ ku naD+he/ a Da pra tI/ pe Na pa tI/ ka se ka se ka se/ pha se pha saM pa se/ ma hA pha sai pha se swAH/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka'
80a8: stsal pa/ kun dga' bo khyod kyis gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag zung shig/ long shig chongs shig/ lhogs shig/ kun chub par gyis sha gi/ gzhan dag la yang rgya cher rab tu ston cig/ kun dga'
80b1: bo sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnyed par dka'o/ / gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag rnyed par dka'o// kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags 'di dag ston pa yang shin tu rnyed par dka'o// kun dga' bo rigs kyi bu
80b2: 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la la gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa dang len pa dang 'chang ba dang klog pa dang / kun chub par byed pa dang / gzhan dag la yang rgya cher rab tu ston pa de ni tshe rabs bcu bzhir
80b3: tshe rabs dran par 'gyur ro/ / tshe 'di nyid la yang sngon gyi las ma gtogs par gzhan gyi gnod pa thams cad las 'da' ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang rjes su 'thun par 'gyur ro// kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags
80b4: gzhi 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bye ba phrag brgyad bcu rtsa bzhis gsungs te/ gang gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag las 'da' bar byed pa de ni de dag thams cad la 'khus pa yin no// rigs kyi bu'am rigs kyi bu mo
80b5: gang la la dag gis gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag shing skam po gsher bag med pa la bsrung ba byas te/ yongs su bskyab pa dang yongs su gzung ba dang bcing ba dang zhi ba dang / bde legs su 'gyur ba byas
80b6: na shing de las lcu gu dang / lo ma dag kyang skye bar 'gyur te/ me tog dang 'bras bu rnams kyang mngon par 'grub par 'gyur na/ mir gyur pa lta ci smos/ na maHsarba bud+d+he b+ha/ sid d+hAn tu d+ha ra NI/ man tra pA da ne swA hA/ de nas
80b7: bcom ldan 'das kyis yang dge slong rnams la bka' stsal pa/ dge slong dag sems can rnams kyi don dang / phan pa dang bde ba dang mdangs dang ldan par bya ba dang / gzi brjid dang ldan par bye ba dang / grags pa dang ldan par
80b8: bya ba dang / yon tan dang ldan par bya ba dang / stobs dang ldan par bya ba dang / mdog dang ldan par bya ba dang / bsrung ba dang sba ba dang bskyab pa'i phyir gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi gzhan dag kyang bshad par bya'o// 'di lta ste/
81a1: ad te/ mad te/ ba k+She/ pA ra ke/ be ke DA dra ma ti/ ta ram ti/ DA Dam ti/ Tu Ta ma Ti/ Tu Da T+Ta re/ su ra/ ti li mu le/ ti le swA hA// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tsha dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/ kun
81a2: dga' bo khyod kyis gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag zung shig/ long shig/ chongs shig lhogs shig/ kun chub par gyis shig/ gzhan dag la yang rgya cher rab tu ston cig/ kun dga' bo sangs rgyas 'byung ba
81a3: rnyed par dka'o/ / gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag rnyed par dka'o// kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa yang shin tu rnyed par dka'o// kun dga' bo rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang
81a4: la la gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa dang / len pa dang 'chad pa dang klog pa dang / kun chub par byed pa dang / gzhan dag la yang rgya cher rab tu ston pa de ni tshe rabs nyi shu rtsa gcig tu tshe rabs dran par 'gyur ro//
81a5: tshe 'di nyid la yang sngon gyi las ma gtogs par gzhan gyi gnod pa thams cad las 'da' ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang rjes su 'thun par 'gyur ro// gang la la zhig la bsrung ba byas na de la yang 'byung po thams cad kyis
81a6: mi tshugs so/ / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang lha ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad kyis mi tshugs so// sbrul dang srin bu dang sin bu lu ta dang / sbrang
81a7: bu lcags phye thams cad kyis ma tshugs so/ / rims rlung dang mkhris pa dang bad kan dang 'dus pa dang / dus tshigs 'gyur ba las byung ba thams cad kyis mi tshugs so// zhag gcig pa 'am/ zhag gnyis pa 'am zhag gas
81a8: pa 'am/ / zhag bzhi pa 'am/ zhag bdun pa 'am/ zla ba phyed pa 'am/ zla gcig pa 'am/ lo gcig pa'am/ nad rgyun rings sam/ skad cig pa rnams kyis mi tshugs so// 'bras sam/ phol mig gam/ rkang shu 'am/ lhag pa'am
81b1: me dpal lam/ shu ba'am/ khyi rdo'am/ g.yan pa 'am/ mdze thams cad dam/ klog pa thams cad dam/ gshed byed thams cad dam/ skur ba'i las thams cad dam/ byad thams cad dang / ro langs thams cad kyis kyang mi tshigs
81b2: so/ / kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgus gsungs te/ gang gzungs kyi gsang sngags kyi gzhi 'di dag las 'da' bar byed pa de ni de dag thams cad la 'bum
81b3: ba yin no/ / kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag ni rgyal po'i pho brang ngan 'dug na yang yid la bya'o// chom rkun gyi nang na 'dug ni yang yid la bya'o// srin po'i nang na 'dug na yang yid la bya'o// gcan zan
81b4: khro bo'i nang na 'dug na yang yid la bya'o/ / 'brog dgon pa'i nang na 'dug na yang yid la bya'o// klung dang bgrod dka' ba na 'dug na yang yid la bya'o// me'i nang na 'dug na yang yid la bya'o// chu'i nang na 'dug na yang yid la
81b5: bya'o/ / de yid la byas pa de rnams las 'jigs pa de dag thams cad mi 'byung ngo // des dug zos pa thams cad kyang kha zas nyid du 'gyur ro// kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa ni 'byung po
81b6: thams cad kyis mi tshugs so/ / yi dgas thams cad dang / srul po thams cad dang / gshed byed thams cad dang / skur ba'i las thams cad dang / byad thams cad dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad kyis mi tshugs te/ kun dga'
81b7: bo 'dor na de la gzhan gyi gnod pa thams cad kyis mi tshugs so/ / kun dga' bo gsang ba'i rigs pa ni chad pas bral bar 'gyur ro// chad pas gcad pa'i rigs pa ni brdegs pas/ brdegs pa'i rigs pa ni brgyad pra
81b8: brgyad pa'i rigs pa na ba sdigs pas/ bsdigs pa'i rigs pa ni mig tshugs su bltas pas thar bar 'gyur ro// kun dga' bo gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag gis gang la bsrung ba byas pa 'am/ yongs su bsgrub
82a1: ba byas pa'am/ yongs su gzung ba 'am/ bcings pa 'am/ zhi ba dang bde legs su 'gyur ba byas pa gzhan du 'gyur ba de ni gnas med de/ lha dang bcas/ bdud dang bcas/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten dang /
82a2: dge sbyong dang bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu dang / lha dang mi dang lha ma yin gyi nang na yangs ma mthong ngo // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag ni gnod pa dang / nad go ba la dang / 'khrug pa thams cad las
82a3: nges par 'byung bar byin gyis brlabs pa'i phyir ro/ / de nas chos kyi rnam grangs 'di rdzogs pa'i rjes la rgyal po chen po bzhis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis kyang /
82a4: chos kyi rnam grangs 'di rgya cher rgyas par bgyi ba dang / chos smra ba de dag rjes su yongs su gzung ba dang / dam pa'i chos ci nas kyang yun ring du gnas pa dang / bdud thams cad tshar gcad pa'i slad du gzungs kyi gsang sngags
82a5: gzha 'di rnams rjes su stsal bar 'tshal na/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de la legs so zhes bgyi ba gnang bar mdzad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis rgyal po chen po ni la thugs brtse ba'i phyir cang mi gsung ba
82a6: phyung bas gnang ste/ / rgyal po chen po bzhi po de dag gis kyang bcom ldan 'das kyis cang mi gsung bar gyur pas gnang bar rig nas ched du brjod pa ched du brjod do// de ni 'di lta ste/ da nad ke de nad De/ ma hA nad Ne/ dzam b+ha ne
82a7: stam b+hane/ Ta Te Te Ten/ ma hA Ta ne/ kung Te/ kung can/ mahA krung Tan/ d+harma la/ tsarma le swAhA// bcom ldan 'das 'di dag ni gzungs 'di'i 'khor gyi tshig lta bur gda' ba lags te/ rigs kyi bu'am gas kyi bu mo gang la/
82a8: la gzungs sngags gzhi 'di dag 'dzin pa dang / bzlas te bton nas 'chang ba de ni sngon gyi las ma gtogs par gzhan gyi gnod pa thams cad las 'da' ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang rjes su 'thun par 'gyur ro// de la ni dam/
82b1: pa'i chos thams cad yongs su gzung ba la yang bang chad 'byung bar mi 'gyur lags so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag la grags po dag khyed bstan pa yun ring du gnas par bya ba'i phyir shras/
82b2: pa legs so legs so zhes bya ba byin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo khyod kyis de dag rdzu 'phrul che bar 'gyur ba dang / phan yon che ba dang byin che bar
82b3: 'gyur ba'i phyir gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di zung shig/ long shig chongs shig/ lhogs shig/ kun chub par gyis shig/ gzhan dag la yang rgya cher rab tu ston cig/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das rgyas par bgyi
82b4: pa'i slad du bdag gis bzung lags so/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don 'di nyid rgyas par bstan pa'i phyir de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag bka' stsal to// gzungs sngags kyi ni mdo sde 'di// sangs rgyas kun
82b5: gyis gsungs pa ste/ / sems can rnams la phan pa'i phyir// de ni ngas kyang bshad pa yin// gang zhig gzungs sngags mdo sde 'di// 'dzin tam yang na klog byed pa// tshe rabs nyi shu rtsa gcig tu// de ni tshe rabs dran par
82b6: 'gyur/ / gzungs sngags 'di rjod byed de la// mi min gang yang rung ba dang // gnod sbyin grul bum srin po dag/ nams kyang bar chad mi byed do// gzungs sngags 'di rjod byed de la// 'dod khams dbang phyug gang yin pa/
82b7: sdig can bdud de nam du yang / bar chad byed par mi 'gyur ro// gzungs sngags 'di 'dzin byed de yi// pha ma dang ni phu nu dang / sring mo mdzu ba shes gnyen dag kyang // log par ltung bar mi 'gyur ro// de phyir gzungs
82b8: sngags mdo sde 'di/ / 'jigs med gang gis zos gyur nas// gzungs sngags 'di rjod byed pa deg rnams cha 'jigs par mi bya'o// gzungs sngags 'di 'dzin byed de yis// bskal pa bye ba stong rnams su// sgrib pa'i
83a1: las ni gang byas pa/ / zhag bdun gyis ni byang bar 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa'i bsod nams gang // bskal pa bye bar bsgrubs pa kun// gzungs sngags 'di 'dzin byed pa des// zhag bdun gyis ni zil gyis
83a2: non/ phyogs bzhi'i 'jig rten skyong ba po// rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag/ lus ngan dang ni yul 'khor srung // mig mi bzang dang 'phags skyes po// bdog ldan zhing grags dang ldan// 'khor bcas blon mas de dag kyang //
83a3: gzungs sngags 'di ni rjod byed pa// de la rtag tu srung bar byed// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo dang nyan thos chen po de dag dang / 'phags pa byams pa dang / 'jam
83a4: dpal la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams dang / rgyal po chen po bzhi dang lha dang mi dang lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa
83a5: la mngon par bstod do/ / // 'phags pa rigs sngags kyi rgyal po sgron ma mchog gi gzungs rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya a b+hi Shiny+tsa nitriHd+hA ra NI/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa dbang skur ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs
83a6: sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ / 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' rab
83a7: na dge slong brgyad stong gi dge 'dun chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa' grangs med pa bye ba sngon gyi rgyal ba la lhag par bya ba byas pa rnams dang thabs gcig rgyu bzhugs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan
83a8: pa shA ri'i bu la bka' stsal pa/ shA ri'i bu khyod kyis 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i ma dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sngon gyi spyod pa dang / bden pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems da'i chos yongs su gzung ba/
83b1: byang chub sems dpa'i chos 'di dag bsgoms shig/ sngon cig/ 'di ltaste// gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs so// de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bus bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das
83b2: gzungs ni yul na mi gnas/ / phyogs na mi gnas na bcom ldan 'das gzungs gzungs shes bgyi ba la/ bcom ldan 'das gzungs shes bgyi ba 'di'i tshig gi don gang lags/ de skad ces gsol ba dang / bcom//
83b3: ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa shAtI rI buM la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ri'i bu legs so legs so// shA ri'i bu khyod 'di ltar theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa dang / theg pa chen po la mngon par brtson pa dang /
83b4: theg pa chen po la lhag par bya ba byed pa dang / khyod gzungs yul na mi gnas/ phyogs na mi gnas par ston pa yang legs so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ shA ri'i bu gzungs ni chos nyid kyis 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang //
83b5: da ltar byung ba ma yin te/ shA ri'i bu gzungs ni 'das zhes mi 'chad// ma 'ongs pa zhes mi 'chad/ da ltar byung ba zhes mi 'chang / dngos por mi 'chad/ dngos po med par mi 'chad/ mtshan ma dang mtshan ma med par mi
83b6: 'chang / chos gang skye ba'i phyir ram/ 'gug pa'i phyir mi 'char mod kyi/ shA ri'i bu 'on kyang byang chub sems dpa' la than par bzhed pa'i phyir ston te/ gang 'di gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs kyi gnas ni gzugs med
83b7: ga bya ba'i lam du gyur pa/ rigs pa'i stobs kyis gnas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan/ sangs rgyas kyi lhag par bya ba sgrub pa/ sangs rgyas kyi tshul khrims/ sangs rgyas kyis bsdus pa/ sangs rgyas kyi mtshams
83b8: sbyor ba/ / sangs rgyas 'byung ba'o// de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bus bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gzungs gang la gnas shing gzungs de thob na byang chub sems dpa' bla na med
84a1: ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ba dang / dam bca' ba bzung ba dang / chos la mi gnas pa dang / bdag the tsom ma mchis pa dang / slob dpon ma mchis pa dang / rang gi lam lag
84a2: ba bcom ldan 'das bshad du gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa bshad du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ri'i bri legs so legs so// shA ri'i bu gzungs thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni
84a3: sangs rgyas nyid du brjod do/ / shA ri'i bu gang la la zhig byang chub sems dpa' gzungs thob pa la sti stang du byed dam/ bla mar byed dam/ rim gror byed dam/ mchod na des sangs rgyas thams cad la sti stang byas
84a4: par 'gyur ro/ / gang dag gis gzungs 'di thos pa dang / gang dag mos pa de dag kyang sangs rgyas rnams ji lta ba de bzhin du mchod pa'i 'os su 'gyur zhing byang chub kyi sems dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur ro// shA ri'i bu
84a5: gzungs ni 'di yin te/ san d+hA ra NI/ ud d+ha ra NI/ sam pra tiSh+Tha tA/ su ta pa/ su pra tiShI tA/ bi dza ya ba lA/ swa b+ha pra tri dzA/ a ro hA/ dz+nyA na pa ti/ ud bA da nI bI nA ma nI/ a b+hi Shiny+tsa ni/ a b+hi b+hU hA rA/ shu b+ha ba Ti e ni thIta
84a6: ba hu kum b+ha/ a b+hi pa tsa// shA ri'i bu 'di dge ni dbang bskur ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi chos kyi ming nams te/ 'das pa rnams dang / ma 'ongs pa rnams dang / da ltar byung ba rnams dang / lags par gnas pa
84a7: rnams byang chub sems dpa' gang gis legs par bzung ste/ 'chang ba de myur du mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba'i phyir bskal pa brgya dang / bskal pa stong dag smon lam gyis zad par byed par 'gyur/

94b1: rgyas pas thub dbang gi/ dri med 'od zer bkye ba ni// mi g.yo rdo rje can zhes bya// dkyil 'khor chen por zhugs pa yi// rdo rje can dag rab btul ba// gang yin de kun dag byas nas// dkyil 'khor dri med skor bar byed// ngan song /

94b3: nang du zhugs/ / de nas 'jigs pa'i sgra skad kyis// 'gengs shing mig ni glog ltar 'gyu// rig sngags hUM zhes sgrogs pa po// rdo rje 'jigs byed 'jigs byed pa/ bzhin mdzes 'dzum gyis rnam par brgyan// sdigs byed mig rtsa rgod
94b4: gyur cing / stan las langs te phyag 'tshal nA// legs par mchod byas smras pa ni// kye ma skye ba'i phyogs 'joms shing // bskal pa du ma'i dri ma sa la// rig sngags yon tan sgrub byed pa// thub mchog rnams kyis rab tu gsungs//
94b5: de gzigs dge ba du ma brnyes// sangs rgyas blo gros rgyas par 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa' blo gros che// bskal pa gcig tu spyod pas kyang // brgyud mar sangs rgyas kun 'byung zhing // spyod pa du ma 'byung ba yi// yon tan brgya yi spos ldan
94b6: 'di/ thos par spro bar mi nus so// longs spyod rgya mtsho chen po can// byang chub sems mchog dkyil 'khor du// rgyal mchog rnams kyis dbang bskur ba'i/ phyir mi ldog pa'i chos can ldan// 'di thos sangs rgyas spyod pa yi// samra
94b7: can kun gyi sdig pa rnams/ / ma lus rab tu gsal nas ni// blo chen dri ma med par 'gyur// zhi zhing dag byed bkra shis la// rdul med rgyan te zhi bar byed// dge zhing mya ngan thams cad sel// sdug bsngal thams cad nges par 'joms
94b8: dbang byed gsang sngags dam pa ste/ / sa stengs sdig pa thams cad sel// ma smad 'bras bu nges par sbyin// bstan pa yin te sdang ba 'dul// nyes pa byas pa sel ba yin// gzungs 'di gang gis thob gyur de// sangs rgyas rnyed
95a1: pa dka' ba yang / / ring por mi thogs thob par 'gyur// sgrib pa thams cad rab zhi zhing // khyab bdag nyon mongs kun sel ba// gang zhig nyon mongs zhi byed pa'i// gzungs 'di 'chang bar byed pa yis// kun du bzang po nyid
95a2: dang ni/ / lag na rdo rje nyid kyang 'thob// rig sngags 'chang gi bdag po yang / 'di thos pa ni thob par 'gyur// 'jig rten kun na lam me ba// bcom ldan rnam par snang mdzad kyang // dkyil 'khor dam pa gting med pa// 'di ni ji srad
95a3: ma gsan par/ / rab zhi nyon mongs 'dul ba yi// rang 'byung go 'phang ma brnyes te// rnam par dag phyir gsan gyur nas// gas na ma thag tu rnam par dag/ de byar phun sum tshogs pa dang // legs par 'dod pas brjod par bya// gzhan
95a4: gyis mi thub gzungs gsan nas/ / thub pa kun gyis gang brnyes pa// 'khor ba 'dir ni nam du yang // bdud kyi las dang 'khrug med dang // mya ngan med cing 'thab med pa// gzungs la gnas pas thob par 'gyur// gnas kyi dam pa thob
95a5: nas kyang / thub pa drim med pa'i blo// gzigs pa bzang rnams gang gshegs pa'o// bzang 'gro der ni 'gro bar 'gyur// legs pa 'dod pa rnams kyis ni// tshig gi mdo 'di mnyan par gyis// nyon mongs zad par bya ba la// rgyal
95a6: bas gsungs pa'i gzungs 'dis chog/ sdig pa byed cing dge la sdang // sdig pa'i rang bzhin rab 'jungs pa// gang gis thos nas de spong ba// nga yi mngon sum 'byor par 'gyur// sdig pa gzhan yang mi bya zhing // snga ma rnams kyang
95a7: gshegs par bya/ / gzungs mchog 'di yi mthu stobs kyis// sdog pa thams cad 'byang bar 'gyur// tshe rabs gzhan ni stong dag dang // tshe rabs bye ba phrag brgyar yang // sdig pa mi dge gang byas pa// dag 'gyur 'di la the tshom
95a8: med/ / par gyi don chos brgyad dang // de bzhin tshes ni bco lnga la// bsnyen gnas legs par lha blangs la// cho ga bzhin du sangs rgyas mchod// de nas rmongs pa med pa yang // nyon mongs dgra ni rab 'joms shing // shanaH
95b1: khyab dka' rab med pa/ / nyes pazlog pa'i gzungs brjod na// thub pa'i zhal mtha ba' 'ad// 'bar bangs par mthong bar 'gyur// denas tshogs rnams rdzogs pa la// rnal ba'i sras po nyid du 'gyur// 'ad ban
95b2: med la mnga' ba yi/ / yon tan mtha' yas rab rgyas pa// bskal pa bye ba stong du yang // mtha' mi rtogs pa thob par 'gyur// de nas rdo rje 'dzin gyi tshig/ dkyil 'khor dag na gnas rnams kyis// thos nas rgyan
95b3: rnams sna tshogs pa/ / bcom ldan 'das la 'bul bar byed// rdo rje ral gri la sogs pa// lha bdag gsal ba thams cad dang // ri bo ti si'i ri rab la// gnas pa'i rig sngags 'chang rnams dang // de bzhin dkyil 'khor
95b4: chen po na/ / 'khod pa'i rig sngags bachad rnams dang // ma la ya yi bo la// gnas shing rgyan 'bar thogs rnams dang // khyab 'jug lha chen la sogs pa// lha yi bdag po rnams dang na// lag na rdo rje la sogs pa// byang
95b5: chub sems dpa' stobs chen rnams/ / nor bu dpung rgyan rna cha dang // rgyan rnams rab tu g.yo ba'i lus// rab tu bskyod de langs nas ni// sdig bral mnga' bdag rgyal ba la// phyag 'tshal thal mo sbyar byas nas// kun gyis
95b6: sa ya dbang phyug po/ / thub mchog dam pa de la ni// mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad dag gis bstod// mnyam nyid chos te de bzhin nyid// shin tu rtogs pa lam me ba// dul ba brtan pa dri ma sel// dri ma med pa skyon bral ba// thub pa
95b7: sangs rgyas shin du zhi/ / 'jig rten mgon po skye dgu'i bdag/ de bzhin gshegs pa nyon mongs thul// de bzhin rgyal ba rdul bsal ba// ston pa ston mdzad brtan pa ste// sdig pa med pa rdul dang bral// 'jig rten mgon
95b8: mdzad snang mdzad pa/ / dag bzhi bzas gtsang sras// nyon mongs rab bcom pan 'dogs pa// ston pa po ste dri ma sel// spyod tshul dri med tshul bzang ba// zab pa rnam par gnon pa brtan// bcan po thugs brtse rnam
96a1: par rgyal/ / mgon po de bzhin mgon mdzad pa// zhi ba'i bdag nyid zhe sdang bral// bcings pa las grol nges par grol// 'jig rten kun mchog 'khra ba'i sa// bdag gir mi 'dzin dri ma med// ngan song sol pa
96a2: dpal dang ldan/ / dpal mdzad de bzhin phan pa mdzad// mnyam pa med pa dpe med pa// khyab bdag nyon mongs las rnams spong // khengs pa med pa dman med pa// mnyam pa de bzhin mi mnyam mnyam// snang ba brnyes pa snga
96a3: byed med/ / 'jig rten snang mdzad sdig med pa// sgrib pa thams cad spangs pa ste// 'jig rten kun la phan par brtson// dpa' bo zhi bzhi mdzad pa// nyon mongs dgra rnams zad par mad// mnga' bdag thabs byin thabs/
96a4: che ba// sems can kun gyi 'khras lags// don yod rnyed dka' blo dang ldan// rdo rje dkyil 'khor thub par dka'// skyob pa 'jigs sel tshangs pa ste// de bzhin sangs rgyas chos 'dzin pa// dpa' bo chen po 'jigs
96a5: pa med/ / gzugs bzang mtshan rnams gsal ba ste// sum bcu rtsa gnyis mtshan mnga' ba// chos kyi longs spyod rgya mtsho lags// dpe byad bzang po bkod pa yis// spras pa'i bdag nyid ya mtshan ston// dga' ba
96a6: med pa'i ston pa po/ / de bzhin nges pa bde sbyin pa// mthu can yangs pa rgya che ba// bdud bzhi'i stobs rnams sel mdzad pa// brtson chen spro ba che ba ste/ dgyes pa chen po stobs po che// mthu brnyes brtan po chen po ste//
96a7: gnas ldan dbang gis dar ba lags// gsal ba gsung ldan dpe med pa// dag pa stong pa nyid kyis rgyal// rab tu zhi ba mun pa med// blo gros chen po chos 'dzin pa// phun sum tshogs ldan sa chen brnyes// 'dod pa
96a8: rnams ni 'dul mdzad pa/ / dpal mdzad dpal mda' dpal dang ldan// dpal gyis longs spyod shin tu rgyas// bcom ldan legs bsgos sgo bar mdzad// gsung ldan bkra shis rgyal ba'i gnas// mnyam nyid mnyam
96b1: pa nyid mkhyen pa/ / mnyam pa nyid kyis mtshan dpag med// rab tu dgyes pa longs spyod gsal// gzhi bcas sems pa mnyam pa lags// blo dag blo ldan drim spangs// gnas chen brtan par ldan pa ste// rgyas pa
96b2: longs spyod dri ma med/ / thub pa thugs rje'i rgyan mda' ba// bskal pa bzang po 'jigs pa'i skyabs// de bzhin 'jigs med nyon mongs sel// dri med skyon bral longs spyod can// sna tshogs 'od ldan dkyil 'khor
96b3: mdzes/ / sku bzang dge ba'i rim pa mchog/ thugs rje'i 'od ldan 'od bzang ba// mi gnas longs spyod dam pa lags// chos kyi rgyu ste yon tan gnas// rjid 'os mchog gnas 'dis spyod cha// nam mkha' mtshan
96b4: ternam dag blo/ / rin chen gzugs 'dra bkra shis pa// khyu mchog che spyan pardzi ma// rgyal ba skyon gsal shes rab can// shes rab thabs dang ldan pa ste// 'jig rten mi dge kun las 'das// dag par longs spyod bstan
96b5: pa can/ / sa dang stobs dang ye shes bzod// pha rol phyin pa kun la mnga'// ting 'dzin mnyam par longs spyod pa// rnam thar sgro la mngon sum pa// gtong ba sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam// chos chen bde bar 'char ba lags/
96b6: thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul las 'das// spyod yul sgrib pa mi mnga' ba// byang chub sems dpa'i dbang po rgyal// dam pa'i don tshul che ba// shes bya'i yul rnams mtha' dag la// sgrib pa med par 'char ba brnyes/
96b7: rigs chen 'thun par skyes pa ste// de bzhin gshegs pa dge ba'i gnas// khyad par brnyes pa mnyam nyid brnyes// mI mnyam sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam// don chen shin tu mthar phyin pa// nyon mongs bral ba thub
96b8: bar dka'/ / dge sbyong sdig pa spyod mdzad pa// gnod pa med par bde bar 'byin// blo rgya che ba thams cad mkhyen// thos pa'i mtshon cha ma lus gsan// dkon pa bde bar thob 'gyur ba// mnyan pa khyad par yul dang ldan
97a1: 'jig rted thams cad dang mdzad mgon/ / ni gnas mtshan mthub par dkyul// bsam thos ma khyab bsam yas yul// dpe med pa ste dper bya ba// 'od bayang ba dkyis dpal dang ldan/ lags gas
97a2: blo yi stobs kyis 'byung / / mkhas pa zhal bzang bde sbyin pa// rab dgyes 'das pa'i spyod yul can// gsung ba chen po ye shes che// gnas chen bkra shis chen po sde// mchod par gyur pa yul las 'das// bya ba'i
97a3: mtshan nyid med pa po/ / sangs rgyas yul du skyes pa ste// shes bya'i spyod yul rgya che ba// kun mkhyen longs spyod 'bras bu can// 'jig rten dbang 'das spyod yul ba// kun mkhyen yul gyi snang ba ste// thabs mnga' bun
97a4: sum tshogs ldan pa/ / rdzu 'phrul rol pa'i thabs dang ldan// chos kyi gor thabs ston pa po// rab ston yon tan sgrar mdzad pa// spyod pa ma lus 'dul bar mdzad// yongs su rdzogs pa rnam par dag/ sangs rgyas spyod yul
97a5: rnam sangs rgyas/ / bgegs med ma legs byed pa bcom// bdud kyis dregs bsel bar byed// g.yul ngor rnam par rgyal ba brnyes// dpa' bo chen po pham med stobs// theg pa chen po shing rta bcibs// blo chen rgal bar
97a6: dka' ba yi/ / nyon mongs rgya mtsho'i pha rol gshegs// theg pa chen po'i tshul la gnas// thog pa mchog la longs spyod pa// nyan thos 'das pa'i spyod yul can// rang rgyal las kyang 'das pa ste// sangs rgyas sa yi 'bras
97a7: bur gnas/ / gong nas gong du khyad par mkhyen// khyod ni nam mkha'i gnas na bzhugs// bde 'byungs dang zhing rnams kyi// mtshon chen dag la longs par spyod// sangs rgyas dbang po rgyas pa la// mtshan rgya rtsa brgyad kyis
97a8: bstod nas/ / de la lha sogs tshegs rnams kyis// phyag byas mgo smad phyogs gcig 'khod// de nas dkyil 'khor chen po na// gnas pa ma lus chem mer 'khod// thod du rdo rje'i thod 'ching ba// langs nas cod pan rab
97b1: tra g.yos/ / dkyil 'khor mthon po thams cad du// skad dper chen pos yongs kar nas// nor bu'i rgyan ni rnam g.yos zhing // ha ha grags pa'i sgra sgrogs te// kye ma sangs rgyas yon tan che// bskal pa grangs med
97b2: gsum bsags pa/ / byang chub sems stsogs mchog rnams kyis// mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad legs par brjod// kye ma rnyed dang bde 'byung ba// mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad thos nas kyang // gang zhig klog cing rgyal la bstod//
97b3: 'bras bu chen po 'grub par 'gyur// mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad bsngags bcas pa// bcom ldan 'das drung brjod na ni// sgrub dang kun nas nyon mongs dang // sdig pa thams cad dag pa 'thob// mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad mtsho/
97b4: btan na// sgrib pa kun las nges grol zhing // nyon mongs mtha' dag rnam par spong // shes rab chen po nyid du 'gyur// de ni longs spyod chen po dang // bde ba las kyang nyams mi 'gyur// de yi tshe rabs thams cad du//
97b5: blo ldan tshe rabs dran par 'gyur// de nas rdo rje'i thod 'ching ba// yon tan mtha' yas sras de la// bcom ldan bdud las rgyal ba yis// mngon sum gzigs nas bka' stsal pa// rgyal bI sa 'di zhi ba ste// nga rgyal la sogs nyon mong/
97b6: 'joms// 'jig rten bde ba kun las 'das// de bzhin gshegs bde mngon du phyogs// gzhan gyis mi tshugs gzungs dang ni// mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad nyan byed pa// de dag rnam dag bdag nyid de// sems can kun la bde 'dod pa
97b7: lan cig thos pa tsam gyis kyang / / de dag sa chen 'bras bur gnas// ring por mi thogs dgar 'gyur na// 'chad stsogs lta la ci zhig smos// de phyir rtag tu rab bsgrims la// brtan du bde ba 'dod pa yis// yon tan brgya mtsho lan
97b8: ba'i gzungs/ / mnyan par bya zhing bcad par bya// gang zhig nang par langs nas brjod// bdag nyid kyis kyang bton na ni// de yi don kun 'grub 'gyur la/ gnod pa dang yang zad mi 'gyur// 'di ni yon tan kun gyi spos// dge ba bun
98a1: sum tshogs sbyin pa/ / kun mkhyen bla med 'bras bu'i mchog/ bde ba byung thob par byed pa yin// 'bras bu 'byor pa ci yang rung // thob par mi 'gyur dogs pa med// kun mkhyen go 'phar thob gyur nas// dpe med gnas
98a2: su 'gro bar 'gyur/ / de ni dge zhing 'bras bur ldan// sangs rgyas sa yi 'bras bu sbyin// yid du 'ong zhing yon tan ldan// snying rje dri ma med sbyin pa// 'di ni mnyam pa nyid kyi mdo// 'jig rten kun nas dga' ba ste// 'jig rten
98a3: kun gyi bde ba byung ba/ / 'di dang 'dra ba gang yang med// ston pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa rdzogs s+ho// / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi mtshan
98a4: brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo// na maHsarba bud d+ha b+ho d+hi satwa nA~M// sa man ta a mo g+ha a pra ti ha ta sha sa na nAM
98a5: na ma Ar+ya a ba lo ki te shwa rA ya/ ma hA bo d+hi satwA ya/ badz+ra satwA ya/ badz+ra bi bu lA ya/ pa da ma sam b+ha bA ya/ ba da ma yo na ye/ tad+ya thA/ oM trI ka ra/ shrI ka ra/ pra b+ha ka ra/ badz+ra satwe/ badz+ra sa ma b+ha bA/ pad ma sa ma b+ha ba/ ba da ma
98a6: sA ga ra/ pad ma go tsa ra/ ba ra d+harma hA kA ru Ni kaM/ kA ru Ni sa maM b+ha ba/ hU~M hU~M/ d+ha ra d+ha ra/ da ra dar/ ba ra ba ra/ ma hA kA ru Ni ka ma hA shud d+ha satwe swA hA// de nas phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis phyag g.yas
98a7: pa brkyang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi mgo bo la byugs nas/ bka' stsal pa/ yon tan rin po che'i phung po khyod kyis gzungs sngags 'di bshad pas sems can rnams la sadra/
98a8: rgyas 'byung ba'i chos bstan pa legs so legs so// 'di thos pa tsam gyis kyang sems can rnams shin du rnam par dag par byed pa'o// gang la la nyan pa dang / 'char ba dang / klog pa dang / kun chub par byed pa des ni yon tan
98b1: phun sum tshogs pa thams cad dang / dag pa'i mchog kyang thob par 'gyur ro// de nas lha'i dbang po dbang phyug chen po dpag tshad 'bum phrag du mar khyab cing 'jig rten gsum po kun du rgyas ko lta ste/ 'khor dang bcas
98b2: pa dang / rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor du 'dus pa'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis mgo bo btud nas 'phags pa sman ras gzigs dbang phyug pa'id jug pa gos partse ba zhes bya ba'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pas mngon par
98b3: bstod pas yi dbang phyug rdo rje dkyil 'khor ba/ / srid gsum ma lus yon tan chen po'i bdag/ dri med skyon bral zla ba'i dkyil 'khor can// snying rjes khyab pa'i dkyil 'khor rgya che ba// rab dga' rab dgyes rab tu ston pa po//
98b4: bskal pa bzang po rnam thar zhi ba'i mchog/ shin tu rnam dag yon tan chen po'i bdag/ rnam dag du mar grags pa'i me tog thod// rab mchog srid gsum dag gis mig gcig pa// mchog sbyin 'gro ba kun gyi 'byor
98b5: ba mdzes/ / dpag med pas kyang dpag med bskal bar 'gyung// skyabs dang yid 'phrog dag cing gsal bar mdzad// nor bu'i thod can rdo rje las byung ba// srid gsum gcig pa dpa' bo pad ma'i spyan// thos pa'i rgya mtsho sems can
98b6: kun zas dpa'/ / 'gro ba thams cad rnam par grol mdzad mchog/ snyan cha 'gul zhing par ma dag pa bsdams// dbang phyug bde gshegs bzhugs pa'i thor tshugs can// tshul bzang yon tan rkyen du 'tsham pa'i gzugs// 'jig
98b7: pa'i rlung chen 'chub pa'i mtshon cha can/ / dge ba'i rgyu ste dam pa stsol ba'i rgyu// tshul gyi longs spyod pa de chen mchog gi rgya// dkyil 'khor mchog gi spyod yul rgyu gcig pa// srid gsum sgrol ba'i zab pa gcig pu lags// dkyil 'khor
98b8: mchog gi rgyan te sdig med pa/ / gser mdog 'od rgyan rten du gyur pa ste// mnyam pa nyid kyis mi mnyam mtshungs par 'gyur// sa brnyes 'od zer rgyas pa rgyan phreng mda'// chen po'i che ba thog ma med pa ste// snga ma mun pa bsal cing
99a1: nyon mongs med/ / dge bas dag pa spyod yul rnam par dag/ tshul gyis dkyil 'khor yangs shing rnam par dag/ srid gsum dbang phyug pad ma las byung ba// srid gsum bde can yangs pa'i dbang phyug ste// dbang
99a2: phyug mi g.yo rnal 'byor mkhas pa po/ / de bzhin gshegs pa chen po rab mchog yangs// nor bu'i rgyan gyi rdo rje rgyan du thogs// pad mas brgyan pa lhun po las byung ba// dge snoslong yon tan chen po'i snod gcig pa// bde la
99a3: longs spyod rnam 'dren chen po'i bdag/ smon lam rgya chen rgya mtsho ldan pa ste// 'gro ba srid par lhung ba grol mdzad pa// sa dang mnyam pa thams cad gzigs par mdzad// bskal bzang bskal pa stong gi snang ba po// rdo rje mchog sa/
99a4: sgeg pa'i dkyil 'khor can// yon tan rnam grangs khyab par dkyil 'khor ba// dge ba'i mtshan nyid dpa' bo'i rtsel mnga' ba// de bzhin nyid chos ro mkhyen spyod yul can// cod pan thig le dmar po'i dkyil 'khor ldan// lha chen
99a5: brgya mda' sum bcu gsum bdag dbang / / lha dang lha min dbang byas rnams kyis btud// brtson 'grus brgya dang ldan zhing rtsal stong mnga'// bsod nams brgya mnga' mtshon cha brgya 'chang ba// pad ma brgya pa pad ma nyid las
99a6: byung / / dkyil 'khor brgya yi dbus na mdzes pa ste// chos brgya ldan pa mchog stong ston pa po// sangs rgyas stong phrag mang pos yongs bstod pa// bskal pa rab 'byam mang por mkhas pa ste// dkyil 'khor mang po dag na da
99a7: baba'i sku 'jig rten 'das pa'i mthu mnga' ston pa po/ / rgya chen dri med dkyil 'khor na bzhugs pa// rab dga' bsgyings pa 'thor mdzad me tog thod// na bza' dang dkar la mnabs 'od mdzad pa// thugs kyi dkyil 'khor thugs rdzas
99a8: brgyan pa las/ / cha phrang gser mdzad mtha' yas zad mi shes// dpa' bo nyi ma'i 'od zer ba rgya mnga' ba// nor bu'i dkyil 'khor zla 'dra 'od gsal zhing // nyi mas kha phye pad ma mchog bsdams pa// me tog mtshon cha thogs pa'i/
99b1: lha zhes grags// gtsug phud gsum pa tshangs sras skye dgu'i bdag/ btsun rigs mchog ste rigs chen nang du skyes// rang gi rigs gsal dbang chen dkyil 'khor ba// pad ma bzang po'i rigs mchog thig las mtshan//
99b2: spyan bzang dge ba'i lha rnams rten gyur pa// gsang sngags mang po 'dzin pa'i dbang phyug po// tshegs chen 'dun ma 'dus pa'i mnga' bdag lags// spyan gsum dag gis dkyil 'khor mdzes gyur pa// ka la bing ka'i skad
99b3: kyis sdang ba 'dul/ / mnga' dang ru gzhu stobs chen mtshon chabasnams// stobs kyi lha ste stobs dang brtson pas 'dul// rgyan rnams sna tshogs legs par spras pa ste// rgyal ba rig sngags 'chang ba mang pos bstod// tshogs mchod
99b4: dag byed rnams kyis rab baspyod pa/ / chu srin 'dzin khri'i 'jigs las rab grol mdzad// gzugs mda' mnga' zhing bde skyid rab sbyin pa// lha yul 'gro ba'i khyad par dkyil 'khor can// mtshungs med pas kyang mtshungs med mthu rtsal/
99b5: mnga'// stabs gshegs yon tan tshe mchog 'od zer ldan// 'jig rten nang na mkhas pa spyan ras gzigs// sa bzhi'i dkyil 'khor dbus kyi dkyil 'khor can// 'od zer mang po stong phrag zad mi shes// nyon mongs rdul rnams tham
99b6: cad sel mdzad pa/ / mtha' dang bral ba kun du gzigs pa ste// rab zhi kun las 'phags pa'i spyod yul can// don dang tshul la sems can gcig dpa' ba// theg pa bzang po 'dzin pa'i nyi ma lags// dul dang sbyin dang rgal
99b7: la dad pa brnyes/ / skye dgu rnams kyi dri ma ma lus bcom// blo gros bzang po rab dgyes ston pa po// bde ldan gos rgyan yang ba sna tshogs can// bcom ldan 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa med par mdzad// rtag tu dge ba kun mochog ston
99b8: pa po/ / rgyal bas gsungs pa'i rnam thar brnyes pa'i blo// bde ba longs spyod cher 'byung dri ma med// zhal gyi dkyil 'khor rgyas shing dri med pa// mi dang sred med brgya byin lag pa'i mchog/ 'jig rten mang po gzigs pa 'dabang phyug
100a1: pa/ / stobs dang rigs dang mthu stobs che ba lags// sangs rgyas mtshungs shing chos mchog rin chen ma chungs// dge 'dun mtshungs shing chags bral thub par dka'// khyad par gsum 'phags rin chen mchog chen sa
100a2: khyab bdag nyon mongs rnam gsum rdul bsal ba/ / rdo rje sems mchog khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// pad ma dri med phyag gi dbus bsnams pa// thor tshugs can la gzugs ldan cod pan thogs// spyi bo 'od dpag med rgyas khyod phyag
100a3: 'tshal/ / de nas bcom ldan rang byung mun sel ba// chen sgra ltar brtan pas bka' stsal pa// mchog chen rdo rje gla la bstod pa yi// ming brgya rtsa brgyad skyon sel legs pa mang // dza ste la la rtag tu dge mchog 'dod// spyan ras gzin
100a4: dbang la ni bstod byed pa/ / des ni ring por mi thogs yon tan gyi// longs spyod mchog chen chos na thob par 'gyur// mi ni gang zhig rtag tu 'dis bstod pa// spyan ras gzigs dbang dam pa sbyin par byed// sdig pa rnams kyang de la
100a5: 'byung mi 'gyur/ / 'dod pa gang yin pa de blag de yis 'thob// da ni sdig pa'i dri mas mi gos te// lam bsrang bzang pos dmigs te 'gro bar 'gyur// srid gsum skyabs 'os gcig bu pade ma skyes// de 'drar chos kyi mchog la
100a6: spyod par 'gyur/ / de ltar ming gi khyad par grub 'dod cing // gang zhig rtag du bde ba 'dod pa yis// 'gro kun skye dgu'i bdag po spyan ras gzigs// pad ma las byung rtag tu bstod par gyis// bcom ldan 'das bla ma 'phags pa
100a7: sbyin ras gzigs dbang phyug gi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa rdzogs s+ho/ / / 'phags pa byams pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
100a8: ba~M byams pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' byams pas rang ga snying po smras pa/ na ma sna yang d+hoka nA/ sarba rba thA ga ta nA~M/ sh+tsa g+sa mos sa/ su ru su ra/ d+ha ra d+ha ra/ mahA d+har/ tsar tsar/ ma hA tsa ra/ b+ha raSh+Ta
100b1: mahA b+ha ra/ kas pakas pa/ ma hAgs pa/ b+hUs twA s+pha raN d+harma a pra/ sA gar swA hA// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// kyem gzungs chen mo 'don yon tan chab ste mthar yas par
100b2: khyab pa/ bskal pa bye ba thag mang po yang shin du thos pa dka' ba/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba thams cad ston pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa grangs med pa 'jig rten gyi khams tha daji snyed kyis bsnyen bkur mdzad mdzad pa/ sgrib pa dang /
100b3: sdug bsngal ba dang / 'khrug pa dang / rmi la ma ngan pa dang / lhas ngan pa thams cad las thar bar byed pa/ sems can gyi khams mtha' yas mu med pa yongs su thar bar byed pa ste shin du dkon pa'o// de nas rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor
100b4: 'khor lha dang lha ma yin du bcas pa/ nor bu'i cod pan gyis bsgyings pa/ rgyan phreng rab tu g.yas pa rnams kyis spyi bor thal mo sbyar nas byang chub sems dpa'i mchog 'phags pa byams pa la mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad kyis
100b5: mngon par bstod pa/ / dpa' bo chen po thabs brnyes pa// rgyal 'tshab mi yi bdag po ste// 'jig rten bdag po rnam par gsal// dar pa chen po mngon par rgyas// tshan chen stobs ldan che ba ste// de bzhin yangs shing rdul dang bral//
100b6: dbang chen rtse ltar 'od ldan pa// sa yi dbang phyug rnam par gnon// rgyal chen mtshon cha brgya pa ste// mtshon cha chen po'i rdo rjes mtshon// yon tan 'od brgyas bsgyings pa ste// nor bu'i rna cha'i rgyan thogs pa// srid gsum dag na
100b7: sba ba'i sku/ / rgya mtsho lta bu'i spyod yul can// lhun po zla 'byin te sa yi// rtsa nas dkyil 'khor 'char ba po// dkyil 'khor chen po longs spyod pa// rab tu dga' ba de bzhin des// yongs su dga' ldan chen po'i lha// tsha ba
100b8: la rnams kun gyis mchog/ sangs rgyas bdud rgyud rgyas mdzad cing // sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor rgyan dang ldan// sangs rgyas longs spyod longs par spyod// sangs rgyas bstan pa ston pa po// ti se zla 'byin bzhin du yang /
101a1: sa yi dbang phyug bde mdzad pa// pad ma 'dab stong rtse mo can// rdo rje'i pad ma legs par skyes// chos kyi longs spyod longs par spyod// sa dang mnyam par thub par dka'// snang bar byed pa 'byung ba po// srid gsum
101a2: ye shes nyi ma lags/ / gtso bo chen po cher grags pa// seng ge chen po stobs po che// cha lugs chen po zhal che ba// skye bo ngan dang sdug bsngal 'dul// rdo rje bya ru bai dUr+ya// nor bu'i dbu thod rgyan du thogs// byi ru gser gyi/
101a3: bcal bkram la// sku chen zhabs kyi stabs kyis gshegs// zhal mdangs nyi ma du ma'i gzi// lcang lo cod pan dbu thod can// rig sngogs 'chang brgyas zhabs la btud// rjed par bya ba rnams kyis mchod// nor bu brgya 'gul 'od
101a4: zer gyis/ / brang gi phyogs rnams dag par byas// cod pan can te 'od 'tsher ba// nyi ma bye ba brgya 'od ldan// rin chen sna tshogs mchog bkram zhing // dri med dkyil 'khor rab tu 'phro// rlung gis ma lus bskyod pa yi// 'bar ba
101a5: chen po'i lta ba can/ / 'od zer mang pos phog pa yi// phan pa'i thabs ni rab ston pa// brjid pa'i tshul gyis bzhad pa yi// 'od kyis zhal gsal rnga yab bskyod// dpung rgyan 'od zer spel mar bkod// mtshon bris shin tu
101a6: mdzes par 'char/ / lhun po phrad cing 'khrugs pa ltar// ha ha zhes pa'i sgra chen sgrogs// rdo rje chen po rtse mo can// shin du dga' mdzad bde sbyin pa// byams pa'i dkyil 'khor go char bgos// brtsan pa kun las rnam par
101a7: rgyal/ snying rje'i stobs las byung ba ste// mtshon cha chen po shin du 'bar// byams pa byams pa'i rtog pa can// kun nas sba ba'i dkyil 'khor pa// ma pham thub med dag pa ste// sangs rgyas cha lugs mnyam med che// byams
101a8: pa'i snying po snying po che/ / byams pa'i pad ma las byung ba// rdo rje 'chang chen rdo rje can// rdo rje'i bstan pa'i dkyil 'khor ba// rig sngags 'chang ba rnams kyis btud// de bzhin bsnyen cing bstod pa po// grub pa chen po
101b1: rig sngags grub/ / rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor mdzes par mdzad// thams cad grub mdzad grub pa po// sangs rgyas gdung gi sdong chen lags// gsang sngags chen po'i rnam par nges// mdo sde'i bkod pa'i mdo sdung ba// nges
101b2: gyur nges pa'i 'od sgron gyis/ / sdang bas dri ma sal bar mdzad// 'bar ba rtsa dmar 'od snang ba// dkyil 'khor dkar po che ba ste// gzhung dang 'thun pa'i chos dbyings dang // nye bar gyur cing shin tu des// skr-i tA swAtA'i
101b3: bdag po mchog/ 'od zer ba de legs bde ba mdzad// stobs chen 'chang ba bkra shis pa// nyi ma 'dra ste snyoms pa lags// bstod byed rgyal ba'i longs spyod ldan// mkha' ltar dri med spyod yul can// dpa' ba
101b4: rdo rjes 'joms par mdzad/ / rdo rje chen po rab sgrub pa// sgrub pa po ste rtsod pa med// dkyil 'khor ldan pa rdo rje ston// rlung chen shugs kyis bskyod pa yi// g.yo dang 'brug sgrogs sgra ldan pa// sangs rgyas spyod yu
101b5: pad ma ste de bzhin nyid kyi mtsho las skyes/ / mngon shes chen po mngon shes brnyes// khyab bdag sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam// de nas sa yi dbang phyug po// byams pa'i dkyil 'khor byams pa la// bstod
101b6: nas kun mkhyen gnod bral ba/ / thub pa nyi mas bka' stsal pa// kye ma ming brgya rtsa brgyad mchog/ ming gi yon tan 'od ldan pa// bde dang phun sum tshogs sgrub pa// thabs chen bla na med pa ste// ming brgya rtsa brgyad
101b7: 'di dag ni/ / 'jig rten kun gyi bde bskyed pa// 'di ni bton pa tsam gyis kyang // sdig pa thams cad dag par 'gyur// sdig pa dag la rgyal ba yi// byams pa'i bstod pa'i gnas po la// ming rgya rtsa brgyad dam pa 'dis
101b8: mi ni la la gang bstod pa/ / de la lha la sogs kun dang // lag na rdo rje stobs chen rnams// rtag pa nyid du sdug bsngal kun// gtan du bsal cing brtson par byed/ gang zhig ming brgya rtsa brgyad mchog/ myur du
102a1: du 'don pa'i ma de ni/ / sangs rgyas sa yang thob 'gyur te// 'di la the tsom yod med do// nang par stsal nas langs nas ni// gang zhig byams pa'i sems kyis bstod// de la byams pa rtogs pa yi// byams pa
102a2: bde legs byed par 'gyur/ / de phyir dri ma thams cad sel byed cing // sdig 'joms yon tan thams cad skyed pa dang // de bzhin 'jig rten sdug bsngal sel ba yi// ming brgya rtsa brgyad ched du dag par lhogs// 'phags
102a3: pa byams pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa rdzogs s+ho/ / // 'phags pa nam mkha'i snying po'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa// 'phags pa nam mkha'i snying po zhal
102a4: ras rgya che zhing spyan gyi 'od 'phro bas nam mkha'i dkyil dri zhim par mdzad pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ / nam mkha'i spyod yul can sa'i dkyil 'khor thams cad snang bar mdzad pa la phyag 'tshal lo// oM swa sti ka mA la
102a5: kri bo bu la sa ma~M b+ha ba/ d+harma d+harma go tsa ra swA hA// gzungs 'di brjod ma thag tu ngan song dang ngan 'gro thams cad ni rab tu zhi bar 'gyur// sa yang g.yos par gyur// rnga bo che dag gi sgra yang grag par 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams
102a6: cad kyis kyang legs so zhes bya ba byin no/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyis bka' stsal pa// kye 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams nam mkha'i snying po'i snying po dkyil 'khor
102a7: mngon sum pa rnams kyi swA hA/ mchog gi gzungs 'byung bar shin tu dka' ba// bsod nams chen po/ sdig pa dang nyon mongs pa thams cad sreg pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis/ rin po che'i phung por gyur pa
102a8: 'di nyon cig dang / 'di thos pas dri ma med par 'gyur zhing legs par 'khrus byas par 'gyur la shin du rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// pad ma lta bur 'gyur te// 'khor gyi 'dam gyis mi gos so// nyi ma lta bur 'gyur te/ sems can
102b1: thams cad snang bar byed do/ / zla ba lta bur 'gyur te/ sems can thams cad rab tu sim par byed do// nam mkha' lta bur gyur te/ ngan song gi sdug bsngal thams cad kyis mi gos so// sa gzhi lta bur gyur te//
102b2: mthon dman med do// lhun po lta bur 'gyur te/ sems can thams cad kyis bskyod par mi nus so// thar pa lta bur 'gyur te/ bde ba dang sdug bsngal gyis mi gos so// de la sogs pa yon tan stong phrag bzas pa tshad ma grangs
102b3: med pa dag thob par 'gyur te/ / nyan pa dang 'chang ba dang / klog pa dang / rjod pa dang / ston pa tsam dang / bzlas brjod byas pa tsam gyis gang ci yang rung ste/ de'i 'dod pa dang / smon pa dang / re ba de dag 'grub par 'gyur ro// bzlas brjod byas
102b4: pa tsam gyis kyang char ches pa dang / char mi 'bab pa dang / sdad pas dkrugs pa dang / mi nad dang / rmi lam ngan pa dang / gnod pa 'byung ba dang / 'jigs pa'i dus dang / 'chi ba dang / chom rkun dang / dgon pa dang / g.yul 'gyed pa dang
102b5: gcan zan dang / mu ge'i sdug bsngal rnams las yongs su srung bar byed la// bde ba dang 'byor pa dang / ci 'dod pa dang / cil dag pa thams cad kyang 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas 'khor de dag thams cad kyis ha ha zhes ca tsa
102b6: dang gzha gton te/ sgra ring zhes byas nas gos dang rgyan sna tshogs bskyod de/ snying nas phyag 'tshal nas byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la dbang byed pa 'phags pa nam mkha'i snying po'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i bsngag pa
102b7: brgya mtsho'i bstod pa yang dag par brjod pa/ / nam mkha'i snying po'i srid gsum sems can mchog/ 'byor ldan blo gros rin chen rgya mtsho mda'// sems can dag pa bla med rin chen mchog/ thar pa'i sa bon 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal
102b8: sel/ / kun mkhyen tshul mkhyen legs dang legs min mkhyen// thar mkhyen chos mkhyen bde dang mi bde mkhyen// lam mkhyen gces mkhyen dge dang mi dge mkhyen// dus mkhyen dge mkhyen stobs dang stobs min mkhyen/ 'gro
103a1: mchog chos mchog sems can yon tan mchog/ lam mchog sngags mchog tshul dang tshul min mchog/ rgyan mcho chos mchog 'dzin dang 'dzin min mchog/ dag mchog rtogs mchog btsog da ma/
103a2: mchog/ zhi rab snying rje'i rab ste 'khor gyi rab/ 'od rab thar pa'i rab ste rten gyi rab/ rgya rab sngags kyi rab ste thugs brtse'i rab mnyam rab sems can rab ste gsum rig rag legs sgron mchog sgron stobs dang
103a3: stobs mamini sgron/ / thar sgron rigs sgron rgyal dang rgyal min sgron/ dge sgron gzi sgron nor bu'i 'od kyi sgron/ rgyu skar zla ba'i rgyan las shar ba'i sgon// mchog 'od yon tan kun gyi 'od zer 'od// legs 'od thar pa'i pho brang
103a4: rten gyi 'od/ / 'od chen gti mug rab tu 'byed pa'i 'od// rdo rje'i 'od 'bar bde ba'i 'od 'char ba// rdo rje'i dbang po 'dren dbang sems can dbang // rin chen 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgyan dbang po// rgyal dbang rgyal ba'i stobs
103a5: rgun tshad med dbang / / dpa' bo rig sngags 'chang dbang sring gsum dbang // rdo rje bzang po rdo 'od rdo rje 'bar// rdo rje sems dpa' rdo rje 'bar bas brgyan// rdo rje 'od can rdo 'dzin rdo rje drag/ rdo rje rgya chen rdo rje rab mchog dbang //
103a6: na bza' sngo zhing sku yi cha lugs sngo// sku mdog sngo zhing sngo ba'i 'od kyis brgyan// ral gri rdo 'jebs sngo zhing brtan pa bsnams// mkha' sngo gzhal med khang 'bar nang na bzhugs// lha zhal dri med shin tu mi bzada' bar//
103a7: rab tu drag la 'ad zer 'phro zhing 'gyu// sdigasel rdul ltar 'a khrug byed phreng mchog can// glog gi stobs kyis snang bas bsgegs la brtan// ral gri mtshon thogs dbang ldan mthu stobs mchog/ rdo yi mtshon thogs
103a8: mda' dang mdung thung 'jigs/ / 'khor lo'i mtshon thogs bcibs pa ri dang 'phrul// gsal shing mtshon thogs bgags kyi stobs 'joms pa// bde 'byung 'jig rten gsum bdag rdo rje'i dbyug/ sku rnams thams cad
103b1: nyi ma'i 'od kyis brgyan/ / grags pa'i rigs su 'byung bas rgyal po mdzad// mu tig phreng bas bsgegs shing mdzes par bgyis// sku mdzes brnyes shing phun sum tshogs pa brnyes// rab 'byam mchog brnyes sa la 'jug pa pa
103b2: mthu stobs lhag pa brnyas shing grub pa rnyes la/ / dag pa gsum gyi stobs brnyes mthu brnyes pa/ bde 'dren zhib 'dren cing 'di 'dzin pa// cha lugs gsal mtshag dar ba chen po 'dren// byams 'dren nyim 'dren cing skye ba 'dren/
103b3: legs 'dren zhing gi stobs 'dren snying rje can// dri ma cha lugs gsal ba cha lugs 'bar// rnam grags bsgeg pas grags pa'i bdan can// 'gro ba'i skabs 'byed 'jug dang ldog pa ma khyen// longs spyod gsal bar ston pa'i
103b4: sems kyis 'jug/ sku dmar sku 'thon sku mdzes sku bzang ba// sku bser sku dkar dar ba chen po'i sku// sku rol rdo rje sku mda' spyan legs su// rigs sku reg sngags 'chang ba rin chen bsnams// gtsug gi nor bu gtsug
103b5: can cod pan mchog/ cod pan can te chos 'dzin rdo rje mchog/ dpal 'dzin rin chen dam pa 'chang ba'i mchog/ sngags gzhi phyag rgya 'chang ba phun sum tshogs// rab mdzes mkha' la gshegs shing rab tu rgyu// srid
103b6: gsum nyi ma gcig tu 'od stong mnga'/ / ri rtser 'char ba bdal legs bkra shis pa// yon tan mthu stobs khyad par rnam par grags// nor bu chen po nor spug nor bu'i 'od// nyi ma'i nor bu tshul spyod nor bu 'bar// yid bzhin
103b7: nor bu 'gro kun mgon gcig pu/ / nam mkha'i dkyil na nor bu'i gcig snang ba// sems can rnam dag yangs shing rnam par grags// srid gsum srungs ma gcig pu rgyal sras mchog/ zhi ba rab tu zhi ba skyabs 'os stag/
103b8: skye dbu'i bdag pa bad byung ba ma skyes// kun nas 'od bzang lags pa shad ces mnga' ba// dang pa legs bshad rang rdul lags pashad phyag// thobazang 'od bzang ba de ldan ste/ gnas bzang // ma las rab na
104a1: mchog gi chos dang ldan/ / zhi mdzad rgyal 'byung bde ba 'byung ba'i gnas// 'od kyi 'byung gnas bde mdzad dbang du mdzad// legs 'byung shes rab 'byung gnas stobs skyed pa// snying rje'i 'byung gnas blo bzang rnam
104a2: grangs mdzad/ / rnam grol ngas grol shin tu grol ba'i blo// blo yangs rnam par bkram shing rnam par grags// kun tu longs spyod sgo ste blo yi mchog/ blo gros brtan pa dkon mchog gsum las bsgrubs// sangs rgyas pad pa
104a3: 'dab rgyas 'dra ba'i zhal/ / dag cing spyan yangs cha lugs yid du 'thad// snying po gsal ba'i snying por brtan zhing dul// ngo bo nyid kyis rgyun brnyas rab gsal ba// spyan zur mda' ni rab tu gtang legs pa// 'jigs med
104a4: zhal ras ston gyi zla ba 'dra/ / mdung thung brgya yi mtshon mchog mtshon cha rdzogs// drag po 'dzags pa sdig sel gsum las skyes// rab dul mkhas pa 'grogs dga' 'dris par sla// rab tu drag pa gnyen rab gser mdog can//
104a5: lha chen bde byed gsal shing phyag na bsnams// spyan gsum rig pa gsum ldan me gsum sel// 'dod bzad me tog mtshon thogs me tog mda'// na bza' bzang man pas g.yas 'phen chabs char 'phen// legs
104a6: bris sna tshogs mtshon cha sna tshogs mda'/ / na bza' sna tshogs sna tshogs rgyan gyi dpal// zhal ras zla ba 'od zer rgyas pa 'dra// zhal mdangs bstan pas 'jig rten kun 'byor mdzad// bshad pa nyi mI 'od zer rab 'jebs
104a7: mda'/ / zhal mdangs rgya mtsho gas la mdzad lam me ba// dbang chen rdo rje'i thog legs 'jigs pa'i sgra// rdo rje drag po nor bu g.yo ba 'dzin// sgra snyan snang bar mdzad pa'i mthu dang ldan// blo gros chen po blo gros rna ba'i mchog
104a8: rgyan 'dzin dpal 'dzin rin chen zhal dang ldan/ / rgyu dang mi rgyu 'gro ba kun gyi gnas// de bzhin gshegs pa mgon sras phreng ba bzang // stobs chen 'jig rten blo gros ngo bo nyid// skye dgu'i bdag po bka' lung mnyam zhing
104b1: brtags/ / mi yi mnga' bdag mtho ris skyed pa'i rgyu// sbyar 'dra 'dod pa'i mnga' dang rdo rje can// mthu stobs mnga' zhing spyan bzang sdug par ldan// ston par bzang po stong nyid rab lam gyi stegs// gces gsum 'phel
104b2: pa'i rgyu la 'jug pa mdzad/ / brtan po rgyu la dang tA+es gyur pa// dkyil 'khor dam pa kun gyi slob dpon lags// gcig pu skya dgu'i dkyil 'khor cho ga mkhyen// rnam par snang mdzad zhing gi gnas nas skyes// dbang bskur brnyes
104b3: shing sa bcur legs par gnas/ / gnas chen son pa mchog gnas gcig pu lags// skye dgu rnams kyi nyon mongs sel ba dang // sdig 'joms mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad 'di thos nas// bde gshegs sras mchog
104b4: sra zhig 'don byed pa/ / 'jig rten zla ba gcig shar bzhin du snang // nam mkha'i snying po sems can gcig pu yi// mdun 'dug nang bar bstod pa 'di brjod gang // de ni srid gsum sems can mchog 'gyur zhing /
104b5: dri ma'i gnas kun las kyang thar bar 'gyur// g.yul dang 'thab rtsod shin tu mi bzad dang // mu ge'i gnod pa min byung ba na// mkhas pa su zhig sngar langs dad bskyed nas// nam mkha'i snying po la ni bstod
104b6: byed pa/ / de ni 'jigs pa'i 'byung gnas thams cad dang // sdug bsngal 'byung 'dren sdig pa rnams las grol// des ni zhi mchog mchog bde kun gnas dang // bde ba rgya chen nges par thob par 'gyur// bde
104b7: 'thob longs spyod 'phel bar bya ba'am/ / rgyal srid 'thob dang byad gzugs nor 'thob dang // rigs 'thob yon tan kun gyi gzhi bsgrub phyir// gton na 'grub 'gyur 'di la the tsom med// de phyir ji ste rtag
104b8: tu 'dod bde kun/ / 'dod na 'gro ba kun la gcig dpa' ba// nam mkha'i snying po srid gsum mgon po la// rtag tu brtan cing bsngags kyang bstan par bgyi// 'phags pa nam mkha'i snying po'i mtshan
105a1: brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa/ rdzogs s+ho// // 'phags pa kun du bzang po'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
105a2: po snying rje chen po kun du bzang po nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu rab 'byams ma lus pa dang mnyam pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi chos kyi snang ba bsal ba brnyes pa/ sa'i dkyil 'khor kun du 'phros pa'i sku tha dad pa med cing dus gsum gyi sku
105a3: mnyam nyid brnyes pa/ gzugs sna tshogs can// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i mchog dang / rab mchog dam pa sbyin pa/ yon tan chen po'i skus kun du mnga' mdzad pa la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas de'i

110a1: mdzad pa/ / bzod pa dka' ba reg mi bzod// sdig dang bgegs rnams gcod mdzad pa// drag po chen po rdo rje khro// skyel byed drag po skyel bar mdzad// gting dpag dka' ba ring du gshegs// rin chen rgya mtsho

110a4: 'gyed / / grol mdzad mgon po ston pa po// rab mchog rab mchog rnams kyi mchod// mgrin chen mgrin pa'i mdog sngo pa// mgur bzang zhal bzang dam pa lags// cod pan chen po rdo rje'i 'od// phun sum tshogs
