110a8: mdzes shing stobs bskyed sna tshogs stobs// dga' ba skyed pa dga' bar mdzad// dkon mchog gsum po 'dzin pa'i mchog/ lha chen dpa' bo chen po ste// brtan po dpa' bo lham ma pa// bad ba chen po 'tshang ba
110b1: cang / / byung ba rnas ma / na tshams thod pa sa// reg sngags 'chang ba 'tshogs dga' ba// pangs can pa byug ngabya// pa ga las zung ba ma 'amag/ nag pa can po 'byung sa//
110b2: chen thogathog chen po ste// rlung chen bzhad mo 'byung ba dang // rdo rje'i mtshon cha brgya rdzogs pa// rdul por thab dka' brtson pa ste// 'thung po chen po'i tshogs kyi rje// zhi ba dbang po rdo rje'i mtshon// brag gi rtse mo rnam par
110b3: 'gems/ / rgyal ba'i sras po gzugs che ba// rdo rje yi ni dkyil 'khor brgyan// rdo rje'i lcags mangs sreg mdzad pa// rdo rje'i 'das ni rnam par sbyong // rdo rje don yod rdo rje dbang // rdo rje bzang po rdo rje'i rtsal// ye shes
110b4: dag pa theg pa che/ / thabs bsnyes snying rje chen po lags// rdo rje chen po ched mo can// spyan bzang rnam par gzigs pa po// rdo rje dril bu rnam dag spyan// mdzad po sdug pa dam tshig mkhyen// rdo rje chen po mgon po pa// rdo rje
110b5: sa 'og 'jigs par mdzad/ / rdo rje chen po gad rgyangs sgron// me tog chun po 'od gsal ba// dag pa zas gtsang sras kyi sras// nges pa skal bzong gtsang ba lags// sna tshogs can te lha kun mchog/ rdo rje'i dpung gi
110b6: dkyil 'khor ldan/ / rdo rje'i gtsug sdug shes rab can// rdo rje'i bkod pa rab tu mdzes// mdzes pa shin tu rnam par dag/ bskal pa'i rlung chen lta bu lags// dpa' bo bsang ba chen po 'chang // rig sngags 'chang
110b7: gi mchog gis rjes/ / gas rab po ste gsang ba gsung // skyes pa pad med tshogs dga' ba// rdo rje thog thog sgra chen sgrogs// rdo rje'i sgrog ste rnam par 'joms// rdo rje'i lcags kyu gyes pa che// rdo rje 'bar ba che 'bar ba/
110b8: norabs spras pa'i na bza' gsol// spos dang me tog phreng gis brgyan// dbu yi snyan chagadub bskor btags// sangs rgyas bstan pa ston pa po// rgyal po sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam// dbang phyug chen po grags
111a1: brtsed kyil 'khor slob dpon du kyil 'khor can/ / sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor ston pa 'o// dgra rgyan cod pan kun nas bcings// sna tshogs can gyis brgyan pa lags// de ltar de rjed bang phyug mgon
111a2: mtshan brgyan brgyad dag gis bstod/ / rdo don yod pas gsungs pa// rdo rje gas pas brgyan pa yaM// rdo rje mtshan rtsa brgyad pa 'di// mngan rdo rje na yod 'byung // snang bathams cad zlog byed pa// ming ni brgyan brgya
111a3: ba 'di/ / dad pa gang zhig 'chang byed pa// grub pa thams cad thob 'gyur zhing // nges pa kun las rnam par grol// lag na rdo rje stobs po che// rtag tu phyi bzhin 'brang bar 'gyur// lag na rdo rje'i yon tan che//
111a4: gang zhig nang bar langs nas brjod// de ni sdig pa kun las grol// ngan song kun las thar par 'gyur// gsang sngags thog mar smos pa 'di// sra zhig nang par langs nas 'don// rgyal po chen po grong khyer ba// gnyen
111a5: rnams kyang ni dga' bar 'gyur/ / bstod pa'i mchog ni su 'don pa// 'jig rten thams cad de dbang 'gyur// sdig pa thams cad zad pa dang // tshe dang bsod nams 'phel bar 'gyur// ji ltar 'dod pa dam pa yis// bde/
111a6: bde yis thob par 'gyur// gang zhig nang bar langs nas ni// lag na rdo rje'i drung du brjod// de ni ji ltar 'dod pa dang // ldan 'gyur 'di la the tsom med// ming brgya rtsa brgyad 'don pa la// bgegs dang log 'dren
111a7: thams cad dang / / 'jigs byed rgyal po rnams kyis kyang // zil gyis gnon par mi nus so// shes rab can na gang zhig gis// ming brgya rtsa brgyad mchog bston na// gzugs bzang stobs ni skyed pa dang // bde ba 'asem
111a8: bde'i yis 'thob/ / gang zhig ming brgya rtsa brgyad 'di// nges par gnas shing gtsang mar 'don// mdor na yon tan rgyas pa yi// bde ba de yis thob par 'gyur// 'phags pa lag na rdo rje'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs
111b1: sngags dang bcas pa/ rdzogs s+ho// // 'phags pa 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa// phyogs bcu'i yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shes bya mtha'
111b2: dag ma lus par lta bzad cing mchog dum du byung ba rnam par dag pa'i bri mde'i ba rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa thugs drim dang skyon thams cad dang bral ba// yon tan drim
111b3: med pa'i tshigs kyi 'od zer gyis brgyan pa'i spun pas rten gyi padam la lha dang mi dang l+h+wa ma yin dang/ / k+Sha dang / ragazugs 'chang rnams kyi thong rmugs dang cod pan gyi gyi mos gtugs pa la phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub
111b4: sems dpa' chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngan song gi 'gro ba sna tshogs rnam par 'joms pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ / tad+ya thA/ oM b+he ma hA ma Ni ru tsi ra ka lA pa bi tsid tra/ mug ta dA ma/ a la~M kri ta sha ri ra/ ba ra sa twa ma
111b5: tathA ga tam pA d+ha ma ko Sha d+har/ za bar d+harmal ba ta/ bi dza ye su rata/ sam b+h+yo tag su pa dasha ka/ kle sha ga dpra sha ma ka/ shUn+ta tA wi b+hA ba/ a nu swa re/ ma hA b+ho d+hi sa twa bA ra/ bar ta/ ba ratadang / oM ma hA bsha

112a1: ra dza sa ma/ bi ra dza u0f7fra/ u bad du tA mAM/ swa ra u pa dra ba pra sha ma ka/ a bi big ta nA/ ku sha la saM b+ha ra/ ba ri pu ra yi tA/ ku si da nA ma/ tA bir+ya dA tA/ ma ran d+harmi Na/ ma mi ta ba dA dA tA/ ma ma bi b+ha ga bAn/ nA tho b+ha ga sha
112a2: ran/ pa ra ya nAM/ tra tA/ sarba duHkhA ni me pra sha ma ya/ sarba kle shar dzA si mi/ a ba na ya/ sarba san sar u ba dra ba/ du la kha ni me nA sha ye/ sarba ku she la d+harma ba ri pU ra me ku ru/ sarba karma a ba daH/ kle sha pa rab ta me bi ki ra/ ma hA
112a3: b+ho d+hi sa tra si bi d+hi/ bir+ya par mi tA/ yo ge mes na ni yo dza ya/ a ra Na d+harma/ pi ra ka bi ra dza/ san dza ha/ pra dza ha/ d+ha ra ni sa ma/ kha sa ma/ dza la ni d+ha sa ma/ me ru sa ma/ ma hA bo d+hi satwa ba ra da swA hA// rig sngags don kun sgrub pa
112a4: 'di/ / 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis bshad pa na// de ma thag tu sems can rnams// skye dang rga ba zad par 'gyur// ngan 'gro thams cad zhi gyur nas/ bdud kyi sde rnams rab tu 'dar// lha rnams thams cad rab tu dga'// log/
112a5: 'dren rnams ni sreg par 'gyur// sdig pazhi par byed pa yi// gzungs 'di bshad pa'i mod las yang // grangs med phrag ni dung phyur rnyed// 'khor ba'i brtsonar dag nas thar// 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa yis// 'jam
112a6: ba'i dbyangs ni rab bsgrags shing / / gang tshe rig sngags bshad pa na// brag dang nags dang tshal du bcas// chub dang ni mi rgyu ba'o// sa gzhi pa de yi tshen g.yos// sangs rgyas 'od kyi snang ba yis// sa yi steng yang khyab par
112a7: gyur/ bgegs dang log 'dren thams cad dang // srin po mi bzang gzugs can rnams// stobs bcu ldan la phyag 'tshal zhes// skad phyung tshig ni mthun par smras// lha rnams zhi ba'i cha lugs can// thams cad yid
112a8: ni dga' gyur nas/ / gang no rdo rje'i ngal gri che// de'i drung lhags smras pa ni// phyag 'tshal mchog sbyin rdo rje'i mchog/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs ni stobs chen pa/ shugs stong ldan ba rgyal ba can// bgegs kyi yul 'khor rab
112b1: 'joms pa/ / sngags 'chang gsang sngags chen po 'chang // sna tshogs gzugs can mi yi bdag/ shin tu stobs ldan gzugs mdzes 'jigs// drag po drag por rab 'joms pa// gzi brjid gzi brjid ma pa
112b2: ba'i dpal/ / dpal ldan mnyam pa med pa'i dpe// rdo rje can te snying sbyong ba// mi shes pa yi rab rib sel// sgeg pa'i cha lugs mchog mnga' ba// skye dgu'i bdag po sgeg par dgyes// gzhu stobs can la phyag ra
112b3: pa/ / nyon mongs dgra rnams sel bar mdzad// mdzes pa na bza' sna tshogs gsol// me tog phreng rgyan sna tshogs can// spyan bzang dbu ni mdzes pa ste// dgyes shing na bza' mdzes par gsol// 'jam pa'i dbyangs
112b4: de rab tu bzhad/ / dkar nag 'byes pa'i spyan mnga' ba// ta ha'i sgra ni grags par sgrags// rab tu dga' bas bstan pa dga'// rgya chen gser gyi mdog dang ldan// rgya mtsho snying po'i spyod yul can// tshul mkhyen tshul
112b5: ldan 'jigs pa ste/ / sdang ba'i snying ni 'jigs par mdzad// cha lugs sngo las sbyong ba// lha yi bdag po dga' bar mdzad// 'dod pa'i lta ste 'dod sel bstan// rgyal po'i 'jig rten sa 'dzin pa// brtan po rnams la
112b6: brtan par grags/ / yon tan bdag gis phyogs su bzhad// btud pa yis btud phyag bgyis pa// rtag tu mchod cing brjed pa lags// stobs po che la shugs che ba// phyag ring g.yul chen mnga' ba po// sgregs chen
112b7: rdo rje rngam pa ste/ / 'dzem shes rab srung ngo tsha shes// dkyil 'khor chen po'i snying po'i mchog/ dkyil 'khor chen po ston pa po// dkyil 'khor chen po grags pa ste// dkyil 'khor chen po mdzad pa lags// dkyil 'khor
112b8: blo dpon dkyil 'khor can/ / zhabs la rjed pa'i tshogs dang ldan// ha ha swA hA'i bdag che ba// mchod pa chen po sa dang mnyam// hUM gis 'jigs mdzad 'jigs pa ste// 'jigs pa'i 'od kyis gsal ba po// lha dang lha/
113a1: min rnams kyis btud// de bzhin mchod cing ri mong bgyid// zham ring gdabyangs chen po can/ rlung dag mun pa sel mdzad pa// 'jig rten gsum du snyan par grags// gnod sbyin sran pos bsnyen bkur
113a2: pa/ / d+hag po dkar mdzad pade 'thung ba// mnga' bdag gtsug gi nor bu can// 'dzum zhing sgeg par kun tu ston// spyod pas ltar brtan pa lags// nor bu'i dkyil 'khor 'od mdzes pa// nyi ma gsal ba ltam me ga// nyi
113a3: ma'i 'od 'dra 'ja' grags bzhin/ / tha ler zhugs shing rgya cher bzhad// mthong na dga' zhing dga' bar mdzad// nor sbyin de bzhin gsang sngags sbyin// dbang phyug sbyin zhing rgyal srid sbyin// gzugs sbyin de
113a4: bzhin stobs sbyin pa/ / dpal ldan dpal mdzad bgegs gnon ri// kun tu rmongs pa sel bar mdzad// 'dus pa'i nang du gdan gshegs pa// zhabs la mchod pa'i tshogs bsags pa// dpung rgyan snyan
113a5: gdub kor can/ / nor bu'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa ste// rgyu dang mi rgyu 'gro ba'i sgron// rab rib sel bar mdzad pa po// ston pa ston mdzad skyong mdzad pa// dbang po mnga' bdag dmag gi mchog/ 'jigs pa sel bar mdzad
113a6: paste/ / 'jigs pa med pa'i gnas sbyin pa// dkar ba sngob 'od bzang ba// mgrin sngon gyi ni ston pa lags// ji ltar 'dul ba 'dul 'gyur ba// de bzhin cha lugs rab tu ston// shes rab ral zis 'debs
113a7: par mdzad/ / song nyid chos ni lhur 'dzin pa// byams pa mchog dang tha ma mkhyen// rnam par grags pa gsan pa des// rig sngags 'chang ba rnams kyis bskyod// rig sngags 'chang ba stobs po che// shin tu rnam
113a8: rgyal 'khor los spyang/ / 'jigs med po thos shes rab can// de bzhin gshegs pa chos 'dzin pa// mgur bzangs 'dul mjed shib ste// zhi ba'i laman ston mdzad pa// lha dang lta min bas pas bzung // sangs na

113b4: 'joms pa/ / tshan chen ngas 'joms rnal 'byor pa// 'dod pa gnod pa khyab par gshegs// mgon po rgyal ba'i sras kyi mchog/ gshin rje ba ma mdzad skye dgu srung // las dang nyon mongs rab sreg pa// stan

113b8: cher bzhad cing / / 'azug chen sgra ni sgrogs pa yis// de bzhin gshegs pa zhal gsal ba// shar phyogs gzigs nas bka' stsal pa// skye ma gsang sngags mchog gi yul// sems can gti mug bsal ba'i
114a1: phyir/ sems can rnams kyi bsod nams tshogs// shin tu rgyas pa byung bar gyur// kye ma bsod nams cher byas pa'i// sems can rnams kyi rab sbyang phyir// dam pas sbyin pa'i grub pa'i gzungs// 'jam
114a2: pa'i klog gis rab tu bshad/ / la la gang zhig mnyam bzhag nas// sdug bsngal thams cad sel ba yi// grub pa'i gzungs 'di 'don pa'am// yang na nyan tam sems kyang rung // de yi don kun 'grub 'gyur zhing //

114a4: kyis/ / rab dga' shin tu dri ma med// 'od byed pa dang 'od 'phro can// sbyad dka' de bzhin mngon du gyur// ring du song dang mi g.yo ba// legs pa'i blo gros chos kyi sprin// sa chen dam pa de dag kyang // gang zhig nges gnas 'dod

114a6: sngags 'chang kun spyad pa dang / / sdig pa thams cad zhi byed pa// bkra shis mchog tu dge ba yi// ming brgya rtsa brgyad yid 'od 'di// ser mo bcu yi thal sbyar nas// 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi mdun 'dug la// shin tu dang ba'i sepa?
114a7: kyis su/ / nang par langs nas su brjod pa// de la rig sngags 'chang kun dang // de bzhin lha yi bdag po rnams// gnod sbyin srin po mang po dag/ rtag tu yang ni srung bar byed// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras kun dang //

114b1: po rnams/ / bgegs dang log 'dren chen po dag/ dga' zhing bsam pa dam pa yis// rgyud ma dag nas phyag kyang 'tshal// dpyir bgegs rnams dga' 'gyur bas// 'tshe bar byed kyang mi nus so// lan cig klags nas

115a1: gyi ngo tshes brgyad dam/ tshes bcwa lnga la smyung bar 'dug cing gso sbyong dang ldan par byas te/ spos dang / bdug pa dang / mar me dang / me tog dang / me tog phreng dang / byug pa la sogs pas mchod la

115a4: thams cad sel bar byed do/ / de nas rdo rje me tog thod chen pos gsum gyi dbang phyug dang / thabs gcig du 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po de'i na nas stan las langs te/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po sgrib pa thams cad

115a6: phyag 'tshal lo/ / smin pa kun las nges par grol// nyon mongs dri ma kun sel cing // nyes pa kun las rnam par grol// skyon bral khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// lam srang gcig pu'i tshul ston cing // theg pa gcig
115a7: bu'i tshul gcig pa/ / theg pa chen po'i tshul brnyes te// theg pa dag la khyod phyag 'tshal// snang ba chen po snang ba rnyes// yon tan dkyil 'khor 'jig rten dag/ zla ba bzhin du 'od dkar ba// 'jig rten 'das pa khyod/
115a8: phyag 'tshal// theg pa chen po dag pa che// sangs rgyas theg pa rtogs gyur cing // rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor rnam grags pa// rdo rje chen po khyod phyag 'tshal// dpa' bo chen po bdud las rgyal// dar ba chen po nyon mongs
115b1: tsho sa/ / bgags thub gshin rje thub pa ste// rin chen dra ba khyod phyag 'tshal// zlab chen po nyi ma che// sman po chen po dbang phyug ce// lha chen mgon pa chen po ste// 'byor pa chen po khyong phyag 'tshal// sgrib pa thams cad gcod mdzan ba
115b2: nga / / rlob pa thams cad sel mdzad pa// kun mkhyen yon tan bdag nyid che// rnams la khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas spyod yul zhugs pa ste// chos kyi spyod bral gshegs pa lags// ye shes dbang phyug ye shes mo//
115b3: sreng bral khyod la phrag 'tshal lo// kun mdzes yon tan snying po mkhyen// rdo rje yin dkyil 'khor brgyan// sangs rgyas lam ste don yod ce// ye shes dag la byed phyag 'tshal// bstan pa gnas pa dbang bdag po// bde mdzan
115b4: thugs kyang zhi ba ste/ / yangs pa dri med shes rab can// snang ba dag la khyod phyag 'tshal// zab cing bstan la rnam par gnan// zhi la 'jig rten dag par mdzad// ston pa skyabs 'os srid gsum na// dpa' btsan khyod la phyag
115b5: 'tshal lo/ / bskal pa chen po nyon mongs bcom// 'khor ba'i dkyil 'khor 'joms pa ste// zhi bzhi mdzad bde 'byung ba// chu bo zhi mdzad khyod phyag 'tshal// thar pa'i sku ste chos lugs che// bde 'gror gnas pa dri ma med//
115b6: rnam dag thugs mnga' zhi ba mkhyen// nyes sel khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rtse mo yangs pa rnam par grags// sngags chen mang pos 'dul mdzad pa// snying po chen po dkyil 'khor mchog/ dkyil 'khor mkhyen pa khyod phyag 'tshal//
115b7: sdug bsngal gsum se la gsum gyi mchog/ dkon mchog gsum dang spyod yul 'dra// rnam gsum mkhyen pa snyed pi bdag/ rnam thar gsum khyod phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' yon tan gyis// 'byor pa bsnyes shing
115b8: mnyam nyid brnyes/ / bskal pa dag ni grangs med par// tshegs chen bsags pa khyod phyag 'tshal// sa la gnas pas chen brnyes/ sa yi 'bras bu phun sum tshogs// yang dgas 'dzin las byung ba// ye shes sa khyod phyag
116a1: 'tshal lo/ / ting nge 'dzin la mnga' brnyes pa// nyes gsum spong zhing sdig pa sel// ting 'dzin mkhyen cing rgya che ba// mnyam pa nyid mnyam khyod phyag 'tshal// mgon po chen po snang ba che// sdug bsngal chen
116a2: po'i rim sa la/ / zhi gyur ma lus ni mdzad pa// yon tan pha mtha' khyod phyag 'tshal// sangs rgyas kun mtshungs gsung ldan pa// chos kun zhi ba phun sum tshogs// dkon mchog gsum rigs dpe med pa// rin chen
116a3: mtha' yas khyod phyag 'tshal/ / rdo rje chen po dri med mchog/ rdo rje'i mtshon bsnams sdig mi mnga'// nam mkha' ma lus yul dang ldan// ye shes spyod yul rgya mtsho mnga'// de bzhin gshegs dang yul gcig pa// sel
116a4: pa po ste dri ma sbyod/ / shes rab chen po rgyal ba'i sras// sred gcod khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor rdo rje'i mchog/ rdo rje'i 'dul ba rdo rje 'chang // rdo rje'i rtsal can rnams kyi rtsal// rdo rje snang ba khyod phyag
116a5: 'tshal/ / rin chen chen po rin chen blo// rin chen rdo rje 'od che ba// rin chen 'od mdzes rin chen 'byung // rin chen bstan pa srung mdzad pa// stong pa nyid kyi yul brnyes pa// ye shes stong pa nyid kyis ston// stong nyid longs
116a6: spyod yul dang ldan/ / stong nyid mchog khyod phyag 'tshal lo// shes rab mtshungs med shes rab can// dge ba rnam dgas dang bral// chos gcig las byung snang ba po// 'jig rten 'das pa'i tshul chen 'gas// 'jig rten
116a7: snong mdzad smram khas pa/ / 'jig rten chos las rnam par 'das// 'jig rten mkhyen pa'i yon tan brnyes// brgyan par mdzad pa dkyil 'khor dag/ nyes pa ma lus bsal ba ste// bal chen skye po kun la bar// sa 'dzin
116a8: rnam par grags pa po/ / kun mkhyen khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// dga' mkhyen dga' la longs spyod pa// dga' ba'i rigs mchog rnams kyi mchog/ dga' bar mdzad pa'i rtog pa can// dga' la snang ba khyod phyag 'tshal/
116b1: sgeg can 'jam zhing dgongs par ldan// rnam par bsregs la spyod pa brtan// rdo rje rig pa bsgeg pa'i mchog/ sreg chen khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa'i mchog/ rdo rje mchog gi dkyi
116b2: 'khor che/ / theg pa chen po'i tshul la gnas// bla med mchog khyod phyag 'tshal lo// dpa' bo byang chub sems dpa'i mchog/ sgrib pa thams cad sel mdzad la// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor rnams kyis ni// ming
116b3: brgya rtsa brgyad kyis bstod nas/ / rdo rje'i bstan pa rnam grags pa// bcom ldan rdo rje'i can gyis gsungs// kye ma 'byor ces snang ba yi// dkyil 'khor rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor pa// gang zhig ming brgyartsa
116b4: brgyad ba/ / 'di dag so sor rjod byed na// nga ni nyes pa kun zlog cing // rtag tu de yi phyi bzhin 'brang // nang bar langs nas gtsang ma yis// sgrib pa thams cad sel ba la// blo ldan gang zhig bstong byed pa// /
116b5: de yi sdig pa med par 'gyur// gang zhig ming brgya rtsa brgyad mchog/ nang bar langs nas rjed byed pa// ldang ba thams cad de dbang 'gyur// bgegs rnams kyis kyang yongs su btang // sdig pa dag pa
116b6: 'thob pa dang / / de bzhin bsod nams 'phel ba dang // ye shes rgya mtsho longs spyod cing // sa mchog chen po thob par 'gyur// gang zhig nges par gnas byas la// ming brgya rtsa brgyad mchog 'don pa// des ni
116b7: 'byor chen sangs rgyas sa/ / ring por mi thogs thob par 'gyur// rgyud chen ldan zhing blo cho ba// gang zhig ming mchog 'don pa ni// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor bstan pa la// ring por mi thogs 'jug par 'gyur/
116b8: byang chub sems dpa' chen po sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa rdzogs s+ho// // 'phags pa sa'i snying po'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags
117a1: dang bcas pa/ dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po chen po byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa'i snying po la phyag 'tshal lo// oM sum b+ha ni/ sum b+ha/ ha ra tsa ram tra pA sha ma ru tA/ a mo g+ha badz+ra sa twa swahA/
117a2: de nas yon tan sbyin pa yi// gzungs 'di bshad ma thag tu yang // rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// ti se'i gengs bcas g.yos par gyur// sa yi snying po tshogs dbang la// bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis smas// skal
117a3: ldan chen po 'gas po gas/ / sa steng khyod kyis yangs par byas// khyed kyi gzungs ni nam grags shing // yon tan dpag med mchog skyed pa// sems can kun gyi sdug bsngal dang // nyes bzlog byed thos pa ni// 'khor/
117a4: par rab tu rgyu ba na// nyes pa kun gyis mi gos te// ji ltar 'dam gyi pad ma dag/ 'dam gyis nyes pas mi gos bzhin// lus can dag las su yang rung // khyod kyis gsang sngags 'chang byed pa// de dag las ni
117a5: gcig tsam yang / / byang chub las ni ldog mi 'gyur// mkhas pa gang zhig gzungs sngags mchog/ thos nas mos par byed pa ni// nges par yon tan thams cad kyang // thob par 'gyur te the tshom med// de nas thams
117a6: cad ldan pa'i 'khor/ / langs te sa yi dbang phyug po// sa yi snying po sa mchog la// ming brgya rtsa brgyad spras pa ni/ sa yi snying po gtso bo che// glog 'gu lta bu'i spyan mda' za// cod pan can tes brnyes pa/
117a7: phun sum tshogs ldan 'byor ba mchog/ rig ldan rig mdzad mchod pa'i gnas// gtso bo dge sbyong ston pa po// gzhi bcas ldan pa'i rlung gi tshul// mAM hA'i bla ldan snying rje'i rab// thams cad mkhyen pa'i nyam
117a8: la rin mam khyen par zags/ / gang sngags mang kya cher // sa yi bang drug ga bas// sheg pa shes pa dag sa na ga/ 'brab pa ma nas na pag/ kyang tham
117b1: snying po mkhyen/ / snying po brnyes pa 'jigs pa med// mgon po sangs rgyas gzugs mnga' ba// shes rab kyis ni ma lus gzigs// 'dod chags la sogs skyon gsal cing // gar thabs chen po ston pa po//
117b2: ston pa dpags pa sam shing dang 'dra// nam mkha'i dbang phyug gsung snyan pa// nyi ma chen po nyid yin te// dbang phyug chen po 'bar bas bskor// yon tan mtha' yas longs spyod pa// sa yi dbang phyug spyod yul
117b3: can/ / chos kyi longs spyod longs spyod che// yon tan rgya mtsho'i gangs chen mtsho// yon tan sna tshogs longs spyod pa// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi mchog/ thabs tshul zab la mkha' pa ste// theg pa
117b4: chen po 'jigs pa che/ / mchod pa chen po sgra che ba// zla ltar grags pa'i dkyil 'khor can// rdo rje 'chang chen mtshan brgya pa// rdo rje dkyil 'khor me tog thod// blo gros chen po phyag ring ba// pad ma chen po
117b5: spobs po che/ / gsang sngags chen po tshogs chen po/ sa gzhi chen po lhun po lags// lag na rdo rje yon tan des// nor bu'i me tog thod kyis brgyan// mnyam nyid 'byam la longs spyod pa// rgyal chen
117b6: zhing gi rgya mtsho can/ / rdo rje'i 'od mnga'i rdo rje ldan// sa yi bdag po lhun po bzhin// sa la longs spyod longs spyod bzang // mtshon cha g.yo ba phun sum tshogs// rab 'byam snod ni rnam par grags//
117b7: smra mkhas rdo rje rab 'joms pa// spyan rtsa yi tsam dmar ba ste// me tog sngon po'i thod kyis bcings// spro bo chen po phyag ring ba// brtan po brtan la bde sbyin paded dpon dpal bzang chen po ste// gangs
117b8: tsan ldan po lta bu lags/ / dbang po gshin rdo'i rgyal chen dang // btsan po khyab 'jug stobs dbang phyug/ 'jig rten mchog rigs sangs rgyas tshangs// de bzhin nyid tshul spyod yul can// rin chen tog ste
118a1: cher bzhad pa/ / dgyes pa na bza' sna tshogs gsol// gzigs pa ring ba spyan yangs pa// nam mkha' bzhin du thogs pa med// thogs pa mi dpogs rin chen gtsug/ srid gsupa 'dod
118a2: pa med pa'i rgyu/ / dul ba nyon mongs dri ma gsal// dag pa gtsang ba gso sbyong can// rnam par gnon pa'i yul las 'das// ljang mdog skyabs mdzad snying rje che// stobs kyis grags pa rgya che ba// bsams
118a3: na shes pa'i spyod yul can/ / dpa' bo seng ge 'jigs par byed// sdang ba rnams kyi snying 'joms pa// mnga' bdag grags pa yul dang ldan// dga' ba rgya chen rab byung ba// rigs mkhyen rigs kyi snying po
118a4: mkhyen/ / rigs kun du ni mchod pa lags// rgyal po rigs mchog skyes pa'i rten// rdo rje yi ni dkyil 'khor brgyan// rdo rje sa 'og rab grags pa// rig sngags 'chang ba stobs po che// mngon par 'phags pa
118a5: khyab pa mchog/ mgrin bzangs nad dang bral ba lags// skyong mdzad ston pa dag pa ste// sangs rgyas lam ni rab ston pa// grol ba smin mdzad 'dud par mdzad// dkyil 'khor ma lus rnams kyis brgyan//
118a6: rab zhugs dkyil 'khor rnams la mkhas// rdo rje'i slob dpan yon tan rten// grub pa sbyin pa rnam dag mchog/ tshul dang tshul min rtogs pa po// dkyil 'khor rtse ser mnga' ba ste// 'od zer ljang khu'i 'od dang ldan/

118a8: cing na bza' dag/ dag pa mkhyen cing dag par ldan// dag pa'i chos mnga' snang ba ste// 'byung ldan srid pa sel mdzad pa// 'khor bzad mdzad shes rab can// tshul shes tshul la spyod yul ba// rdo rje rgya
118b1: mtsho'i snying po lags/ / rdo rje sems dpa' dge ba che// 'byung ldan rab 'byam shes rab can// ma lus grags pa'i 'od bzang ba// sa yi snying po snying po che// rdo rje'i snying po rnam par 'dren// dpag tu med pa
118b2: dpag med rdzogs/ / khyad par 'phags pa'i yul la gnas// zab cing gsal ba'i gtso bo ste// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor 'od zer gsil// dga' dang dad pa skyed pa ste// ye shes rgya chen spyod yul ba// rlung gi
118b3: drag shul lta bur drag/ drag po lags te drag sel gtsang // rgyal bar byed cing rgyal bzhi// rgyal ba'i dpal mdzad dga' bar mdzad// ldan po ti sa ma la yas// spyod yul zab mo non pa ste// rin can rdo rje snying
118b4: po che/ / sa bzhi'i spyod yul mnga' ba lags// rin chen brag las byung ba'i 'od// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dag gis brgyan// de bzhin gshegs la lhur dgyes pa// shugs drag dpal gyi gzhi rten lags/
118b5: rab gsal dpa' mdzod gtsang ma ste// phyogs bcu'i dbang phyug dbang phyug che// de ltar rdo rje 'chang chen la// ming brgya rtsa brgyad mchog rnams kyis// rdo rje sems dpa' bstod nas ni// rdo rjes gsum dbang
118b6: mchog smras/ / yon tan snying po shes rnams kyis// ming rgya rtsa brgyad mchog rjod cing // nyes pa zlog pa 'di las gzhan// sa yi steng na ngas ma mthong // ming brgya rtsa brgyad dam pa 'di// thams cad 'grub byed dga'
118b7: bste/ / sdig pa thams cad sel ba dang // / dri ma kun bral yon tan nges// de phyir bsgrim pa thams cad kyis// phun sum tshogs pa 'dod pa'i mis// ming brgya rtsa brgyad dge ba 'di// rtag tu yang ni brjod par
118b8: gyis/ / ming brgya rtsa brgyad dam pa 'di// bsam pa kun dang 'byor pa yi// gnas mchog bla na med pa ste// dpal yon brgya chen byin pa yid// yid ni shin tu dad pa yis// sa yi snying po'i mtshan gsal ba/ 'dod//
119a1: pa thams cad rab sgrub pa'i// yon tan mchog ni gang rjod dang // dpal yon rgya chen 'dzin pa yi// ming brgya rtsa brgyad dam pa 'di// ming ni gang zhig rjod byed pa// sdug bsngal kun las byung

121a7: bdag byung / / phyag dar kyim 'phung po de las kyang legs so zhes bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa lags so legs so// dang ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgras bzang po'o// zam

121b1: phyag mdzad nas lan gsub bskor ba mdzad nas nyid kyi klulas na bza' bsil nas mchod rten rnying pa phyag dar gyi phung po lta bu de la gsol te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis mchi ma byung ba chen po byung bas bshums pa mdzad/

122a6: bu'o/ / kha cig gis ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa la gnas so// kha cig gis ni byang chub tu lung bstan pa thob po// kha cig gis ni sa dang po'o// kha cig gis ni sa gnyis pa'o// kha cig gis ni sa gsum pa'o// /

125b1: bka' stsal pa/ lag na rdo rje nyon cig/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba dang / gang dag yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad kyi de bzhin

125b3: rnam grangs yin no/ / na ma s+t+rai yad d+hi ka nAM/ sarba ta thA ga tA nAM/ oM b+hu bi bAM ban pa rab thaM/ tsu lu tsu lA/ d+ha re d+hA ra/ sarba ta thA ga tAd+hA tud+b+hare/ bad mA ma b+hi ti/ dza ya bA re/ u tsu la sA ra ta thA gat+ta/ d+har+m+ma tsakra pA par
125b4: te na badz+ra bo d+ha mi Na Da a laM ka ra/ a laM kri te/ sarba te thA ga tA a d+hiSh+Thi te/ bo d+ha ya bo d+ha ya/ bo d+hi ne bo d+ha ni/ bud d+hA ya bud d+ha yaM/ sabo d+ha ni saM bo d+ha ya/ tsa la tsa la tsa le tu/ sarba a pa ra Na naM/ sarba pA baM bi ga te/

126a8: mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas chos thams cad kyi tshul dang /
126b1: 'dul ba dang rnam par 'phrul pa'i gzi brjid kyi rgyal po la phyag 'tshal lo// phyag 'tshal dus gsum sangs rgyas la// phyag 'tshal dkon mchog gsum dge la/ mi 'khrugs pa dang 'od dpag med/ spyan

174b3: bya'o/ / gnas khang gtsang ma'i nang du 'dug ste/ yongs su dag par khrus byas nas gos btsang ma bgos te/ ba dan sbyangs mar me sbar te/ spos dang / me tog dang / zhal zas kyi mchod pa byas nas sems rtse gcig
174b4: tu btang te/ dmigs pa tha dad pa gzhan la mi dmigs par chos bzhin du 'don cing yongs su 'dzin par byed na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' nyi 'od dang / byang chub sems dpa' zla 'od lha dang / drang srong tshad med/

174b6: pa'i gtsug lag ji snyed pa de dag kyang yongs su 'dzin par 'gyur/ mu stegs can gyi chos kyi cho ga dang / smra ba ji snyed pa thams cad kyang rtogs shing khong du chud par 'gyur ro// rig sngags 'di 'don cing yongs su
174b7: 'dzin par byed pa gang yin pa des ni 'jig rten na gdon nang rnam pa brgyad khri bzhi stong yod pa dag gsos nas 'tsho bar byed do/ / 'dre srin thams cad la dbang byed cing lha'i bu'i bdud rnams kyang 'dul bar byed/ mu stegs
174b8: can rnams kyang char gcod par byed do/ / gal te ri 'am dgon pa na gnas te mdo sde kha ton du 'don pa dang bsam gtan bsgom pa ni ri'i lha dang / 'dra srin gnod pa byed pa dag nan gyis rgyal ka byas nas sems mnyam
175a1: par gzhag tu ma drang bar gyur na/ rig sngags 'di lan cig bzlas pa byas na 'dre srin de dag thams cad 'chi bar 'gyur ro// gal te chos bzhin du bzlas brjod byas te sems can rnams la snying brtse ba'i
175a2: sems bskyed par gyur na/ bdag kyang de'i tshe dge ba'i lha dang / klu'i rgyal po thams cad dang / lag na rdo rje gsang ba pa rnams la rtag par de'i rjes su 'brang zhing yongs su srung ba gyis shig/ de'i nye 'khor na gnas nas mig gi
175a3: 'bras bu bzhin du yongs su spangs shig/ rang gi srog gi dbang po bzhin du skyobs shig ces bsgo bar 'gyur ro// gang dag la bsgo bar byed pa bstan pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad de smras pa// bdag gis gsang ba'i bdag po rje
175a4: rje 'chang/ / bdud rtsi 'khyil pa sme brtsegs lcags kyu can// stobs ldan shad kar dang sde brgyad dag/ btad nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis dbang phyug dang ni mthu chen dang // ku be ra dang ser skya'i bdag po
175a5: dag btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed/ / bdag gis nor srung dang ni chu lha dang // dge rgyas dang ni ba ri tsi tra dag/ btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis so sor tsa dang ma hA ra// ku lan tan ta dang ni
175a6: lngas rtsen dag/ btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis bi ba ka la'i rgyal po dang // dpal ldan byi ta dang ni sa ra hA ra// btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis tshangs pa dang ni sam par//
175a7: gnas gtsang ste lnga dag mtshe ma dag/ btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis brgya byin sum bcu rtsa gsum lnga// spobs chen dpal ldan dang ni sa tan// gtang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung
175a8: bar byed/ / bdag gis rgyal po yul 'khor bsrung dang ni// ma mo lha la sogs pa mthu chen 'khor// btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis rgyal po 'phags skyes po dang ni// mig mi bzang dang rnam
175b1: thos bu dag kyang / / btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis gser mdog rma bya'i rgyal po dang // sde dpon nyi shu brgyad dang drang srong 'khor// btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis
175b2: nor bu bzang po dag dang ni/ / sde dpon chen pos 'dzin bu la pa// btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis dga' bo dang ni bsnyen dga' bo// klu rgyal rgya mtsho dang ni e la'i 'dab// btang nas rtag tu gzung
175b3: 'dzin srung bar byed/ / bdag gis lha ma yin dang dri za dang // mkha' lding mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye rnams// btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// bdag gis chu dang me dang glog gi lha// grul bum bdag po dang ni sha za dag/
175b4: btang nas rtag tu gzungs 'dzin srung bar byed// dge ba'i lha de dag dang klu'i rgyal po dang ma mo la sogs pa de dag kyang so so nas 'khor lnga brgya dang bcas pa dang / mthu chen po dang ldan pa'i gnod sbyin dag gis kyang rtag par

175b6: bgegs dang bar chad yongs su sel bar byed do/ / gal te gcong rong dag tu gnas te lam stor bar gyur pa las rig sngags 'di bzlas par gyur na de'i dbang gis dge ba'i lha dang / klu'i rgyal po dag dge ba'i mi'i gzugs
175b7: su mngon par sprul nas lam yang dag pa nyid ston par 'gyur ro/ / gal te ri dang nags tshal dang / de gon pa dag tu gnas pa las chu dang me dag gis phongs par gyur na yang klu'i rgyal po dag gis yongs su bsrung ba'i phyir chu

176a5: nagasang ba'i tshe/ / rtse gcig thugs rje chen po'i gzungs bzlas na// dug nyid zil mngar zas skom nyid du 'gyur// bud med sbrum ma bu ni btsal ba'i tshe// gdud kyis bgegs byas sdug bsngal mi bzod tshe// rtse gcig thug

177a1: gang dgas dang po ma thob par 'gyur la/ / sa bcu pa'i bar du yang ma thob pa thob par 'gyur ro// gzhan yang sangs rgyas kyi sa'i bar du yang phyin par byed pa'i phyir mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis dang / dpe byad

177a5: cad bla na med pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed par nus so/ / sems can gang dag tshe 'di nyid la smon pa rnams mngon par 'grub par 'dod na zhag nyi shu rtsa gcig gi bar du gso sbyong dang / tshul khrims la gnas nas gzungs

177b1: zhugs te 'khrus byas pa las de na gnas pa'i sems can de dag gis lus bkrus pa'i chu lus la rig par gyur na/ sdig pa'i las dang khwa na ma thob lcib thams cad yongs su byang nas zhing yongs su dag pa dag tu

177b8: gter nyid du rig par bya ste/ sangs rgyas gang gA'i klung gi bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgu'i bye ma snyed rnams kyis phangs shing gces par mdzad pa'i phyir ro// gang zag de ni 'od can gyi lus kyi gter yin par rig par zo ma
178a1: de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od byer kyis snang bar mdzad pa'i phyir ro/ / gang zag de ni byams pa dang snying rje'i gter yin par yang rig par bya ste/ 'di ltar gzungs kyis sems can yongs spyod
178a2: par byed pa'i phyir ro/ / gang zag de ni dam pa'i chos kyi sde snod yin par rig par te/ gzungs kyi sgo thams cad kun sdud par byed pa'i phyir ro// gang zag de ni bsam gtan dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi sde snod yin par rig par bya ste/

196b1: rigs kyi bu'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig las kyi rnam par smin pa'i dbang gis tshe bas su nye ba'i tshe 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i phyag rgya ldam bgyis te/ gdugs re bzhin du mchod pa bgyis nas/ a ga ru bsregs te/ rig

197a8: thogs so/ / yang gcigags na rin po che'i phyag tu thogs so// yang gtsog gis ni la mi la thogs so// yang gcig gis ni rin po che'i nod bu thogs so// yang gcig gis ni ri ni pa che'i 'khor lo thogs so// yang gcig gis
197b1: nipad ma 'phye ba thogs so/ / yang gcig gis ni zhags pa thogs so// yang gcig gis lcang ma'i lcug mthogs so// yang gcig gis ni 'od zer kha dog lnga 'byin par bgyid do// yang gcig gis ni bzang phreng thog so//

199b1: nang pa la gzhus na nang gang yang rung ste mi 'tshe ba ma mchis lags so/ / rig sngags ni 'di lta ste/ na mo sarba bud d+ha/ d+harma saM g+hA ya/ na ma Ar+yA ba lo ki te shwa rA ya/ bo d+his twa ba rgya/ na mo badz+ra ba Ni n+ya/ kho d+has tra ba s+ya/ tad+ya thA/ si bi si bi/ kA ya si bi/ ba la sha ba la

199b8: tshe yang lan bdun bzlas brjod bgyis na mtshams ma mchis pa lnga dang / shin tu lci ba bzhi'i kha na ma tho ba rnams kyang 'byang bar 'gyur lags so// sems can thams cad la byams pa dang / snying rje bskyed par gyur na kha na ma tho ba thas

201a8: re mdud nas dpung pa g.yon pa la mdud par bgyi'o/ / gzhan yang sug pa g.yon pa'i srin lag dang / gud mo dang / 'dzub mo rnams khu tshur bcangs te/ mthe bos steng du mnan nas mthe chung chom rkun gyi phyogs su kha bstan te/ sngag/

220b3: nam tham ngan pa m+b+haH/ Ar+thas b+ha d+hA sab+h+yaH/ A yA swAH/ bai d+hA yA ya swAH/ dap+ta bid yU ya swAt+ma// ba ra dwa mum+b+hak+Sha/ ber pra d+ha ya swAH/ a t+pal min pa tham+b+ha nA la srAn+tu/ a dAn+t+ra me ka~M rmA dren mo t+ta AH/
220b4: oM ran ran d+hu phaT swAH/ oM da ya d+b+ha pa swA hA/ oM rbad drAr+dz+dza tA/ oM hU~MdI ya swA tAM/ oM hU~M dz+wal gyi badza ya// oM me g+ha ba shA a pra titata Sh+T+rI r+b+ha hrI baT swA hA/ oM bi sre ma ta~M swA hA/ oM A ro l-i ka thAhA/ oM ba~Mdz+dza/
220b5: le ban+d+ha le mA tAM/ oM a ra li ka s+dza s+t+rai pa Ta smyeH/ ni ma ta i ne ya ta bi daM nA ya a s+'ud+has+ya mi thAg lan kan no a she Nak+Sha la mAk+Sha r+tha swAH// oM pad med swA ya swA hA// oM b+hUng+ga d+he rmas b+hA ya b+hUhA/
220b6: klags pas la sa thams cad 'grub pa yin no/ rus gsum dub zlas na mtshams med pa lnga rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// lis kyi sgrib pa thams cad rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ a ga dre'i bdage sas dang / thal
220b7: ba dang / chu dang / nyungs dkar dang / seng ldeng gi pur bu la sogs pas mtshams bcing ngo // rims nad thams cad la bsrung skud bcing bar bya'o// nad thams cad la mar ram/ mar nag gam/ chu la yongs su
220b8: bzlas te sbyin par bya'o/ / lus khyab pa'i nad la mtshon chas bcad cing bsrung skud kyang bya'o// lto bon bal tshwa chus nyams par byed pa 'am/ 'jim bag gam/ chus kyang bya'o// mig gi nad la skud pa dkar po rna ba la
221a1: bcing bar bya'o/ / so'i nad la ka ra bi ri'i so shing gis so// mtshams bcing ba la tshon snga lnga'i skud pa la lan nyi shu rtsa gcig gi bar du yongs su bzlas nas seng ldeng gi pur bu bzhi la bcings te/
221a2: phyogs bzhir 'dab pa byas na/ mtshams bcing ba yin no// thams cad du bsrung skad dam/ chu 'am/ thal bas bya'o// gza' thams cad la mtshon sA lnga'i skud pas bya'o// rims thams cad la skud pa
221a3: dkar pos bya'o/ / sbrul dang / srin bu dang / ba swa byi ba dang / lhog pa dang / gre ba 'gag pa rnams la sbrang rtsi pi pi ling dang ldan pas bya'o// mig gi nad la dri zhim po'i chu 'am/ rgya skyags kyi chu'am/ sbrang rtsi'am/
221a4: shing mngar gyis bya'o/ rtsod pa'i dus thams cad du rtsod pa dang ma snyan par brjod pa la chu la yongs su bzlas te gdong bkru bar bya'o// yul gzhan gyi rgyal po'i 'tsho ba la yul 'khor du bum pa gang ba yang dag par
221a5: bzhag nas gtsang mas gos gtsang ma gyon te mchod pa chen po byas shing klags na zhi ba chen por 'gyur ro/ / de'i chus kyang gtor bar byas na sems can thams cad bsrung ba yin no// nye bar tshe ba thams cad dang /
221a6: yams rnams zhi ba yin no// phyag rgya tsan dan gyi/ thig le la lan nyi shu rtsa gcig gi bar du yongs su bzlas na mtshams med pa thams cad zad par byed do// rtag tu bzlas na khyim bsrung ba'o// pad ma'i sbyin
221a7: bsreg gis sems can thams cad kyi bsrung ba'o/ / tsan dan gyi sbyin sreg ges gza' dang / 'byung po dang / rgyu skar thams cad las bsrung ba'o// rgyal ba dang / rnam par rgyal ba dang / gzhan gyis mi thuH
221a8: pa dang / na gu li dang / dri'i na gu li dang / d+ha ra na dang / ma 'jigs pa'i lag pa dang / dbang po'i lag pa dang / dri'i br-i yang sku dang takar dang 'khor lo dang / 'khor lo chen po dang / rnam par gnon pa dang / so mar dza dang / mu
221b1: nang nge zhes bya ba ste/ de dag gang yang rung ba la brgya rtsa brgyad kyi bar du yongs su bzlas nas nor bu lta bur byas nas mgo ba dang dpung pa la bcing bar bya'o// byis pa rnams kyi ni mgul du'o// bud med rnams bya
221b2: 'dems su bcangs na rang nyid mchog tu skal ba dang ldan par byed do/ / g.yang med pa nyams nas bu yang ster ro// nor bu 'di bcangs pas thams cad du bsrung ba byas pa yin no// dug dang mes mi tshugs so//
221b3: dug gis byas pa yang skye bar mi 'gyur ro// nad byung ba yang mi skye zhing myur du zhi bar 'gyur ro// gza' rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ro// rlung dang sprin dang thog ni chus rengs par byed do// kar bi ri'i lcug mas ni las thams
221b4: cang byed do/ / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi snying po mchog tu grub pa 'dis ma bslabs par yang las 'di rnams byed do// de nas bsgrubs par 'dod na zang skra'i cho ga ni chen snga ma lus pas sangs
221b5: rgyas kyi sku gzugs mnyam par bri bar bya ste/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ral pa'i gcod pan 'chang ba ri dgas kyi lpags pas smad dkris byas shing phyugs bdag gi tshe lugs 'chang
221b6: rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa bya'o/ / wa gzam khan gas sbyong dang ldan pas ri mo bri bar bya'o// de nas sgrub pa pos sku gzugs de'i mdun du ba lang gi lcibs dkyil 'khor byas la me tog dkar po bkram
221b7: dzazhim po'i chus bkang ba'i bum pa brgyad gzhag par bya'o/ / nye bar spyod pa brgyad dang / nye bar 'kho ba drug ban rtsa bzhi dang / khrag med pa'i gtor ma sha dang bcas pa bya'o// a ka ru'i bdug s+ho
221b8: pasregs la rig pa stong phrag brgyad bzlas par bya'o/ / nyin zhag gcig tu bsrung bar gnas pa 'am/ dkar gsum za zhing / dus gsum du khrus byas nas gos gtsang mgyon par gyur pas bzlas pa bya'o//
222a1: de nas sku gzugs kyi mdun du rang nyid bris pa bltas te de mthong bas dga' bar 'gyur ro// ji srid du 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug byon te/ bsapa pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed do//
222a2: rnams ma mig sman la yongs su bzlas te mig sa sras na de nas mi snang bar 'gyur zhing nam mkha' la 'gro bar 'gyur ro// yang dag par rmongs pa med pa'i tshogs shes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin rab tu 'thob bo// sgrub pa po ga
222a3: 'dod pa de 'dis byed do zhes bya'o/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug dang / dge slong de dag dang / byang
222a4: chub sems dpa' de dag dang / gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de dag dang / lha dang mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rang ste/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par stod do//
222a5: 'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i snying po zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar gyi mkhan po a mo g+ha badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba ba ri rin chen grags pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
222a6: @#/ rgya gar skad nga / da sha b+h+ra mi d+hA ra Ni/ bod skad du/ sa bcu pa'i gzungs/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas gsang sngags la 'jug pa rnams kyis
222a7: dgongs pa thams cad so sor bsgrub par 'gyur ba ni/ oM zhes bya ba don yod zhags pa pad ma gtsug tor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du gsang sngags yi ge gcig po 'jig rten mgon po'i spyan sngar 'bum
222a8: dran par byas nas dang po la gnas par 'gyur ro/ / sngon sdig pa bsags pa'i sems can dmyal ba mi zad pa gang ci yang rung ba de dag thams cad ji ltar rlung gis phyag dar gtor ba bzhin 'jig par 'gyur ro//
222b1: dngos grub thams cad thob par 'gyur/ don thams cad rjes su 'jug par 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / gang dkyil 'khor gyi lha gzhan yang dgyes par 'gyur la/ 'phags pa spyan ram
222b2: gzigs dbang phyug rtag tu mchog sbyin par mdzad do/ / gsang sngags oM zhes bya ba dran nas tshe 'phos pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can du 'gro bar 'gyur ro// gsang sngags yi ge gcig pa'o// oM b+hA
222b3: yi ge gnyis pa 'bum zlas brjod byas nas gnyis pa'i yon tan thob par 'gyur ro/ / de bzhin gshegs pa snang ba mtha' yas kyi spyan snga na 'dug par 'gyur zhing mchog thams cad rjes su sbyin par mdzad do// /
222b4: sdig pa thams cad kyang rnam par dag par mdzad/ sngon gyi las ngan gyi nad kyang sos par 'gyur/ nor gyi dbang phyug nor bu bzang po'i bu dbang du 'gyur zhing nye bar gnas par 'gyur ro// mig gang gis kyang phyir
222b5: zhing bar chad byed rus par mi 'gyur/ tshe 'phos nas kyang ri gru 'dzin du skye bar 'gyur/ don yod zhags pa'i dngos grub kyang thob par 'gyur ro// yi ge gnyis pa'o// oM pad me/ gsang sngags yi ge gsum pa
222b6: 'bum bzlas brjod byas nas gsum pa la yang dag par 'jug par 'gyur/ pad ma yangs pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi phyag rgya dang / gsang sngags gang yin pa thams cad la zhugs par 'gyur/ 'phags pa spyan ras
222b7: gzigs dbang phyug gzhon nu'i cha byad can mdun na bzhugs par 'gyur ro/ / 'dod pa thams cad kyi mchog rjes su sbyin par mdzad do// don yod zhags pa'i pad ma gtsug gtor gyi dkyil 'khar ston par
222b8: mdzad/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor rnams ston par mdzad/ thams cad du dngos grub rjes su sbyin par mdzad do// yi ge gsum pa'o// oM pad ma gri/ gsang sngags yi ge dzan
223a1: pa 'bum bzlas brjod byas nas bzhi pa la 'jug par 'gyur ro/ / 'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa mi 'khrugs pa sku mdog gser gyi kha dog can mdun na bzhugs shing dpung pa brkyang nas
223a2: phyag spyi bor 'jog par mdzad la/ rigs sngags 'chang ba legs so zhes bya ba rjes su sbyin par mdzad de/ rigs sngags 'chang tshur shog khyod kyi sdig pa dang sgrib pa thams cad yongs su dag
223a3: ste/ rang gi ngo bo thams cad shin tu dri ma med par yongs su dag go// mi'i 'jig rten 'di nas tshe 'phos nas nga'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'ong zhing tshe rabs dran par 'gyur ro// phyir zhing rnams
223a4: kyang mngal na gnas pas gos par mi 'gyur/ 'jig rten pa'i dgos pa thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// sa bzhi pa'o// oM pad ma b+hu dza~M/ gsang sngags yi ge lnga pa 'bum bzlas brjod byas na
223a5: sa lnga pa la gnas par 'gyur ro/ / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas pad ma'i bla ma rab tu ston par mdzad do// sgrib pa thams cad yongs su zad par
223a6: 'gyur ro/ / rigs sngags 'chang la legs so zhes bya ba'i sgra byin par 'gyur te/ rigs sngags 'chang ba legs so legs so// khyod la bsod nams kyi phung po chen po skyes te/ rigs sngags 'char khyod dge ba'i
223a7: rtsa ba chen po skyed pas rigs sngags 'chang khyed tshe 'phos nas de bzhin gshegs pa bye ba khrag khrig dgu bcu cu gnyis kyi drung du dge ba'i rtsab mtshungs pa med par skyed par 'gyur 'ang / nga'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du skye bar 'gyur//
223a8: khyod kyis don yod zhags pa'i pad ma'i gtsug tor gyi snying po dang / bsad pa'i dkyil 'khor dang / phyag rgya chen po'i rim par bye ba 'grub cing rigs sngags 'chang khyod sdig pa dang sgrib pa thams cad spangs kyis bya ba thams
223b1: cad gyes shig/ yid la bya ba'i bsgrub pa thams cad ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du de dag thams cad shin tu grub par 'gyur ro// sa lnga pa'o// oM pad ma lo ki te/ gzungs sngags drug pa 'bum bzlas brjod byas nas drug pa 'thob
223b2: ste 'jug par 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad snang bar mdzad par 'gyur/ stod gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul phra mo snyed kyis de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
223b3: sangs rgyas rnams gzigs shing mngon sum du ston par mdzad/ dbugs 'byin par mdzad do// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas pad ma gzigs pa'i rgyal mtshan nges
223b4: rigs sngags 'chang de la yang dag par dbugs 'byin par mdzad de/ rigs sngags 'char khyod nga'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas byang chub snying po'i mthar thug gi bar du tshur shog/ las byas pa shin tu yongs su zar
223b5: cing / khyod kyis sems can dmyal ba'i sgo rnams ni bcad/ khyod kyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi sgo rnams ni phye/ khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sa bon dang rigs spyi ni khong du chud/ khyod kyis don yod
223b6: pa'i zhags pa'i pad ma'i gtsug tor gyi snying po dang / gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor ni grub/ khyod kyis thams cad du gnas kyi sgo rnams ni bye bas/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i las sgrub pa rnams ji ltar yid la
223b7: byas pa bzhin las thams cad byos shig/ oM pad ma dz+wa la hUM drug/ yi ge bdun pa 'bum bzlas brjod byas ma thag tu ting nge 'dzin par ma dri ma med pa sgrib pa dang bral ba dag pa zhes bya ba thob par 'gyur la/ ting nge 'dzin
223b8: gad thob pas lus shin tu 'bar bar 'gyur zhing / 'od zer khri dge sna tshogs su 'gyur/ sa bdun pa la gnas par 'gyur/ lus kyi snang ba gang gis stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sangs rgyas
224a1: kyi zhing thams cad kyi gnas rnams sdang bar byed cing / gang dang gang du 'od zer rin po che 'bar ba rnam pa sna tshogs pa dgabab pa las me tog gi char sna tshogs pa rnams 'byung bar 'gyur la/ de bzhin gshegs pa

224a4: mchog yin no/ / 'di ni 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang phyug gi snying po gsang ba ces pa'i dkyil 'khor don yod zhags pa pad ma gtsug tor gyi snying po yang dag pa'o// rigs sngags 'chang khyod kyis

224b8: Sh+T+r-i/ Sha bi ma le hU~M phaT/ gsang sngags yi ge bcu pa 'bum bzlas brjod byas na phyir mi ldog par gyur nas sa bcu la gnas par 'gyur zhing / lha dang mi'i skye dgu dag 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'o// zhes

225a2: kho na nyid kyis dngos grub bla na med pa 'di ni don yod zhags pa'i snying po rnam par sprul pa bzlas brjod tsam gyis 'grub pa yin te/ bdag gis sngar bstan pa thams cad la lhag par zhen pa gtsang ma/ gtsang sbra spyod pa/ gos

225a7: rim tA pA ri pA ra ya hUM/ da ra da ra/ bi ba d+hA ra/ be tsiH/ sarbas b+hUmA pa b+ho ga/ sarba ta thA ga ta/ ma hAdAn pA da me g+ha pra bar+t+ta ya/ ta ra ta ra ta ra ya ma hA pad ma maNi hU~M phaT swA hA/ 'di ni don yod zhags pa'i sbyin pa'i
225a8: rol tu phyin pa'i snying po chen po ste/ gang gis yungs 'bru tsam gyi sbyin pa yang byin te/ dran pa tsam gyis la ni bdun bzlas brjod byas na mchod sbyin chen po rnam par 'phrul po chen po shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i sbyin pa'i
225b1: pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro/ / dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po snying rje chen po dang ldan pa 'phags pa spyan ras
225b2: gzigs dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo/ / oM a mo gA shi la/ saM b+ha ra saM b+ha ra/ b+ha ra b+ha ra/ ma hA shad d+ha satwa pad ma b+hi b+ha shi ta b+hu dza/ d+ha ra d+ha ra sa man ta a ba lo ki ti hUM phaT swA hA// gzangs 'di ga so song gi yan lag
225b3: brkyang bzung nas bsrung bar gnas pa byas te mi smra bar lan nyi shu rtsa gcig tu dran par brjod par bya'o/ / de nas don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po bzlas brjod bya'o bzlas brjod byas pa tsam gyis mo la tshul khrims
225b4: dag pa chen po dang ldan par 'gyur ro/ / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// tshul khrims kyi dri zhim po mang po lus la byung zhing / phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten du grags par 'gyur ro// /
225b5: gang zhig nyi ma re re zhing gzangs 'di dran par byed na de ni rtag tu tshul khrims yongs su dag par 'gyur ro// dge slong gang la la zhig tshul khrims zhig cing nyams par gyur pas bsnyung bar gnas pa byas te/
225b6: gzungs 'di bzlas brjod byas pa tsam gyis mod la tshul khrims yongs su dag par 'gyur zhing / tshul khrims mang po dang ldan par 'gyur ro// dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag 'tshal
225b7: lo/ / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po snying rje chen po dang ldan pa 'phags pa spyan ngas gzigs dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo// oM a mo gAk+ShAn ta sarba bo d+hi sarba Nak+Sha Na ma hA sa twa mA dra na/ sarbas

226a1: kyis mnyam par gnas pa dang / byol song gi skye gnas su gtogs pa'i ri dgas dang / bya dang / ltos 'gro la sogs pa gang dag 'das pa gang yin pa dang / gnas pa gang yin pa dang / skye bar 'gyur ba gang //

226b1: thAg tA ma hA a ma gA ku ru Na d+ha na/ sa mA d+hi/ sarba bi mo k+Sha/ a pra ka bya ka/ tsu ru tsu ru hUM phaT swA hA// gzungs 'di 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi drung du yid la byed pas rtse gcig du dran par byas na dran

246a8: dbyings 'khrugs par mi byed na/ de phyir gzungs ni thob par 'gyur// mdo sde 'di ni mnyan par bya/ 'di la gzungs ni zad pa med/ ye shes 'byor 'di 'di lta ste/ des na byang chub thob par 'gyur// byang chub sems
246b1: dpa' 'jigs med pa/ / gzungs 'di rab tu bzung byas na// phyogs bcu dag gi sangs rgyas kyi// chos bstan pa ni thos par 'gyur// don dang tshig 'bras bskyod kun gyi// / mchog gi chos ni rnam par shes// nyi
246b2: ma'i 'od zer ji snyed pa/ / de snyed tshig rnams shes par 'gyur// gang dag chos kyi mchog 'gyur ba// rlabs chen gzungs kyi sgo rnams te/ gang zhig mdo 'di 'dzin de la/ thams cad rtag tu mngon du 'gyur/ gal te sems
246b3: can thams cad kyis/ / de la bskal par dogs dris te/ the tshom thams cad chad gyur kyang // de yi ye shes mi zad do// mdo sde 'di la su dga' ba/ de ni chos kyi rgyal po'i sras/ byang chub mchog la nye ba ste/
246b4: yid brtan gyur dang chos 'dzin pa'o// gzungs 'dri 'dzin par su byed pa// de la sems can thams cad dag/ sangs rgyas rnams kyang de la dgyes/ grags pa 'jig rten 'byung bar 'gyur/ su zhig med sde
246b5: 'dzin pa/ de ni 'chi ba'i dus byed che// sangs rgyas bye ba brgyad bcu mthong // lag pa de la nye bar 'dzeg/ gzungs 'di 'dzin par byed pa ni/ bskal pa bye ba stod rnams su/ sngon chad sdig pa gang byas pa/ zla ba
246b6: gcig gis byed par 'gyur/ / byang chub sems dpa'i bsod nams gang bskal pa bye bar bsgrubs pa kur// gzungs 'di 'dzin par byed pa yis/ zla ba gcig gi zil gnon 'gyur// khams gsum sem
246b7: cad ji snyed pa/ gal te thams cad bdud gyur kyang / mdo sde 'di ni gang 'dzin pa// de la bar chad byed mi rus// byang chub 'tshang rgya bar du de// dran dang blo gros rtogs ldan 'gyur// gzungs kyi dam pa gang yin pa/
246b8: de yis lce yi rtse mor gnas// ji ltar mdo sde bstan 'dil/ gzungs ni so sor des pa bzhin// 'di las thams cad mkhyen pa bstan// 'di las byang chub thob par 'gyur// gzungs 'di bshad ma thag tu
247a1: yang / mar me zhes byas nga lung bstan// skad cig de la sangs rgyas ni// gang gA'i klung gi bye snyed mthong // gang zhig sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// bstan pa 'di ni rtogs 'dod cing // mdo sde 'di
247a2: la brten pa des/ / thams cad myur du thob par 'gyur// sangs rgyas zhing ni rnam dag dang / nyan thos phun sum tshogs pa dang / 'od dang mtshan kyang rnam dag pa// mdo sde 'dis ni byed par 'gyur// de bas
247a3: bag na yod gyur la/ / zhag bdun par du 'di sems pa/ sangs rgyas bye ba brgyad bcu yis/ de yi 'og tu gzungs sbyin 'gyur// bsam bya sems par mi bsam ste/ bsam bya min yang mi bsam mo/
247a4: sems shig 'gal bar ma sems shig/ de yi 'og du gzungs thob 'gyur// dper na rgya mtshor phyin pa'i maM// nor la som nyi med pa ltar// de bzhin gzungs 'di thob gyur nas// nga ba la yang so mnyar med/
247a5: 'di las rdzogs pa'i byang chub nye/ de bas 'di la sbyor bar bgyis// zhi ba'i gnas ni thob gyur nas/ rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob par 'gyur// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis yang tshe dang ldan
247a6: ba shA ri'i bu la bka' stsal pa/ shA ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ches bzhi dang ldan na/ gzungs 'di thob par 'gyur ro// bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ 'dod pa rnams la lhag par chags
247a7: ba med pa yin/ sems can thams cad la phrag dag med pa yin/ bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong zhing 'gyod pa med par sbyin pa'i tshul can yin/ nyin mtshan du chos 'dod cing ches kyi kun dga'
247a8: ga ma yin nyon mtshan du chos la dga' zhing chos 'dod pa yin te/ shA ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos bzhi po de dag dang ldan na gzungs 'di thob par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das
247b1: kyis de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag bka' stsal to/ / ngan cing bdud kyi spyod yul pa// 'dod pa dring spang bar byos// de dag sems can dmyal ba'i rkyen// ngan song rnams kyi rgyu yang yin// shes kyi khe dang snyed
247b2: khang grags pa'i phyir/ / pha rol dag la phrag dog mi bya'i ste/ dga' ba'i mig gis sems can bltas byas na/ mthu che ba dang gzugs kyang mdzes par 'gyur/ sems can gang dag kha cig rtsod 'gyur ba
247b3: depo gzhi rtsa yongs su 'dzin pa ste/ de ltar gang la srid par 'gyur ba spangs/ sred pa spang ba byas na gzungs su 'gyur/ gal te byang chub 'dod na gzhan ma sems/ nyin dang mtshan du chos ni btsal
247b4: bar byos/ / chos cig 'di 'dra 'di dag sten byed na/ de la gzugs ni mngon du 'gyur bar 'ong // sha ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos bzhi dang ldan na gzungs 'di thob
247b5: par 'gyur ro/ / bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dgon pa dang / dben pa la gnas pa dang / chos zab mo la bzod pa'i stobs skyed pa nyid dang / rnyed pa dang / kung sti dang / tshigs su bcad pa dag la lhag par chags
247b6: ba med pa dang / / sdug pa'i dngos po thams cad la mi lta zhing / tha na lus dang srog kyang yongs su gtong ba ste/ sha ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos bzhi po de dag dang ldan na/
247b7: gzungs 'di thob par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag bka' stsal to// rgyala~M bas sngags pa'i dgon par gnas par bgyis// de la gnas pas
247b8: gzhan la brnyas mi bya/ / zab mo'i bzod la 'dun pa bskyed nas su/ bag yod mgo la 'bar bzhin gnas par bgyis/ 'di ltar tshul 'chos byed kyi gzhir gyur pa/ shis khe rnyed pa rnams
248a1: la gnas ma byed/ bya dang 'dra bar ngan don dag gis mchog byas te/ mi 'gyur ba yi 'bras bu yod par byos// kye ma sangs rgyas bstan pa legs par rnyed/ sdug bsngal mang po'i rtsa ba khyim yang
248a2: spongs/ / lus dang ngag dang yid kyang yongs dag pas/ sangs rgyas dang ni chos la gus par gyis/ rnyed 'dod dran pa ma yin shes rab min// dad dang tshul khrims ma yin chos sems min// de na byang chub ring ste
248a3: gnam sa bzhin/ / de ltar rnyed pa yongs su spang bar bya// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos bzhi dang ldan na gzungs 'di thob par 'gyur ro// gzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/
248a4: yi ge 'bru brgyad kyi don khong du chud par bya'o// brgyad po de dag gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ pa zhes bya ba don dam par chos thams cad la bdag med pa la 'jug pa khong du chud pa dang / la zhes bya ba mtshan dang dpe byad
248a5: bzang po med par de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sku la 'jug pa khong du chud pa dang / ba zhes bya ba byis pa'i chos rnams dang mkhas pa'i chos rnams ji lta ba bzhin du gnyis su med pa la 'jug pa khong du chud
248a6: pa dang / dza zhes bya ba skye ba dang / rga ba dang / 'chi ba dang / skye ba dang / rga ba dang / 'chi ba med pa'i 'gro ba mi skye mi 'gag pa la 'jug pa khong du chud pa dang / ka zhes bya ba las dang rnam par smin pa dang / las dang rnam par smin
248a7: bsde pa la 'jug pa khong du chud pa dang / d+ha zhes bya ba gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs kyi stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa dag chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa khong du chud pa dang / sha zhes bya ba zhi gnas/
248a8: dang lhag mthong dang / ni gnas dang lhag mthong med par chos thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid pa 'jug pa khong du chud pa dang / k+Sha zhes bya ba chos thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid la 'jug pa khong du chud pa ste/ gzod ma nas ni ba'i phyir zad
248b1: pa med pa dang / 'jig pa med pa dang / rgyu ba med pa dang / chos thams cad mya ngan las 'das par 'jug pa khong du chud pa ste/ de ltar yi ge 'bru brgyad po de dag gi don khong du chud par rtogs par bya ba 'di ni don khong du chud pa
248b2: dang po'o/ / gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di legs par bris te bzung bar bya ba 'di ni don khong du chud pa gnyis pa'o// zla ba phyed phyed cing gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di rtag tu klog pa dang / rjes su dran par
248b3: bya ba'i phyir brtson par bya ba 'di ni don khong du chud pa gsum pa'o/ / gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la mngon par brtson pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos sems can thams cad yang dag par
248b4: dga' bar bya ba dang / yang dag par 'dzin du gzhug pa dang / yang dag par gzed stong pa la gzung ba'i phyir brtson par bya ba 'di ni don khong du chud pa bzhi pa ste/ shA ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
248b5: chen po chos bzhi po de dag dang ldan na/ gzungs 'di ni thob par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag bka' stsal to// yi ge 'bru brgyad 'di dag bsam par bya// mdo sde 'di ni
248b6: bris nas bcang bar bya/ / zla ba phyed cing rtag tu klag par bya// sems can rnams kyang 'di 'dzin gzhug par bya/ byang chub nye dang shes rab rgya yang che// phyogs bcu rnams na sangs rgyas gang su dag/ bzhugs pa
248b7: thams cad des ni mdun du mthong / / de phyir 'dun pa skyed de 'di la bslab/ shA ri'i bu bzhi po 'di dag ni gzungs 'di la mngon par brtson pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i phan yon yin te/ bzhi
248b8: gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad de la dgongs pa dang / de la bdud kyi las kyi mi 'byung ba dang / de'i las kyi sgrib pa myur du 'byang ba dang / spobs pa rgyun mi chad par myung
248b9: du thob pa ste/ shA ri'i bu bzhi po de dag ni gzungs 'di la mngon par brtson pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i phan yon yin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag
249a1: bka' stsal to/ / sangs rgyas kun gyis de ni yid la mdzad// de la bdud kyis glags ni rnyed mi 'gyur// de yi las kyi bsgrib pa myur du 'byung / spobs pa mtha' yas rnams kyang thob par 'gyur/
249a2: shA ri'i bu sngon byung ba 'das pa'i dus na bskal pa grangs med pa'i yang ches grangs med pa/ yangs pa rgya cher gyur pa/ chad med pa de'i tshe de'i dus na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa
249a3: sangs rgyas rin chen dpal gyis gzi brjid rgyal po lta bu zhes bya ba/ rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ bla na med pa lha
249a4: dang mi rnams kyi ston pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'jig rten du byung ste/ shA ri'i bu bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rin chen dpal gyi
249a5: gzi brjid rgyal po lta bu de yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'i dus kyi tshe'i khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po snang ba 'dzin ces bya ba mi'i dbang po rin po che sna bdun dang ldan pa zhig byung ngo / / de'i bu yon tan rin po
249a6: bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dpal zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ de skyes nas lo bcu drug/ lon pa dang / des sgo mtha' yas pas sgrub pa'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshes
249a7: pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rin chen dpal gyi rgyal po lta bu de las thos te/ des gzungs 'di thos ma thag tu thob par bya ba'i phyir rtson par gyur to// de lo bdun khrir rmugs
249a8: pa dang / gnyid kyis ma sten to// nor par ma gyur to// de lan 'ga' yang rgyal srid la dga' ba'am/ nor la dga' ba'am/ bdag la dga' bar ma gyur to// de lo bdun khrid lan dga' yang sa la glos
249b1: ma pab ste/ gcig tu nges par nang du yang dag 'jog la gnas so// sangs rgyas bye ba phrag dgu bcu las chos snyan pa thos te/ thos nas kyang nyams su blangs so// thams cad bzung ngo // gzung nyams
249b2: su blangs nas kyang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rin chen dpal gyi gzi brjid kyi rgyal po lta bu de nyid las rab tu byung ngo / / da rab tu byung
249b3: nas de lo dgu khri 'das pa dang des sgo mtha' yas pas sgrub pa'i gzungs 'di bsgrubs te/ bsgrubs nas kyang sems can rnams la rgya cher yang dag par gshad do// des tshe gcig po de nyid la
249b4: sems can bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag brgyad bcu bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub yang dag par 'dzin du btsud cing / phyir mi ldog pa'i sa la bkod par gyur to// shA ri'i bu 'khor de na
249b5: tshong dpon gyi bu zla ba'i tog ces bya ba zhig yod do/ / des sgo mtha' yas las snang nas kyi rmo rgyurnam tham mo// smra ba'i dge slong de las thos so// thos nas kyang rjes su yid rang bar gyur to// de rjes
249b6: su yi rang ba'i mod las skyes pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba des sangs rgyas bye ba phrag dgu bcu las chos bstan pa thos so/ / thos nas kyang nyams su blangs so// thams cad bzung ngo // thams cad du yang
249b7: gzungs thob pa rnams kyi mchog dang / tshig btsun pa gzung ba'i tshig dang ldan pa rnams kyi mchog dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i spobs pa rgyun mi chod pa rnams kyi mchog
249b8: tu gyur to/ / des bskal pa gsum du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag mnyes par byas so// mnyes par byas nas bskal pa gsum 'das pa dang /
250a1: bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// shA ri'i bya de'i tshe de'i dus na tshong dpon gyi bu zla ba'i tog ces bya bar gyur pa de gzhan zhig yin
250a2: bsnyam du khyod som nyid 'am yid gnyis sam/ the tsam za bar gyur na/ shA ri'i bu khyod kyis de ltar mi lta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
250a3: rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mA ra me mdzad de'i tshe de'i dus na tshong dpon gyi bu zla ba'i tog ces bya bar gyur to/ / shA ri'i bu de'i tshe de'i dus na yon tan rin po che bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dpal zhes bya ba chos
250a4: smra bar gyur pa de gzhan zhig yin pa snyam du khyod som nyi dang / yid gnyis sam/ the tshom za bar gyur na/ shA ri'i bu khyod kyis de ltar mi blta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs

250b1: dpa' chen po myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas tha na gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la rjes su yi rang bar yang brtson par bya'o/ / de ci'i

250b4: nams kyi phung po de'i tshad ni de bzhin gshegs pa ma gtogs par sems can thams cad kyis kyang shes pa 'am/ bsam par mi nus so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe tshigs

250b6: deni che rabs kun tu rgyal ba mthong / / de dag la yang dad pa bsam yas snyed// mdo sde zab mo'i tshul yang shes par 'gyur// de ni myur du byang chub mchog 'tshang rgya// bla med byang chub ma reg bar du yang // de ni ting nge 'di

251a1: pa bzang dang bcas yi rang / byang chub myur du reg par su 'dod dang / bdud rnams myur du gzhom par su 'dod dang / bsod nams brgya'i mtshan bzangs su 'dod pa/ 'di la brtson na snyed par dka' mi 'gyur// ga
251a2: gA'i klung gi bye snyed 'jig rten khams/ / gang gis rin chen bkang ste srin byin yang / bris dang bzung ba'i bsod nams gang yin pa// de la sbyin pas dper yang mi 'gyur ro// de ltar thos nas rtse gcig bag yod/

251a8: chen po 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha rnams kyis nang du skyes pa'i brgyad po 'di dag kyang de la sems par gyur te/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par snang byed ces bya ba dang / snang byed dang /
251b1: shes rab 'od dang / nyi ma'i 'od dang / yang dag skul byed dang / bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs byad dang / skar ma'i rgyal po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyod pa'i blo gros zhes bya ba ste/ byang chub
251b2: sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po brgyad po de dag des gzungs thob par bya ba'i phyir mngon par brtson par 'gyur ro/ / gzungs 'di la brtson pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos kyang bden pa'i dam
251b3: bca' bar bya'o/ / byas pa gzo ba dang / byas pa tshor ba can dang / chos 'dod pa dang / chos la dga' ba dang / zab mo'i chos la bzod pa mngon par brtson par bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' chen po gzungs la brtson pas/
251b4: kun 'ged pa bgo' bsha' byed pa'i ngang tshul can du bya ste/ des ji ltar chung ba dang / ji ltar nyung ba las kyang sbyin pa sbyin par byas na mang po las lta smos kyang ci dgos/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam gra/

277a2: bar 'gyur ro/ / ltas ngan pa thams cad kyang mi sdig go/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi snying po'i gzungs rdzogs s+ho// // dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// sbyin pa'i snying po 'di lan cig/
277a3: zos pas sbyin pa thob par 'gyur ro// oM na ma ste b+hA gA ba tI dA nA d+hi ba te swA hA// tshul khrims kyi snying po 'di lan cig thos pas tshul khrims thob par 'gyur ro// na maHsarba ta ga thA ga tA nAd/ ma hA
277a4: ka n+taM/ / ma kA naM/ na mo b+ha ga ba t+yaM/ shI la pa ri pur+Ne shi ri ye shI la mai/ sA d+ha ya sA d+ha ya/ kin tiSh+Tha saM bud d+ho// b+ha ga ban d+harma s+ya/ sam dz+nyA na pA ya ti swA hA/ bzod pa'i snying po 'di lan cig thos pa/
277a5: bzod pa thob par 'gyur ro// na maHsarba ta thA ga tA ya/ a tsin t+ya go tsa rA ya/ na mo k+ShAn ha ye be tu b+hiHta thA ga tA na bu ta ko Ti b+hi ba ri ba ra ti ta ye ye rak+ShaM ku ru tu ru tu ru sa ma ya ma nu sma ra/ shAkya
277a6: mra ni sarba ta thA ga tA ma pA ra mi tA dz+nyA na go tsa ra dz+nyAn pa ya ti swA hA/ brtson 'grus kyi snying po 'di lan cig zos pas brtson 'grus thob par 'gyur ro// na maHsarba ta thA gat+tanAM/ ma tsin d+ha bi sha
277a7: rA/ / na mo sU te b+ha ga ba te bAr+ya pA ro mai ta bIr+ya na ku ru bIr+ye bI r+ye/ ma hA bir+ya ta thA ga tA/ sarba dz+nyA na pA ya ti swA hA/ bsam gtan gyi snying po 'di lan cig thos pas bsam gtan thob par 'gyur
277a8: ro/ / na maHsarba ta thA ga tA nA~M/ oM b+hi ma le/ ni ra ma le/ d+hu ne d+hA ne/ d+hA na pri ye/ hUM phaT/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po 'di lan cig thos pas shes rab thob par 'gyur ro// na maHta thA ga tA ya/ a bar
277b1: me ng+ga go tsa rA ya/ na mo D+haka pa// dA pA rA ma tA yA/ dAn ma thu ru ku ru ba g+h+nA ni ta thA gA tAs+ya/ sa ma ya ma na smar/ !u0f7fte/ dAd+had+haR+than+tad+hA pas// pha rol tu phyin pa drug bzung bar 'gyur ba'i kA
277b2: rdzogs s+ho/ / // pha rol tu phyin pa bcu'i snying po 'di la ni cig zos pas pha rol tu phyin pa bcu thob par 'gyur ro// nam sarba ta nA~M/ tai thA gau tA nA~M/ da sha pA ra mi tA pa ri pU ra kA nA ma hI/ pha rol tu phyin pa bcu
277b3: thob par 'gyur ba'i gzungs rdzogs s+ho/ / // 'di lan cig brjod pas byams pa thob par 'gyur ro// na maHsarba ta thA ga tA nAM/ tsu ru tsu ru/ mu ru mA ru/ ku ru kA N+De/ kA ru tsi tsi ta mud pA pa ya/ b+ha ga pa
277b4: sarba b+ha yaM me nA sha ya swA hA/ 'di lan gcig brjod pas snying rje thob par 'gyur ro// na maHsarba ta thA ga tA nAM/ na mo b+ha ga ba ti sarba satra bi ye hUM mu di te swA hA/ 'di lan cig brjod pas dga' ba thob par
277b5: 'gyur ro/ / na maHsarba tAthA ga tA nAM/ ma tsin t+ya bi ga nA ma/ oM tu ru tA ru traM/ tu lu hu lu/ mu lu mu lu/ swA tAM// 'di lan cig brjod pas btang snyoms thob par 'gyur ro// na maHsarba ta thA ga tA hri yA
277b6: A ru ga te/ oM ku ru gi ni swA hA/ tshad med pa bzhi thob par 'gyur ba'i gzungs rdzogs s+ho// // bcom ldan 'das ma lags ma shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la phyag 'tshal lo// tad+ya thAHoM mu ni d+harma/ sam
277b7: sar+b+ba A na mata/ zag pa bti / sarbaka tu ba rnaH// sam hA pa tan d+ham// oM sa a.AH/
277b8: 'di bzung bas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa bzung bar 'gyur ro// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya bzung bar 'gyur ba'i gzungs rdzogs s+ho//
278a1: dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// oMn+ti/ na maHsarba bud d+hA nAM/ oM mAM/ b+h+rUMHmr-iHtad+ya thA/ oM b+h+rUMH/ 'di bzung bas 'phags pa phal po che bzung bar 'gyur ro// 'dri ba dang / klog pa
278a2: la yang de dang 'dra'o/ / 'phags pa phal po che bzung bar 'gyur ba'i gzungs rdzogs s+ho// / dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// na maHsa ma~M ta bud d+hA nAM/ a pra
278a3: ti ha ta shA sa nAnAM/ oM kaNi kaH/ ta thA ga ta ud b+ha bag+h+nAnaH/ bairata/ ud tam ud tam/ ta thA ga tA ud b+ha ba hU~M phaT+Ta swA hA// 'di bzung bas 'phags pa sdong po // pa'i mdo thams cad
278a4: rdzogs par klags shing kha don tu byas par 'gyur ro/ / 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor dang dam tshig shes par 'gyur ro// phyag rgya rnams kyang
278a5: shes par 'gyur ro/ / 'phags pa sdong po bkod pa'i snying po rdzogs s+ho// / dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// na maHsa man ta bud d+ha nAM/ a praH
278a6: haHshA sa nA nAM/ oM nun d+ha na hUM hUM phaT phaTe swA hA// 'di bzung bas 'phags pa ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po'i mang bzung bar 'gyur ro// 'phags pa ting nge 'dzin gyis rgyal po'i mdo brdung bar 'gyur
278a7: ba'i gzungs rdzogs s+ho/ / // dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas kun nas thogs pa med par ston pa la phyag 'tshal lo// oM bi shu ne swA hA/ 'di bzung na 'phags pa
278b1: mabya chen mo bzung bar 'gyur ro/ / 'phags pa ma bya chen ma ra snang ba rdzogs s+ho// // dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// namaHsa man ta da d+hAH/ a pra ta ta ta shA sa nAn+te/ a ma?/
278b2: ribadz+ra na ma hA pra ti sa re/ dz+dza hU~M phaT phaT swA hA/ 'di bzung bas 'phags ma rig pa'i rgyal mo so sor 'brang ma chen mo bzung bar 'gyur ro// 'phags ma so sor 'bring ma chen mo bzung bar 'gyur ba
278b3: gzungs rdzogs s+ho/ / // 'phags pa lang dkar gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal lo// blo gros chen po sngags kyi tshig 'di dag bshad par bya'o// tad+ya thA/ oM pad+ma me pad me de bi/ hi ne hi ne hi na/ tsAru
278b4: lA/ hu le hu le hu le/ yu le yu le yu le/ ba le ba le pa le/ mr-i tse tshan de/ b+hin d+he b+han dz+re/ man d+he pra ma d+he/ de na ka re swA hA// blo gros chen po rigs kyi bu'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang la la sngags kyi tshig
278b5: 'di dag 'dzin pa dang / 'chang ba dang / klog pa dang / kun chub par byed na// lha 'am/ lha mo 'am/ klu'am/ klu mo'am/ gnod sbyin nam/ gnod sbyin mo 'am/ lha ma yin na/

279a2: kyis/ glags mi rnyed do// gsang sngags kyi chog 'di dag klog par byed pa des la dkar gshegs pa'i mdo thams cad klags par 'gyur ro// gsang sngags kyi chog 'di dgan
279a3: bcom ldan 'das kyis srin po la sogs pa rnams bzlog pa'i phyir gsungs so/ / 'phags pa la dkar gshegs pa'i mdo// thams cad klags par 'gyur ba'i gzungs
279a4: sngags rdzogs s+ho/ / / pa d+hanA tra rba ma b+ha' te na te na ta thA ga to u0f7fba data/ tsu ma nir d+ha a tha 'a drim ma!/ dko'o/ legs sa//
